  121 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick upper;

  126 |     |     struct RangePoolLocals {

  131 |     | 
  132 |     |     modifier tickPreconditions(int24 lower, int24 upper) {
  133 | *r  |         require(lower < upper);
  134 | *r  |         require(upper < 887272);
  135 | *r  |         require(lower > -887272);
  136 | *r  |         require(lower % tickSpacing == 0);
  137 | *r  |         require(upper % tickSpacing == 0);
  138 |     |         _;
  139 |     |     }
  140 |     | 
  141 |     |     constructor() {
  142 |     |         manager = new LimitPoolManager();
  143 |     |         factory = new LimitPoolFactory(address(manager));
  144 |     |         poolImpl = address(new LimitPool(address(factory)));
  145 |     |         tokenImpl = address(new PositionERC1155(address(factory)));
  146 |     |         
  147 |     |         manager.enableImplementation(bytes32(uint256(0x1)), address(poolImpl), address(tokenImpl));
  148 |     |         tickSpacing = 10;
  149 |     |         tokenIn = new Token20("IN", "IN", 18);
  150 |     |         tokenOut = new Token20("OUT", "OUT", 18);
  151 |     | 
  152 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolParams memory params;
  153 |     |         params.poolType = bytes32(uint256(0x1));
  154 |     |         params.tokenIn = address(tokenIn);
  155 |     |         params.tokenOut = address(tokenOut);
  156 |     |         params.swapFee = 500;
  157 |     |         params.startPrice = 79228162514264337593543950336;
  158 |     |         (address poolAddr, address tokenAddr) = factory.createLimitPool(params);
  159 |     |         pool = LimitPool(poolAddr);
  160 |     |         token = PositionERC1155(tokenAddr);
  161 |     |     }

  165 | *   |     function mintLimit(uint128 amount, bool zeroForOne, int24 lower, int24 upper) public tickPreconditions(lower, upper) {
  166 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  167 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
  168 | *   |         amount = amount + 1;
  169 |     |         // Ensure the newly created position is using different ticks
  170 | *   |         for(uint i = 0; i < limitPositions.length;) {
  171 | *   |             if(limitPositions[i].owner == msg.sender && limitPositions[i].lower == lower && limitPositions[i].upper == upper && limitPositions[i].zeroForOne == zeroForOne) {
  172 | *r  |                 revert("Position already exists");
  173 |     |             }
  174 |     |             unchecked {
  175 | *   |                 ++i;
  176 |     |             }
  177 |     |         }
  178 |     | 
  179 | *   |         LimitPoolValues memory poolValues;
  180 | *   |         LimitPoolLocals memory poolStructs;
  181 | *   |         LiquidityDeltaValues memory values;
  182 |     | 
  183 | *   |         (,poolStructs.pool0, poolStructs.pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore,poolValues.positionIdNextBefore,,) = pool.globalState();
  184 | *   |         poolValues.price0Before = poolStructs.pool0.price;
  185 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity0Before = poolStructs.pool0.liquidity;
  186 | *   |         poolValues.price1Before = poolStructs.pool1.price;
  187 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity1Before = poolStructs.pool1.liquidity;
  188 |     | 
  189 | *   |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params;
  190 | *   |         params.to = msg.sender;
  191 | *   |         params.amount = amount;
  192 | *   |         params.mintPercent = 0;
  193 | *   |         params.lower = lower;
  194 | *   |         params.upper = upper;
  195 | *   |         params.zeroForOne = zeroForOne;
  196 |     | 
  197 |     |         // Get the ticks the position will be minted with rather than what was passed directly by fuzzer
  198 |     |         // This is so the we can properly compare before and after mint states of particular ticks.
  199 | *   |         bool posCreated;
  200 | *   |         (lower, upper, posCreated) = pool.getResizedTicksForMint(params);
  201 | *   |         emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
  202 | *   |         emit PositionCreated(posCreated);
  203 |     | 
  204 | *   |         (, poolStructs.lower) = pool.ticks(lower);
  205 | *   |         (, poolStructs.upper) = pool.ticks(upper);
  206 |     | 
  207 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
  208 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
  209 |     | 
  210 |     |         // ACTION 
  211 | *r  |         pool.mintLimit(params);
  212 | *   |         if (posCreated) limitPositions.push(LimitPosition(msg.sender, poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, lower, upper, zeroForOne));
  213 |     | 
  214 | *   |         (, poolStructs.lower) = pool.ticks(lower);
  215 | *   |         (, poolStructs.upper) = pool.ticks(upper);
  216 |     | 
  217 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
  218 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
  219 |     | 
  220 | *   |         values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityDelta;
  221 | *   |         values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityDelta;
  222 |     | 
  223 | *   |         (, poolStructs.pool0, poolStructs.pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,poolValues.positionIdNextAfter,,) = pool.globalState();
  224 | *   |         poolValues.price0After = poolStructs.pool0.price;
  225 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity0After = poolStructs.pool0.liquidity;
  226 | *   |         poolValues.price1After = poolStructs.pool1.price;
  227 | *   |         poolValues.liquidity1After = poolStructs.pool1.liquidity;
  228 | *   |         poolValues.price0 = poolStructs.pool0.price;
  229 | *   |         poolValues.price1 = poolStructs.pool1.price;
  230 |     |         
  231 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
  232 | *   |         emit Prices(poolValues.price0, poolValues.price1);
  233 | *   |         assert(poolValues.price0 >= poolValues.price1);
  234 |     |         // Ensure prices have not crossed
  235 | *   |         emit Prices(poolValues.price0After, poolValues.price1After);
  236 | *   |         assert(poolValues.price0After >= poolValues.price1After);
  237 |     | 
  238 |     |         // Ensure liquidityDelta is always less or equal to liquidityAbsolute
  239 | *   |         emit LiquidityDeltaAndAbsolute(values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
  240 | *   |         assert(int256(values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter) <= int256(uint256(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter)));
  241 | *   |         emit LiquidityDeltaAndAbsolute(values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
  242 | *   |         assert(int256(values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter) <= int256(uint256(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter)));
  243 |     |         
  244 |     |         // Ensure that liquidityAbsolute is incremented when not undercutting
  245 | *   |         if (posCreated) {
  246 |     |             // positionIdNext should have been incremented
  247 | *   |             emit PositionIdNext(poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, poolValues.positionIdNextAfter);
  248 | *   |             assert(poolValues.positionIdNextAfter == poolValues.positionIdNextBefore + 1);
  249 | *   |             if(zeroForOne){
  250 | *   |                 if(poolValues.price0After >= poolValues.price0Before){
  251 | *   |                     emit LiquidityAbsolutePosCreated(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
  252 | *   |                     assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter > poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore);
  253 |     |                 }
  254 |     |             } else {
  255 | *   |                 if(poolValues.price1Before >= poolValues.price1After){
  256 |     |                     emit LiquidityAbsolutePosCreated(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
  257 |     |                     assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter > poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore);
  258 |     |                 }
  259 |     |             }
  260 |     |         } else {
  261 |     |             // positionIdNext should not have been incremented
  262 | *   |             emit PositionIdNext(poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, poolValues.positionIdNextAfter);
  263 | *   |             assert(poolValues.positionIdNextAfter == poolValues.positionIdNextBefore);
  264 | *   |             if(zeroForOne){
  265 | *   |                 if(poolValues.price0After >= poolValues.price0Before){
  266 | *   |                     emit LiquidityAbsoluteNoPosCreated(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
  267 | *   |                     assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter == poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore);
  268 |     |                 }
  269 |     |             } else {
  270 | *   |                 if(poolValues.price1Before >= poolValues.price1After){
  271 | *   |                     emit LiquidityAbsoluteNoPosCreated(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
  272 | *   |                     assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter == poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore);
  273 |     |                 }
  274 |     |             }
  275 |     |         }
  276 |     | 
  277 | *   |         if (posCreated) {
  278 | *   |             emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
  279 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
  280 | *   |             assert(lower < upper);
  281 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
  282 | *   |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
  283 |     |         }
  284 |     |         
  285 | *   |         emit LiquidityGlobal(poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter);
  286 | *   |         emit Liquidity(poolValues.liquidity0Before, poolValues.liquidity1Before, poolValues.liquidity0After, poolValues.liquidity1After);
  287 |     |         
  288 |     |         // Ensure liquidityGlobal is incremented after mint
  289 | *   |         assert(poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter >= poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore);
  290 |     |         
  291 |     |         // Ensure pool liquidity is non-zero after mint with no undercuts
  292 | *   |         if (zeroForOne) {
  293 | *   |             emit PriceChange(poolValues.price0Before, poolValues.price0After);
  294 | *   |             if (poolValues.price0After < poolValues.price0Before) assert(poolValues.liquidity0After > 0);
  295 |     |         }
  296 |     |         else {
  297 | *   |             emit PriceChange(poolValues.price1Before, poolValues.price1After);
  298 | *   |             if (poolValues.price1After > poolValues.price1Before) assert(poolValues.liquidity1After > 0);
  299 |     |         }
  300 |     |     }

  437 | *   |     function swap(uint160 priceLimit, uint128 amount, bool exactIn, bool zeroForOne) public {
  438 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  439 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
  440 |     | 
  441 | *   |         LimitPoolStructs.SwapParams memory params;
  442 | *   |         params.to = msg.sender;
  443 | *   |         params.priceLimit = priceLimit;
  444 | *   |         params.amount = amount;
  445 | *   |         params.exactIn = exactIn;
  446 | *   |         params.zeroForOne = zeroForOne;
  447 | *   |         params.callbackData = abi.encodePacked(address(this));
  448 |     |         
  449 |     |         // ACTION
  450 | *r  |         pool.swap(params);
  451 |     | 
  452 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
  453 | *   |         (,PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool0, PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool1,,,,) = pool.globalState();
  454 | *   |         uint160 price0 = pool0.price;
  455 | *   |         uint160 price1 = pool1.price;
  456 |     |         
  457 |     |         // Ensure prices never cross
  458 | *   |         emit Prices(price0, price1);
  459 | *   |         assert(price0 >= price1);
  460 |     |     }
  461 |     | 
  462 | *   |     function burnLimit(int24 claimAt, uint256 positionIndex, uint128 burnPercent) public {
  463 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  464 | *   |         positionIndex = positionIndex % limitPositions.length;
  465 | *   |         LimitPosition memory pos = limitPositions[positionIndex];
  466 | *r  |         require(claimAt >= pos.lower && claimAt <= pos.upper);
  467 | *r  |         require(claimAt % tickSpacing == 0);
  468 | *   |         LimitPoolValues memory poolValues;
  469 |     | 
  470 | *   |         (,PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool0, PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool1, uint128 liquidityGlobalBefore,,,) = pool.globalState();
  471 |     | 
  472 | *   |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params;
  473 | *   |         params.to = pos.owner;
  474 | *   |         params.burnPercent = burnPercent == 1e38 ? burnPercent : _between(burnPercent, 1e36, 1e38); //1e38;
  475 | *   |         params.positionId = pos.positionId;
  476 | *   |         params.claim = claimAt;
  477 | *   |         params.zeroForOne = pos.zeroForOne;
  478 |     | 
  479 | *   |         (, PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory lowerTick) = pool.ticks(pos.lower);
  480 | *   |         (, PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory upperTick) = pool.ticks(pos.upper);
  481 |     | 
  482 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = lowerTick.liquidityAbsolute;
  483 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = upperTick.liquidityAbsolute;
  484 |     |         
  485 | *   |         emit PositionTicks(pos.lower, pos.upper);
  486 | *   |         (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists) = pool.getResizedTicksForBurn(params);
  487 | *   |         emit BurnTicks(lower, upper, positionExists);
  488 |     | 
  489 |     |         // ACTION
  490 | *r  |         pool.burnLimit(params);
  491 |     |         if (!positionExists) {
  492 |     |             limitPositions[positionIndex] = limitPositions[limitPositions.length - 1];
  493 |     |             delete limitPositions[limitPositions.length - 1];
  494 |     |         }
  495 |     |         else {
  496 |     |             // Update position data in array if not fully burned
  497 |     |             limitPositions[positionIndex] = LimitPosition(pos.owner, pos.positionId, lower, upper, pos.zeroForOne);
  498 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
  499 |     |             assert(lower < upper);
  500 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
  501 |     |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
  502 |     |         }
  503 |     | 
  504 |     |         (, lowerTick) = pool.ticks(lower);
  505 |     |         (, upperTick) = pool.ticks(upper);
  506 |     | 
  507 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter = lowerTick.liquidityAbsolute;
  508 |     |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter = upperTick.liquidityAbsolute;
  509 |     | 
  510 |     |         (,pool0, pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,,,) = pool.globalState();
  511 |     |         uint160 price0 = pool0.price;
  512 |     |         uint160 price1 = pool1.price;
  513 |     |         
  514 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
  515 |     | 
  516 |     |         // Ensure prices never cross
  517 |     |         emit Prices(price0, price1);
  518 |     |         assert(price0 >= price1);
  519 |     | 
  520 |     |         // Ensure liquidityGlobal is decremented after burn
  521 |     |         emit LiquidityGlobal(liquidityGlobalBefore, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter);
  522 |     |         assert((poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter <= liquidityGlobalBefore));
  523 |     |     }
  524 |     | 
  525 | *   |     function claim(int24 claimAt, uint256 positionIndex) public {
  526 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  527 | *   |         positionIndex = positionIndex % limitPositions.length;
  528 | *   |         LimitPosition memory pos = limitPositions[positionIndex];
  529 | *   |         claimAt = pos.lower + (claimAt % (pos.upper - pos.lower));
  530 | *r  |         require(claimAt % tickSpacing == 0);
  531 |     | 
  532 |     |         LimitPoolValues memory poolValues;
  533 |     |         (,PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool0, PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool1, uint128 liquidityGlobalBefore,,,) = pool.globalState();
  534 |     | 
  535 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params;
  536 |     |         params.to = pos.owner;
  537 |     |         params.burnPercent = 0;
  538 |     |         params.positionId = pos.positionId;
  539 |     |         params.claim = claimAt;
  540 |     |         params.zeroForOne = pos.zeroForOne;
  541 |     |         
  542 |     |         emit PositionTicks(pos.lower, pos.upper);
  543 |     |         (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists) = pool.getResizedTicksForBurn(params);
  544 |     |         emit BurnTicks(lower, upper, positionExists);
  545 |     | 
  546 |     |         // ACTION
  547 |     |         pool.burnLimit(params);
  548 |     |         if (!positionExists) {
  549 |     |             limitPositions[positionIndex] = limitPositions[limitPositions.length - 1];
  550 |     |             delete limitPositions[limitPositions.length - 1];
  551 |     |         }
  552 |     |         else {
  553 |     |             // Update position data in array if not fully burned
  554 |     |             limitPositions[positionIndex] = LimitPosition(pos.owner, pos.positionId, lower, upper, pos.zeroForOne);
  555 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
  556 |     |             assert(lower < upper);
  557 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
  558 |     |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
  559 |     |         }
  560 |     | 
  561 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
  562 |     |         (,pool0, pool1, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,,,) = pool.globalState();
  563 |     |         uint160 price0 = pool0.price;
  564 |     |         uint160 price1 = pool1.price;
  565 |     | 
  566 |     |         // Ensure prices never cross
  567 |     |         emit Prices(price0, price1);
  568 |     |         assert(price0 >= price1);
  569 |     |     }

  749 | *   |     function mintRange(uint128 amount0, uint128 amount1, int24 lower, int24 upper) public tickPreconditions(lower, upper) {
  750 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  751 | *   |         mintAndApprove();
  752 | *   |         amount0 = amount0 + 1;
  753 | *   |         amount1 = amount1 + 1;
  754 |     |         // Ensure the newly created position is using different ticks
  755 | *   |         for(uint i = 0; i < rangePositions.length;) {
  756 | *   |             if(rangePositions[i].owner == msg.sender && rangePositions[i].lower == lower && rangePositions[i].upper == upper) {
  757 | *r  |                 revert("Position already exists");
  758 |     |             }
  759 |     |             unchecked {
  760 |     |                 ++i;
  761 |     |             }
  762 |     |         }
  763 |     | 
  764 | *   |         RangePoolValues memory poolValues;
  765 | *   |         RangePoolLocals memory poolStructs;
  766 | *   |         LiquidityDeltaValues memory values;
  767 |     | 
  768 | *   |         (poolStructs.pool,,, poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore,poolValues.positionIdNextBefore,,) = pool.globalState();
  769 | *   |         poolValues.priceBefore = poolStructs.pool.price;
  770 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityBefore = poolStructs.pool.liquidity;
  771 |     | 
  772 | *   |         (poolStructs.lower,) = pool.ticks(lower);
  773 | *   |         (poolStructs.upper,) = pool.ticks(upper);
  774 |     | 
  775 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
  776 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
  777 |     | 
  778 | *   |         poolValues.constants = pool.immutables();
  779 |     | 
  780 | *   |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeParams memory params;
  781 | *   |         params.to = msg.sender;
  782 | *   |         params.amount0 = amount0;
  783 | *   |         params.amount1 = amount1;
  784 | *   |         params.lower = lower;
  785 | *   |         params.upper = upper;
  786 |     | 
  787 |     |         // Get the ticks the position will be minted with rather than what was passed directly by fuzzer
  788 |     |         // This is so the we can properly compare before and after mint states of particular ticks.
  789 | *   |         bool posCreated = false;
  790 |     | 
  791 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
  792 | *   |             ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(lower, poolValues.constants),
  793 | *   |             ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(upper, poolValues.constants),
  794 | *   |             poolStructs.pool.price,
  795 | *   |             params.amount1,
  796 | *   |             params.amount0
  797 |     |         );
  798 | *   |         if (poolValues.liquidityMinted > 0) posCreated = true;
  799 | *   |         emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
  800 | *   |         emit PositionCreated(posCreated);
  801 |     | 
  802 |     |         // ACTION 
  803 | *r  |         pool.mintRange(params);
  804 | *   |         if (posCreated) rangePositions.push(RangePosition(msg.sender, poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, lower, upper));
  805 |     | 
  806 | *   |         (poolStructs.lower,) = pool.ticks(lower);
  807 | *   |         (poolStructs.upper,) = pool.ticks(upper);
  808 |     | 
  809 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
  810 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
  811 |     | 
  812 | *   |         values.liquidityDeltaLowerAfter = poolStructs.lower.liquidityDelta;
  813 | *   |         values.liquidityDeltaUpperAfter = poolStructs.upper.liquidityDelta;
  814 |     | 
  815 | *   |         (poolStructs.pool,,, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter,poolValues.positionIdNextAfter,,) = pool.globalState();
  816 | *   |         poolValues.priceAfter = poolStructs.pool.price;
  817 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAfter = poolStructs.pool.liquidity;
  818 |     |         
  819 |     |         // POST CONDITIONS
  820 |     |         
  821 |     |         // Ensure that liquidityAbsolute is incremented if position created
  822 | *   |         if (posCreated) {
  823 |     |             // positionIdNext should have been incremented
  824 | *   |             emit PositionIdNext(poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, poolValues.positionIdNextAfter);
  825 | *   |             assert(poolValues.positionIdNextAfter == poolValues.positionIdNextBefore + 1);
  826 | *   |             emit LiquidityAbsoluteLower(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
  827 | *   |             assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter > poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore);
  828 | *   |             emit LiquidityAbsoluteUpper(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
  829 | *   |             assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter > poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore);
  830 |     |         } else {
  831 |     |             // positionIdNext should not have been incremented
  832 |     |             emit PositionIdNext(poolValues.positionIdNextBefore, poolValues.positionIdNextAfter);
  833 |     |             assert(poolValues.positionIdNextAfter == poolValues.positionIdNextBefore);
  834 |     |             emit LiquidityAbsoluteLower(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter);
  835 |     |             assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperAfter == poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore);
  836 |     |             emit LiquidityAbsoluteUpper(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore, poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter);
  837 |     |             assert(poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerAfter == poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore);
  838 |     |         }
  839 |     | 
  840 | *   |         if (posCreated) {
  841 | *   |             emit PositionTicks(lower, upper);
  842 |     |             // Ensure positions ticks arent crossed
  843 | *   |             assert(lower < upper);
  844 |     |             // Ensure minted ticks on proper tick spacing
  845 | *   |             assert((lower % tickSpacing == 0) && (upper % tickSpacing == 0));
  846 |     |         }
  847 |     |         
  848 | *   |         emit LiquidityGlobal(poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore, poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter);
  849 | *   |         emit LiquidityRange(poolValues.liquidityBefore, poolValues.liquidityAfter);
  850 |     |         
  851 |     |         // Ensure liquidityGlobal is incremented after mint
  852 | *   |         if (posCreated) {
  853 | *   |             assert(poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter > poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore);
  854 |     |         } else {
  855 |     |             assert(poolValues.liquidityGlobalAfter == poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore);
  856 |     |         }
  857 |     |         
  858 |     |         // Ensure prices does not change
  859 | *   |         emit PriceChange(poolValues.priceBefore, poolValues.priceAfter);
  860 | *   |         assert(poolValues.priceBefore == poolValues.priceAfter);
  861 |     |     }
  862 |     | 
  863 | *   |     function burnRange(uint256 positionIndex, uint128 burnPercent) public {
  864 |     |         // PRE CONDITIONS
  865 | *   |         positionIndex = positionIndex % rangePositions.length;
  866 | *   |         RangePosition memory pos = rangePositions[positionIndex];
  867 | *   |         RangePoolValues memory poolValues;
  868 | *   |         RangePoolLocals memory poolStructs;
  869 |     | 
  870 | *   |         (poolStructs.pool,,, poolValues.liquidityGlobalBefore,poolValues.positionIdNextBefore,,) = pool.globalState();
  871 | *   |         poolValues.priceBefore = poolStructs.pool.price;
  872 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityBefore = poolStructs.pool.liquidity;
  873 |     | 
  874 | *   |         (poolStructs.lower,) = pool.ticks(pos.lower);
  875 | *   |         (poolStructs.upper,) = pool.ticks(pos.upper);
  876 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteLowerBefore = poolStructs.lower.liquidityAbsolute;
  877 | *   |         poolValues.liquidityAbsoluteUpperBefore = poolStructs.upper.liquidityAbsolute;
  878 |     | 
  879 | *   |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeParams memory params;
  880 | *   |         params.to = pos.owner;
  881 | *   |         params.burnPercent = burnPercent == 1e38 ? burnPercent : _between(burnPercent, 1e36, 1e38); //1e38;
  882 | *   |         params.positionId = pos.positionId;
  883 |     |         
  884 | *   |         emit PositionTicks(pos.lower, pos.upper);
  885 |     |         // (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists) = pool.getResizedTicksForBurn(params);

 1132 |     |     function liquidityMintedBackcalculates(uint128 amount, bool zeroForOne, int24 lower, int24 upper) tickPreconditions(lower, upper) internal {
 1133 |     |         // NOTE: Do not use the exact inputs of this function for POCs, use the inputs after the input validation
 1134 |     |         amount = amount + 1e5 + 1;
 1135 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.LimitImmutables memory immutables = pool.immutables();
 1136 |     |         uint256 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(lower, immutables);
 1137 |     |         uint256 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(upper, immutables);
 1138 |     | 
 1139 |     |         uint256 liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
 1140 |     |             priceLower,
 1141 |     |             priceUpper,
 1142 |     |             zeroForOne ? priceLower : priceUpper,
 1143 |     |             zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(amount),
 1144 |     |             zeroForOne ? uint256(amount) : 0
 1145 |     |         );
 1146 |     | 
 1147 |     |         (uint256 token0Amount, uint256 token1Amount) = ConstantProduct.getAmountsForLiquidity(
 1148 |     |             priceLower,
 1149 |     |             priceUpper,
 1150 |     |             zeroForOne ? priceLower : priceUpper,
 1151 |     |             liquidityMinted,
 1152 |     |             true
 1153 |     |         );
 1154 |     | 
 1155 |     |         if(zeroForOne) {
 1156 |     |             emit LiquidityMinted(amount, token0Amount, zeroForOne);
 1157 |     |             assert(token0Amount <= amount);
 1158 |     |             
 1159 |     |         }
 1160 |     |         else {
 1161 |     |             emit LiquidityMinted(amount, token1Amount, zeroForOne);
 1162 |     |             assert(token1Amount <= amount);
 1163 |     |         }
 1164 |     |     }

 249 |     |         );
 250 |     |     }
 251 |     | 
 252 |     |     function snapshotRange(
 253 |     |         uint32 positionId 
 254 |     |     ) external view override returns (
 255 |     |         int56   tickSecondsAccum,
 256 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 257 |     |         uint128 feesOwed0,
 258 |     |         uint128 feesOwed1
 259 |     |     ) {
 260 |     |         return SnapshotRangeCall.perform(
 261 |     |             positions,
 262 |     |             ticks,
 263 |     |             globalState,
 264 |     |             immutables(),
 265 |     |             positionId
 266 |     |         );
 267 |     |     }

 269 |     |     function snapshotLimit(
 270 |     |         SnapshotLimitParams memory params
 271 |     |     ) external view override returns(
 272 |     |         uint128,
 273 |     |         uint128
 274 |     |     ) {
 275 |     |         return SnapshotLimitCall.perform(
 276 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? positions0 : positions1,
 277 |     |             ticks,
 278 |     |             limitTickMap,
 279 |     |             globalState,
 280 |     |             immutables(),
 281 |     |             params
 282 |     |         );
 283 |     |     }
 284 |     | 
 285 |     |     function immutables() public view returns (
 286 |     |         LimitImmutables memory
 287 |     |     ) {
 288 |     |         return LimitImmutables(
 289 |     |             owner(),
 290 |     |             original,
 291 |     |             factory,
 292 |     |             PriceBounds(minPrice(), maxPrice()),
 293 |     |             token0(),
 294 |     |             token1(),
 295 |     |             poolToken(),
 296 |     |             genesisTime(),
 297 |     |             tickSpacing(),
 298 |     |             swapFee()
 299 |     |         );
 300 |     |     }
 301 |     | 
 302 |     |     function getResizedTicksForMint(
 303 |     |         MintLimitParams memory params
 304 |     |     ) external returns (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionCreated){
 305 |     |         MintLimitCache memory cache;
 306 |     |         {
 307 |     |             cache.state = globalState;
 308 |     |             cache.constants = immutables();
 309 |     |         }
 310 |     | 
 311 |     |         try EchidnaMintLimitCall.getResizedTicks(
 312 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? positions0 : positions1,
 313 |     |             ticks,
 314 |     |             samples,
 315 |     |             rangeTickMap,
 316 |     |             limitTickMap,
 317 |     |             globalState,
 318 |     |             params,
 319 |     |             cache
 320 |     |         ) {
 321 |     |         } catch (bytes memory data) {
 322 |     |             emit SimulateMint(data);
 323 |     |             bytes4 sig;
 324 |     |             assembly {
 325 |     |                 sig := mload(add(data, 0x20))
 326 |     |             }
 327 |     |             
 328 |     |             // SimulateMint error
 329 |     |             if (sig == hex"5cc1f67b") {
 330 |     |                 (, lower, upper, positionCreated) = abi.decode(abi.encodePacked(bytes28(0), data),(bytes32,int24,int24,bool));
 331 |     |             }
 332 |     |             else {
 333 |     |                 lower = -8388608;
 334 |     |                 upper = -8388608;
 335 |     |                 positionCreated = false;
 336 |     |             }
 337 |     |         }
 338 |     |     }
 339 |     | 
 340 |     |     function getResizedTicksForBurn(
 341 |     |         BurnLimitParams memory params
 342 |     |     ) external returns (int24 lower, int24 upper, bool positionExists){
 343 |     |         if (params.to == address(0)) revert CollectToZeroAddress();
 344 |     |         BurnLimitCache memory cache;
 345 |     |         cache.constants = immutables();
 346 |     | 
 347 |     |         try EchidnaBurnLimitCall.getResizedTicks(
 348 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? positions0 : positions1,
 349 |     |             ticks,
 350 |     |             limitTickMap,
 351 |     |             globalState,
 352 |     |             params, 
 353 |     |             cache
 354 |     |         ) {
 355 |     |         } catch (bytes memory data) {
 356 |     |             bytes4 sig;
 357 |     |             assembly {
 358 |     |                 sig := mload(add(data, 0x20))
 359 |     |             }
 360 |     |             // SimulateBurn error
 361 |     |             if (sig == hex"97dd6e0a") {
 362 |     |                 (, lower, upper, positionExists) = abi.decode(abi.encodePacked(bytes28(0), data),(bytes32,int24,int24,bool));
 363 |     |             }
 364 |     |              else {
 365 |     |                 lower = -8388608;
 366 |     |                 upper = -8388608;
 367 |     |                 positionExists = false;
 368 |     |             }
 369 |     |         }
 370 |     |     }
 371 |     | 
 372 |     |     function priceBounds(
 373 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 374 |     |     ) external pure returns (uint160, uint160) {
 375 |     |         return ConstantProduct.priceBounds(tickSpacing);
 376 |     |     }
 377 |     | 
 378 |     |     function _onlyOwner() private view {
 379 |     |         if (msg.sender != owner()) revert OwnerOnly();
 380 |     |     }
 381 |     | 
 382 |     |     function _onlyCanoncialClones() private view {
 383 |     |         // compute pool key
 384 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(original, token0(), token1(), swapFee()));
 385 |     |         
 386 |     |         // compute canonical pool address
 387 |     |         address predictedAddress = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 388 |     |             original,
 389 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 390 |     |                 owner(),
 391 |     |                 token0(),
 392 |     |                 token1(),
 393 |     |                 poolToken(),
 394 |     |                 minPrice(),
 395 |     |                 maxPrice(),
 396 |     |                 genesisTime(),
 397 |     |                 tickSpacing(),
 398 |     |                 swapFee()
 399 |     |             ),
 400 |     |             key,
 401 |     |             factory
 402 |     |         );
 403 |     |         // only allow delegateCall from canonical clones
 404 |     |         if (address(this) != predictedAddress) require(false, 'NoDelegateCall()');
 405 |     |     }
 406 |     | 
 407 |     |     function _onlyFactory() private view {
 408 |     |         if (msg.sender != factory) revert FactoryOnly();
 409 |     |     }
 410 |     | }

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import './interfaces/range/IRangePool.sol';
   5 |     | import './interfaces/limit/ILimitPool.sol';
   6 |     | import './interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   7 |     | import './interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol';
   8 |     | import './interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolFactory.sol';
   9 |     | import './interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolManager.sol';
  10 |     | import './base/events/LimitPoolFactoryEvents.sol';
  11 |     | import './utils/LimitPoolErrors.sol';
  12 |     | import './external/solady/LibClone.sol';
  13 |     | import './libraries/utils/SafeCast.sol';
  14 |     | import './libraries/math/ConstantProduct.sol';
  15 |     | 
  16 |     | contract LimitPoolFactory is 
  17 |     |     ILimitPoolFactory,
  18 |     |     LimitPoolStructs,
  19 |     |     RangePoolStructs,
  20 |     |     LimitPoolFactoryEvents,
  21 |     |     LimitPoolFactoryErrors
  22 |     | {
  23 |     |     using LibClone for address;
  24 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  25 |     | 
  26 |     |     address immutable public owner;
  27 |     |     address immutable public original;
  28 |     | 
  29 |     |     constructor(
  30 |     |         address owner_
  31 |     |     ) {
  32 |     |         owner = owner_;
  33 |     |         original = address(this);
  34 |     |     }
  35 |     | 
  36 |     |     function createLimitPool(
  37 |     |         LimitPoolParams memory params
  38 |     |     ) public override returns (
  39 |     |         address pool,
  40 |     |         address poolToken
  41 |     |     ) {
  42 |     | 
  43 |     |         // validate token pair
  44 |     |         if (params.tokenIn == params.tokenOut || params.tokenIn == address(0) || params.tokenOut == address(0)) {
  45 |     |             revert InvalidTokenAddress();
  46 |     |         }
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |         // sort tokens by address
  49 |     |         LimitImmutables memory constants;
  50 |     |         (constants.token0, constants.token1) = params.tokenIn < params.tokenOut ? (params.tokenIn,  params.tokenOut) 
  51 |     |                                                                                 : (params.tokenOut, params.tokenIn);
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |         // check if tick spacing supported
  54 |     |         constants.swapFee = params.swapFee;
  55 |     |         constants.tickSpacing = ILimitPoolManager(owner).feeTiers(params.swapFee);
  56 |     |         if (constants.tickSpacing == 0) revert FeeTierNotSupported();
  57 |     | 
  58 |     |         // check if pool type supported
  59 |     |         (
  60 |     |             address poolImpl,
  61 |     |             address tokenImpl
  62 |     |          ) = ILimitPoolManager(owner).implementations(params.poolType);
  63 |     |         if (poolImpl == address(0) || tokenImpl == address(0)) revert PoolTypeNotSupported();
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |         // generate key for pool
  66 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
  67 |     |             poolImpl,
  68 |     |             constants.token0,
  69 |     |             constants.token1,
  70 |     |             constants.swapFee
  71 |     |         ));
  72 |     | 
  73 |     |         // check if pool already exists
  74 |     |         if (pools[key] != address(0)) revert PoolAlreadyExists();
  75 |     | 
  76 |     |         // set immutables
  77 |     |         constants.owner = owner;
  78 |     |         constants.factory = original;
  79 |     |         constants.genesisTime = block.timestamp.toUint32();
  80 |     |         (
  81 |     |             constants.bounds.min,
  82 |     |             constants.bounds.max
  83 |     |         ) = ILimitPool(poolImpl).priceBounds(constants.tickSpacing);
  84 |     | 
  85 |     |         // take that ERC1155 contract address and pass that into pool
  86 |     |         // launch pool token
  87 |     |         constants.poolToken = tokenImpl.cloneDeterministic({
  88 |     |             salt: key,
  89 |     |             data: abi.encodePacked(
  90 |     |                 poolImpl
  91 |     |             )
  92 |     |         });
  93 |     | 
  94 |     |         // launch pool
  95 |     |         pool = poolImpl.cloneDeterministic({
  96 |     |             salt: key,
  97 |     |             data: abi.encodePacked(
  98 |     |                 constants.owner,
  99 |     |                 constants.token0,
 100 |     |                 constants.token1,
 101 |     |                 constants.poolToken,
 102 |     |                 constants.bounds.min,
 103 |     |                 constants.bounds.max,
 104 |     |                 constants.genesisTime,
 105 |     |                 constants.tickSpacing,
 106 |     |                 constants.swapFee
 107 |     |             )
 108 |     |         });
 109 |     | 
 110 |     |         // initialize pool storage
 111 |     |         ILimitPool(pool).initialize(params.startPrice);
 112 |     | 
 113 |     |         // save pool in mapping
 114 |     |         pools[key] = pool;
 115 |     | 
 116 |     |         emit PoolCreated(
 117 |     |             pool,
 118 |     |             poolToken,
 119 |     |             poolImpl,
 120 |     |             tokenImpl,
 121 |     |             constants.token0,
 122 |     |             constants.token1,
 123 |     |             constants.swapFee,
 124 |     |             constants.tickSpacing
 125 |     |         );
 126 |     | 
 127 |     |         return (pool, constants.poolToken);
 128 |     |     }
 129 |     | 
 130 |     |     function createLimitPoolAndMint(
 131 |     |         LimitPoolParams memory params,
 132 |     |         MintRangeParams[] memory mintRangeParams,
 133 |     |         MintLimitParams[] memory mintLimitParams
 134 |     |     ) external returns (
 135 |     |         address pool,
 136 |     |         address poolToken
 137 |     |     ) {
 138 |     |         // check if pool exists
 139 |     |         (
 140 |     |             pool,
 141 |     |             poolToken
 142 |     |         ) = getLimitPool(
 143 |     |             params.poolType,
 144 |     |             params.tokenIn,
 145 |     |             params.tokenOut,
 146 |     |             params.swapFee
 147 |     |         );
 148 |     |         // create if pool doesn't exist
 149 |     |         if (pool == address(0)) {
 150 |     |             (
 151 |     |                 pool,
 152 |     |                 poolToken
 153 |     |             ) = createLimitPool(
 154 |     |                 params
 155 |     |             );
 156 |     |         }
 157 |     |         // mint initial range positions
 158 |     |         for (uint i = 0; i < mintRangeParams.length;) {
 159 |     |             IRangePool(pool).mintRange(mintRangeParams[i]);
 160 |     |             unchecked {
 161 |     |                 ++i;
 162 |     |             }
 163 |     |         }
 164 |     |         // mint initial limit positions
 165 |     |         for (uint i = 0; i < mintLimitParams.length;) {
 166 |     |             ILimitPool(pool).mintLimit(mintLimitParams[i]);
 167 |     |             unchecked {
 168 |     |                 ++i;
 169 |     |             }
 170 |     |         }
 171 |     |     } 
 172 |     | 
 173 |     |     function getLimitPool(
 174 |     |         bytes32 poolType,
 175 |     |         address tokenIn,
 176 |     |         address tokenOut,
 177 |     |         uint16 swapFee
 178 |     |     ) public view override returns (
 179 |     |         address pool,
 180 |     |         address poolToken
 181 |     |     ) {
 182 |     |         // set lexographical token address ordering
 183 |     |         address token0 = tokenIn < tokenOut ? tokenIn : tokenOut;
 184 |     |         address token1 = tokenIn < tokenOut ? tokenOut : tokenIn;
 185 |     | 
 186 |     |         // check if tick spacing supported
 187 |     |         int16 tickSpacing = ILimitPoolManager(owner).feeTiers(swapFee);
 188 |     |         if (tickSpacing == 0) revert FeeTierNotSupported();
 189 |     | 
 190 |     |         // check if pool type supported
 191 |     |         (
 192 |     |             address poolImpl,
 193 |     |             address tokenImpl
 194 |     |          ) = ILimitPoolManager(owner).implementations(poolType);
 195 |     |         if (poolImpl == address(0) || tokenImpl == address(0)) revert PoolTypeNotSupported();
 196 |     | 
 197 |     |         // generate key for pool
 198 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
 199 |     |             poolImpl,
 200 |     |             token0,
 201 |     |             token1,
 202 |     |             swapFee
 203 |     |         ));
 204 |     | 
 205 |     |         pool = pools[key];
 206 |     | 
 207 |     |         poolToken = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 208 |     |             tokenImpl,
 209 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 210 |     |                 poolImpl
 211 |     |             ),
 212 |     |             key,
 213 |     |             address(this)
 214 |     |         );
 215 |     | 
 216 |     |         return (pool, poolToken);
 217 |     |     }
 218 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.7.0) (token/ERC20/ERC20.sol)
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | pragma solidity ^0.8.0;
   5 |     | 
   6 |     | import "./IERC20.sol";
   7 |     | import "./extensions/IERC20Metadata.sol";
   8 |     | import "../../utils/Context.sol";
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | /**
  11 |     |  * @dev Implementation of the {IERC20} interface.
  12 |     |  *
  13 |     |  * This implementation is agnostic to the way tokens are created. This means
  14 |     |  * that a supply mechanism has to be added in a derived contract using {_mint}.
  15 |     |  * For a generic mechanism see {ERC20PresetMinterPauser}.
  16 |     |  *
  17 |     |  * TIP: For a detailed writeup see our guide
  18 |     |  * https://forum.zeppelin.solutions/t/how-to-implement-erc20-supply-mechanisms/226[How
  19 |     |  * to implement supply mechanisms].
  20 |     |  *
  21 |     |  * We have followed general OpenZeppelin Contracts guidelines: functions revert
  22 |     |  * instead returning `false` on failure. This behavior is nonetheless
  23 |     |  * conventional and does not conflict with the expectations of ERC20
  24 |     |  * applications.
  25 |     |  *
  26 |     |  * Additionally, an {Approval} event is emitted on calls to {transferFrom}.
  27 |     |  * This allows applications to reconstruct the allowance for all accounts just
  28 |     |  * by listening to said events. Other implementations of the EIP may not emit
  29 |     |  * these events, as it isn't required by the specification.
  30 |     |  *
  31 |     |  * Finally, the non-standard {decreaseAllowance} and {increaseAllowance}
  32 |     |  * functions have been added to mitigate the well-known issues around setting
  33 |     |  * allowances. See {IERC20-approve}.
  34 |     |  */
  35 |     | contract ERC20 is Context, IERC20, IERC20Metadata {
  36 |     |     mapping(address => uint256) private _balances;
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |     mapping(address => mapping(address => uint256)) private _allowances;
  39 |     | 
  40 |     |     uint256 private _totalSupply;
  41 |     | 
  42 |     |     string private _name;
  43 |     |     string private _symbol;
  44 |     | 
  45 |     |     /**
  46 |     |      * @dev Sets the values for {name} and {symbol}.
  47 |     |      *
  48 |     |      * The default value of {decimals} is 18. To select a different value for
  49 |     |      * {decimals} you should overload it.
  50 |     |      *
  51 |     |      * All two of these values are immutable: they can only be set once during
  52 |     |      * construction.
  53 |     |      */
  54 |     |     constructor(string memory name_, string memory symbol_) {
  55 |     |         _name = name_;
  56 |     |         _symbol = symbol_;
  57 |     |     }
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |     /**
  60 |     |      * @dev Returns the name of the token.
  61 |     |      */
  62 |     |     function name() public view virtual override returns (string memory) {
  63 |     |         return _name;
  64 |     |     }
  65 |     | 
  66 |     |     /**
  67 |     |      * @dev Returns the symbol of the token, usually a shorter version of the
  68 |     |      * name.
  69 |     |      */
  70 |     |     function symbol() public view virtual override returns (string memory) {
  71 |     |         return _symbol;
  72 |     |     }
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |     /**
  75 |     |      * @dev Returns the number of decimals used to get its user representation.
  76 |     |      * For example, if `decimals` equals `2`, a balance of `505` tokens should
  77 |     |      * be displayed to a user as `5.05` (`505 / 10 ** 2`).
  78 |     |      *
  79 |     |      * Tokens usually opt for a value of 18, imitating the relationship between
  80 |     |      * Ether and Wei. This is the value {ERC20} uses, unless this function is
  81 |     |      * overridden;
  82 |     |      *
  83 |     |      * NOTE: This information is only used for _display_ purposes: it in
  84 |     |      * no way affects any of the arithmetic of the contract, including
  85 |     |      * {IERC20-balanceOf} and {IERC20-transfer}.
  86 |     |      */
  87 |     |     function decimals() public view virtual override returns (uint8) {
  88 |     |         return 18;
  89 |     |     }
  90 |     | 
  91 |     |     /**

  96 |     |     }

 123 | *   |         return _allowances[owner][spender];

 131 |     |      *

 133 |     |      *

 135 |     |      */

 137 | *   |         address owner = _msgSender();
 138 | *   |         _approve(owner, spender, amount);
 139 | *   |         return true;
 140 |     |     }

 142 |     |     /**
 143 |     |      * @dev See {IERC20-transferFrom}.
 144 |     |      *
 145 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance. This is not
 146 |     |      * required by the EIP. See the note at the beginning of {ERC20}.
 147 |     |      *
 148 |     |      * NOTE: Does not update the allowance if the current allowance
 149 |     |      * is the maximum `uint256`.
 150 |     |      *

 152 |     |      *
 153 |     |      * - `from` and `to` cannot be the zero address.
 154 |     |      * - `from` must have a balance of at least `amount`.
 155 |     |      * - the caller must have allowance for ``from``'s tokens of at least
 156 |     |      * `amount`.

 165 | *   |         _transfer(from, to, amount);
 166 | *   |         return true;
 167 |     |     }
 168 |     | 
 169 |     |     /**
 170 |     |      * @dev Atomically increases the allowance granted to `spender` by the caller.
 171 |     |      *
 172 |     |      * This is an alternative to {approve} that can be used as a mitigation for
 173 |     |      * problems described in {IERC20-approve}.
 174 |     |      *
 175 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance.
 176 |     |      *
 177 |     |      * Requirements:
 178 |     |      *
 179 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 180 |     |      */
 181 |     |     function increaseAllowance(address spender, uint256 addedValue) public virtual returns (bool) {
 182 |     |         address owner = _msgSender();
 183 |     |         _approve(owner, spender, allowance(owner, spender) + addedValue);
 184 |     |         return true;
 185 |     |     }
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |     /**
 188 |     |      * @dev Atomically decreases the allowance granted to `spender` by the caller.
 189 |     |      *
 190 |     |      * This is an alternative to {approve} that can be used as a mitigation for
 191 |     |      * problems described in {IERC20-approve}.
 192 |     |      *
 193 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event indicating the updated allowance.
 194 |     |      *
 195 |     |      * Requirements:
 196 |     |      *
 197 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 198 |     |      * - `spender` must have allowance for the caller of at least
 199 |     |      * `subtractedValue`.
 200 |     |      */
 201 |     |     function decreaseAllowance(address spender, uint256 subtractedValue) public virtual returns (bool) {
 202 |     |         address owner = _msgSender();
 203 |     |         uint256 currentAllowance = allowance(owner, spender);
 204 |     |         require(currentAllowance >= subtractedValue, "ERC20: decreased allowance below zero");
 205 |     |         unchecked {
 206 |     |             _approve(owner, spender, currentAllowance - subtractedValue);
 207 |     |         }
 208 |     | 
 209 |     |         return true;
 210 |     |     }
 211 |     | 
 212 |     |     /**
 213 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` of tokens from `from` to `to`.
 214 |     |      *
 215 |     |      * This internal function is equivalent to {transfer}, and can be used to
 216 |     |      * e.g. implement automatic token fees, slashing mechanisms, etc.
 217 |     |      *
 218 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 219 |     |      *
 220 |     |      * Requirements:
 221 |     |      *
 222 |     |      * - `from` cannot be the zero address.
 223 |     |      * - `to` cannot be the zero address.
 224 |     |      * - `from` must have a balance of at least `amount`.
 225 |     |      */
 226 | *   |     function _transfer(
 227 |     |         address from,
 228 |     |         address to,
 229 |     |         uint256 amount
 230 | *   |     ) internal virtual {
 231 | *   |         require(from != address(0), "ERC20: transfer from the zero address");
 232 | *   |         require(to != address(0), "ERC20: transfer to the zero address");
 233 |     | 
 234 | *   |         _beforeTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);
 235 |     | 
 236 | *   |         uint256 fromBalance = _balances[from];
 237 | *   |         require(fromBalance >= amount, "ERC20: transfer amount exceeds balance");
 238 |     |         unchecked {
 239 | *   |             _balances[from] = fromBalance - amount;
 240 |     |         }
 241 | *   |         _balances[to] += amount;
 242 |     | 
 243 | *   |         emit Transfer(from, to, amount);
 244 |     | 
 245 | *   |         _afterTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);
 246 |     |     }
 247 |     | 
 248 |     |     /** @dev Creates `amount` tokens and assigns them to `account`, increasing
 249 |     |      * the total supply.
 250 |     |      *
 251 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event with `from` set to the zero address.
 252 |     |      *
 253 |     |      * Requirements:
 254 |     |      *
 255 |     |      * - `account` cannot be the zero address.
 256 |     |      */
 257 | *   |     function _mint(address account, uint256 amount) internal virtual {
 258 | *   |         require(account != address(0), "ERC20: mint to the zero address");
 259 |     | 
 260 | *   |         _beforeTokenTransfer(address(0), account, amount);
 261 |     | 
 262 | *   |         _totalSupply += amount;
 263 | *   |         _balances[account] += amount;
 264 | *   |         emit Transfer(address(0), account, amount);
 265 |     | 
 266 | *   |         _afterTokenTransfer(address(0), account, amount);
 267 |     |     }
 268 |     | 
 269 |     |     /**
 270 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from `account`, reducing the
 271 |     |      * total supply.
 272 |     |      *
 273 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event with `to` set to the zero address.
 274 |     |      *
 275 |     |      * Requirements:
 276 |     |      *
 277 |     |      * - `account` cannot be the zero address.
 278 |     |      * - `account` must have at least `amount` tokens.
 279 |     |      */
 280 |     |     function _burn(address account, uint256 amount) internal virtual {
 281 |     |         require(account != address(0), "ERC20: burn from the zero address");
 282 |     | 
 283 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(account, address(0), amount);
 284 |     | 
 285 |     |         uint256 accountBalance = _balances[account];
 286 |     |         require(accountBalance >= amount, "ERC20: burn amount exceeds balance");
 287 |     |         unchecked {
 288 |     |             _balances[account] = accountBalance - amount;
 289 |     |         }
 290 |     |         _totalSupply -= amount;
 291 |     | 
 292 |     |         emit Transfer(account, address(0), amount);
 293 |     | 
 294 |     |         _afterTokenTransfer(account, address(0), amount);
 295 |     |     }
 296 |     | 
 297 |     |     /**
 298 |     |      * @dev Sets `amount` as the allowance of `spender` over the `owner` s tokens.
 299 |     |      *
 300 |     |      * This internal function is equivalent to `approve`, and can be used to
 301 |     |      * e.g. set automatic allowances for certain subsystems, etc.
 302 |     |      *
 303 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event.
 304 |     |      *
 305 |     |      * Requirements:
 306 |     |      *
 307 |     |      * - `owner` cannot be the zero address.
 308 |     |      * - `spender` cannot be the zero address.
 309 |     |      */
 310 | *   |     function _approve(
 311 |     |         address owner,
 312 |     |         address spender,
 313 |     |         uint256 amount
 314 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 315 | *   |         require(owner != address(0), "ERC20: approve from the zero address");
 316 | *   |         require(spender != address(0), "ERC20: approve to the zero address");
 317 |     | 
 318 | *   |         _allowances[owner][spender] = amount;
 319 | *   |         emit Approval(owner, spender, amount);
 320 |     |     }
 321 |     | 
 322 |     |     /**
 323 |     |      * @dev Updates `owner` s allowance for `spender` based on spent `amount`.
 324 |     |      *
 325 |     |      * Does not update the allowance amount in case of infinite allowance.
 326 |     |      * Revert if not enough allowance is available.
 327 |     |      *
 328 |     |      * Might emit an {Approval} event.
 329 |     |      */
 330 | *   |     function _spendAllowance(
 331 |     |         address owner,
 332 |     |         address spender,
 333 |     |         uint256 amount
 334 | *   |     ) internal virtual {
 335 | *   |         uint256 currentAllowance = allowance(owner, spender);
 336 | *   |         if (currentAllowance != type(uint256).max) {
 337 | *   |             require(currentAllowance >= amount, "ERC20: insufficient allowance");
 338 |     |             unchecked {
 339 | *   |                 _approve(owner, spender, currentAllowance - amount);
 340 |     |             }
 341 |     |         }
 342 |     |     }
 343 |     | 
 344 |     |     /**
 345 |     |      * @dev Hook that is called before any transfer of tokens. This includes
 346 |     |      * minting and burning.
 347 |     |      *
 348 |     |      * Calling conditions:
 349 |     |      *
 350 |     |      * - when `from` and `to` are both non-zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens
 351 |     |      * will be transferred to `to`.
 352 |     |      * - when `from` is zero, `amount` tokens will be minted for `to`.
 353 |     |      * - when `to` is zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens will be burned.
 354 |     |      * - `from` and `to` are never both zero.
 355 |     |      *
 356 |     |      * To learn more about hooks, head to xref:ROOT:extending-contracts.adoc#using-hooks[Using Hooks].
 357 |     |      */
 358 | *   |     function _beforeTokenTransfer(
 359 |     |         address from,
 360 |     |         address to,
 361 |     |         uint256 amount
 362 |     |     ) internal virtual {}
 363 |     | 
 364 |     |     /**
 365 |     |      * @dev Hook that is called after any transfer of tokens. This includes
 366 |     |      * minting and burning.
 367 |     |      *
 368 |     |      * Calling conditions:
 369 |     |      *
 370 |     |      * - when `from` and `to` are both non-zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens
 371 |     |      * has been transferred to `to`.
 372 |     |      * - when `from` is zero, `amount` tokens have been minted for `to`.
 373 |     |      * - when `to` is zero, `amount` of ``from``'s tokens have been burned.
 374 |     |      * - `from` and `to` are never both zero.

 377 |     |      */
 378 | *   |     function _afterTokenTransfer(
 379 |     |         address from,
 380 |     |         address to,
 381 |     |         uint256 amount
 382 |     |     ) internal virtual {}
 383 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/IERC20.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.6.0) (token/ERC20/IERC20.sol)
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | pragma solidity ^0.8.0;
  5 |     | 
  6 |     | /**
  7 |     |  * @dev Interface of the ERC20 standard as defined in the EIP.
  8 |     |  */
  9 |     | interface IERC20 {
 10 |     |     /**
 11 |     |      * @dev Emitted when `value` tokens are moved from one account (`from`) to
 12 |     |      * another (`to`).
 13 |     |      *
 14 |     |      * Note that `value` may be zero.
 15 |     |      */
 16 |     |     event Transfer(address indexed from, address indexed to, uint256 value);
 17 |     | 
 18 |     |     /**
 19 |     |      * @dev Emitted when the allowance of a `spender` for an `owner` is set by
 20 |     |      * a call to {approve}. `value` is the new allowance.
 21 |     |      */
 22 |     |     event Approval(address indexed owner, address indexed spender, uint256 value);
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     /**
 25 |     |      * @dev Returns the amount of tokens in existence.
 26 |     |      */
 27 |     |     function totalSupply() external view returns (uint256);
 28 |     | 
 29 |     |     /**
 30 |     |      * @dev Returns the amount of tokens owned by `account`.
 31 |     |      */
 32 |     |     function balanceOf(address account) external view returns (uint256);
 33 |     | 
 34 |     |     /**
 35 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` tokens from the caller's account to `to`.
 36 |     |      *
 37 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 38 |     |      *
 39 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 40 |     |      */
 41 |     |     function transfer(address to, uint256 amount) external returns (bool);
 42 |     | 
 43 |     |     /**
 44 |     |      * @dev Returns the remaining number of tokens that `spender` will be
 45 |     |      * allowed to spend on behalf of `owner` through {transferFrom}. This is
 46 |     |      * zero by default.
 47 |     |      *
 48 |     |      * This value changes when {approve} or {transferFrom} are called.
 49 |     |      */
 50 |     |     function allowance(address owner, address spender) external view returns (uint256);
 51 |     | 
 52 |     |     /**
 53 |     |      * @dev Sets `amount` as the allowance of `spender` over the caller's tokens.
 54 |     |      *
 55 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 56 |     |      *
 57 |     |      * IMPORTANT: Beware that changing an allowance with this method brings the risk
 58 |     |      * that someone may use both the old and the new allowance by unfortunate
 59 |     |      * transaction ordering. One possible solution to mitigate this race
 60 |     |      * condition is to first reduce the spender's allowance to 0 and set the
 61 |     |      * desired value afterwards:
 62 |     |      * https://github.com/ethereum/EIPs/issues/20#issuecomment-263524729
 63 |     |      *
 64 |     |      * Emits an {Approval} event.
 65 |     |      */
 66 |     |     function approve(address spender, uint256 amount) external returns (bool);
 67 |     | 
 68 |     |     /**
 69 |     |      * @dev Moves `amount` tokens from `from` to `to` using the
 70 |     |      * allowance mechanism. `amount` is then deducted from the caller's
 71 |     |      * allowance.
 72 |     |      *
 73 |     |      * Returns a boolean value indicating whether the operation succeeded.
 74 |     |      *
 75 |     |      * Emits a {Transfer} event.
 76 |     |      */
 77 |     |     function transferFrom(
 78 |     |         address from,
 79 |     |         address to,
 80 |     |         uint256 amount
 81 |     |     ) external returns (bool);
 82 |     | }
 83 |     |

  2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.5.0) (token/ERC20/extensions/ERC20Burnable.sol)
  3 |     |

  5 |     | 
  6 |     | import "../ERC20.sol";
  7 |     | import "../../../utils/Context.sol";
  8 |     | 
  9 |     | /**
 10 |     |  * @dev Extension of {ERC20} that allows token holders to destroy both their own
 11 |     |  * tokens and those that they have an allowance for, in a way that can be
 12 |     |  * recognized off-chain (via event analysis).
 13 |     |  */
 14 |     | abstract contract ERC20Burnable is Context, ERC20 {
 15 |     |     /**
 16 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from the caller.
 17 |     |      *
 18 |     |      * See {ERC20-_burn}.
 19 |     |      */
 20 |     |     function burn(uint256 amount) public virtual {
 21 |     |         _burn(_msgSender(), amount);
 22 |     |     }
 23 |     | 
 24 |     |     /**
 25 |     |      * @dev Destroys `amount` tokens from `account`, deducting from the caller's
 26 |     |      * allowance.
 27 |     |      *
 28 |     |      * See {ERC20-_burn} and {ERC20-allowance}.
 29 |     |      *
 30 |     |      * Requirements:
 31 |     |      *
 32 |     |      * - the caller must have allowance for ``accounts``'s tokens of at least
 33 |     |      * `amount`.
 34 |     |      */
 35 |     |     function burnFrom(address account, uint256 amount) public virtual {
 36 |     |         _spendAllowance(account, _msgSender(), amount);
 37 |     |         _burn(account, amount);
 38 |     |     }
 39 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/openzeppelin/security/ReentrancyGuard.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | // OpenZeppelin Contracts (last updated v4.9.0) (security/ReentrancyGuard.sol)
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
  5 |     | 
  6 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
  7 |     | 
  8 |     | /**
  9 |     |  * @dev Contract module that helps prevent reentrant calls to a function.
 10 |     |  *
 11 |     |  * Inheriting from `ReentrancyGuard` will make the {nonReentrant} modifier
 12 |     |  * available, which can be applied to functions to make sure there are no nested
 13 |     |  * (reentrant) calls to them.
 14 |     |  *
 15 |     |  * Note that because there is a single `nonReentrant` guard, functions marked as
 16 |     |  * `nonReentrant` may not call one another. This can be worked around by making
 17 |     |  * those functions `private`, and then adding `external` `nonReentrant` entry
 18 |     |  * points to them.
 19 |     |  *
 20 |     |  * TIP: If you would like to learn more about reentrancy and alternative ways
 21 |     |  * to protect against it, check out our blog post
 22 |     |  * https://blog.openzeppelin.com/reentrancy-after-istanbul/[Reentrancy After Istanbul].
 23 |     |  */
 24 |     | abstract contract ReentrancyGuard is PoolsharkStructs {
 25 |     |     // Booleans are more expensive than uint256 or any type that takes up a full
 26 |     |     // word because each write operation emits an extra SLOAD to first read the
 27 |     |     // slot's contents, replace the bits taken up by the boolean, and then write
 28 |     |     // back. This is the compiler's defense against contract upgrades and
 29 |     |     // pointer aliasing, and it cannot be disabled.
 30 |     | 
 31 |     |     // The values being non-zero value makes deployment a bit more expensive,
 32 |     |     // but in exchange the refund on every call to nonReentrant will be lower in
 33 |     |     // amount. Since refunds are capped to a percentage of the total
 34 |     |     // transaction's gas, it is best to keep them low in cases like this one, to
 35 |     |     // increase the likelihood of the full refund coming into effect.
 36 |     |     uint8 private constant _NOT_ENTERED = 1;
 37 |     |     uint8 private constant _ENTERED = 2;
 38 |     | 
 39 |     |     /**
 40 |     |      * @dev Unauthorized reentrant call.
 41 |     |      */
 42 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardReentrantCall();
 43 |     | 
 44 |     |     /**
 45 |     |      * @dev Unauthorized read-only reentrant call.
 46 |     |      */
 47 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardReadOnlyReentrantCall();
 48 |     | 
 49 |     |     /**
 50 |     |      * @dev Reentrant state invalid.
 51 |     |      */
 52 |     |     error ReentrancyGuardInvalidState();
 53 |     | 
 54 |     |     /**
 55 |     |      * @dev Prevents a contract from calling itself, directly or indirectly.
 56 |     |      * Calling a `nonReentrant` function from another `nonReentrant`
 57 |     |      * function is not supported. It is possible to prevent this from happening
 58 |     |      * by making the `nonReentrant` function external, and making it call a
 59 |     |      * `private` function that does the actual work.
 60 |     |      */
 61 |     |     modifier nonReentrant(GlobalState storage state) {
 62 |     |         _nonReentrantBefore(state);
 63 |     |         _;
 64 |     |         _nonReentrantAfter(state);
 65 |     |     }
 66 |     | 
 67 |     |     function _nonReentrantBefore(GlobalState storage state) private {
 68 |     |         // On the first call to nonReentrant, _status will be _NOT_ENTERED
 69 |     |         if (state.unlocked == _ENTERED) {
 70 |     |             revert ReentrancyGuardReentrantCall();
 71 |     |         }
 72 |     | 
 73 |     |         // Any calls to nonReentrant after this point will fail
 74 |     |         state.unlocked = _ENTERED;
 75 |     |     }
 76 |     | 
 77 |     |     function _nonReentrantAfter(GlobalState storage state) private {
 78 |     |         if (state.unlocked != _ENTERED) revert ReentrancyGuardInvalidState();
 79 |     |         // By storing the original value once again, a refund is triggered (see
 80 |     |         // https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-2200)
 81 |     |         state.unlocked = _NOT_ENTERED;
 82 |     |     }
 83 |     | 
 84 |     |     /**
 85 |     |      * @dev Returns true if the reentrancy guard is currently set to "entered", which indicates there is a
 86 |     |      * `nonReentrant` function in the call stack.
 87 |     |      */
 88 |     |     function _reentrancyGuardEntered(GlobalState storage state) internal view returns (bool) {
 89 |     |         return state.unlocked == _ENTERED;
 90 |     |     }
 91 |     | }

   9 |     |     /// @dev Reads an immutable arg with type bytes.
  10 |     |     function _getArgBytes(uint256 argOffset, uint256 length)
  11 |     |         internal
  12 |     |         pure
  13 |     |         returns (bytes memory arg)
  14 |     |     {
  15 |     |         uint256 offset = _getImmutableArgsOffset();
  16 |     |         /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
  17 |     |         assembly {
  18 |     |             arg := mload(0x40)
  19 |     |             mstore(arg, length) // Store the length.
  20 |     |             calldatacopy(add(arg, 0x20), add(offset, argOffset), length)
  21 |     |             let o := add(add(arg, 0x20), length)
  22 |     |             mstore(o, 0) // Zeroize the slot after the bytes.
  23 |     |             mstore(0x40, add(o, 0x20)) // Allocate the memory.
  24 |     |         }
  25 |     |     }
