/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/external/solady/LibClone.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | /// @notice Minimal proxy library.
   5 |     | /// @author Solady (https://github.com/vectorized/solady/blob/main/src/utils/LibClone.sol)
   6 |     | /// @author Minimal proxy by 0age (https://github.com/0age)
   7 |     | /// @author Clones with immutable args by wighawag, zefram.eth, Saw-mon & Natalie
   8 |     | /// (https://github.com/Saw-mon-and-Natalie/clones-with-immutable-args)
   9 |     | ///
  10 |     | /// @dev Minimal proxy:
  11 |     | /// Although the sw0nt pattern saves 5 gas over the erc-1167 pattern during runtime,
  12 |     | /// it is not supported out-of-the-box on Etherscan. Hence, we choose to use the 0age pattern,
  13 |     | /// which saves 4 gas over the erc-1167 pattern during runtime, and has the smallest bytecode.
  14 |     | ///
  15 |     | /// @dev Clones with immutable args (CWIA):
  16 |     | /// The implementation of CWIA here implements a `receive()` method that emits the
  17 |     | /// `ReceiveETH(uint256)` event. This skips the `DELEGATECALL` when there is no calldata,
  18 |     | /// enabling us to accept hard gas-capped `sends` & `transfers` for maximum backwards
  19 |     | /// composability. The minimal proxy implementation does not offer this feature.
  20 |     | library LibClone {
  21 |     |     /*´:°•.°+.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°•.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°+.*•´.*:*/
  22 |     |     /*                       CUSTOM ERRORS                        */
  23 |     |     /*.•°:°.´+˚.*°.˚:*.´•*.+°.•°:´*.´•*.•°.•°:°.´:•˚°.*°.˚:*.´+°.•*/
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     /// @dev Unable to deploy the clone.
  26 |     |     error DeploymentFailed();
  27 |     | 
  28 |     |     /// @dev The salt must start with either the zero address or the caller.
  29 |     |     error SaltDoesNotStartWithCaller();
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |     /*´:°•.°+.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°•.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°+.*•´.*:*/
  32 |     |     /*                  MINIMAL PROXY OPERATIONS                  */
  33 |     |     /*.•°:°.´+˚.*°.˚:*.´•*.+°.•°:´*.´•*.•°.•°:°.´:•˚°.*°.˚:*.´+°.•*/
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |     /// @dev Deploys a deterministic clone of `implementation`,
  36 |     |     /// using immutable  arguments encoded in `data`, with `salt`.
  37 |     |     function cloneDeterministic(address implementation, bytes memory data, bytes32 salt)
  38 |     |         internal
  39 |     |         returns (address instance)
  40 |     |     {
  41 |     |         assembly {
  42 |     |             // Compute the boundaries of the data and cache the memory slots around it.
  43 |     |             let mBefore3 := mload(sub(data, 0x60))
  44 |     |             let mBefore2 := mload(sub(data, 0x40))
  45 |     |             let mBefore1 := mload(sub(data, 0x20))
  46 |     |             let dataLength := mload(data)
  47 |     |             let dataEnd := add(add(data, 0x20), dataLength)
  48 |     |             let mAfter1 := mload(dataEnd)
  49 |     | 
  50 |     |             // +2 bytes for telling how much data there is appended to the call.
  51 |     |             let extraLength := add(dataLength, 2)
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |             // Write the bytecode before the data.
  54 |     |             mstore(data, 0x5af43d3d93803e606057fd5bf3)
  55 |     |             // Write the address of the implementation.
  56 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x0d), implementation)
  57 |     |             // Write the rest of the bytecode.
  58 |     |             mstore(
  59 |     |                 sub(data, 0x21),
  60 |     |                 or(shl(0x48, extraLength), 0x593da1005b363d3d373d3d3d3d610000806062363936013d73)
  61 |     |             )
  62 |     |             // `keccak256("ReceiveETH(uint256)")`
  63 |     |             mstore(
  64 |     |                 sub(data, 0x3a), 0x9e4ac34f21c619cefc926c8bd93b54bf5a39c7ab2127a895af1cc0691d7e3dff
  65 |     |             )
  66 |     |             mstore(
  67 |     |                 sub(data, 0x5a),
  68 |     |                 or(shl(0x78, add(extraLength, 0x62)), 0x6100003d81600a3d39f336602c57343d527f)
  69 |     |             )
  70 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, shl(0xf0, extraLength))
  71 |     | 
  72 |     |             // Create the instance.
  73 |     |             instance := create2(0, sub(data, 0x4c), add(extraLength, 0x6c), salt)
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |             // If `instance` is zero, revert.
  76 |     |             if iszero(instance) {
  77 |     |                 // Store the function selector of `DeploymentFailed()`.
  78 |     |                 mstore(0x00, 0x30116425)
  79 |     |                 // Revert with (offset, size).
  80 |     |                 revert(0x1c, 0x04)
  81 |     |             }
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |             // Restore the overwritten memory surrounding `data`.
  84 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, mAfter1)
  85 |     |             mstore(data, dataLength)
  86 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x20), mBefore1)
  87 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x40), mBefore2)
  88 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x60), mBefore3)
  89 |     |         }
  90 |     |     }
  91 |     | 
  92 |     |     /// @dev Returns the initialization code hash of the clone of `implementation`
  93 |     |     /// using immutable arguments encoded in `data`.
  94 |     |     /// Used for mining vanity addresses with create2crunch.
  95 |     |     function initCodeHash(address implementation, bytes memory data)
  96 |     |         internal
  97 |     |         pure
  98 |     |         returns (bytes32 hash)
  99 |     |     {
 100 |     |         assembly {
 101 |     |             // Compute the boundaries of the data and cache the memory slots around it.
 102 |     |             let mBefore3 := mload(sub(data, 0x60))
 103 |     |             let mBefore2 := mload(sub(data, 0x40))
 104 |     |             let mBefore1 := mload(sub(data, 0x20))
 105 |     |             let dataLength := mload(data)
 106 |     |             let dataEnd := add(add(data, 0x20), dataLength)
 107 |     |             let mAfter1 := mload(dataEnd)
 108 |     | 
 109 |     |             // +2 bytes for telling how much data there is appended to the call.
 110 |     |             let extraLength := add(dataLength, 2)
 111 |     | 
 112 |     |             // Write the bytecode before the data.
 113 |     |             mstore(data, 0x5af43d3d93803e606057fd5bf3)
 114 |     |             // Write the address of the implementation.
 115 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x0d), implementation)
 116 |     |             // Write the rest of the bytecode.
 117 |     |             mstore(
 118 |     |                 sub(data, 0x21),
 119 |     |                 or(shl(0x48, extraLength), 0x593da1005b363d3d373d3d3d3d610000806062363936013d73)
 120 |     |             )
 121 |     |             // `keccak256("ReceiveETH(uint256)")`
 122 |     |             mstore(
 123 |     |                 sub(data, 0x3a), 0x9e4ac34f21c619cefc926c8bd93b54bf5a39c7ab2127a895af1cc0691d7e3dff
 124 |     |             )
 125 |     |             mstore(
 126 |     |                 sub(data, 0x5a),
 127 |     |                 or(shl(0x78, add(extraLength, 0x62)), 0x6100003d81600a3d39f336602c57343d527f)
 128 |     |             )
 129 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, shl(0xf0, extraLength))
 130 |     | 
 131 |     |             // Compute and store the bytecode hash.
 132 |     |             hash := keccak256(sub(data, 0x4c), add(extraLength, 0x6c))
 133 |     | 
 134 |     |             // Restore the overwritten memory surrounding `data`.
 135 |     |             mstore(dataEnd, mAfter1)
 136 |     |             mstore(data, dataLength)
 137 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x20), mBefore1)
 138 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x40), mBefore2)
 139 |     |             mstore(sub(data, 0x60), mBefore3)
 140 |     |         }
 141 |     |     }
 142 |     | 
 143 |     |     /// @dev Returns the address of the deterministic clone of
 144 |     |     /// `implementation` using immutable arguments encoded in `data`, with `salt`, by `deployer`.
 145 |     |     function predictDeterministicAddress(
 146 |     |         address implementation,
 147 |     |         bytes memory data,
 148 |     |         bytes32 salt,
 149 |     |         address deployer
 150 |     |     ) internal pure returns (address predicted) {
 151 |     |         bytes32 hash = initCodeHash(implementation, data);
 152 |     |         predicted = predictDeterministicAddress(hash, salt, deployer);
 153 |     |     }
 154 |     | 
 155 |     |     /*´:°•.°+.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°•.*•´.*:˚.°*.˚•´.°:°•.°+.*•´.*:*/
 156 |     |     /*                      OTHER OPERATIONS                      */
 157 |     |     /*.•°:°.´+˚.*°.˚:*.´•*.+°.•°:´*.´•*.•°.•°:°.´:•˚°.*°.˚:*.´+°.•*/
 158 |     | 
 159 |     |     /// @dev Returns the address when a contract with initialization code hash,
 160 |     |     /// `hash`, is deployed with `salt`, by `deployer`.
 161 |     |     function predictDeterministicAddress(bytes32 hash, bytes32 salt, address deployer)
 162 |     |         internal
 163 |     |         pure
 164 |     |         returns (address predicted)
 165 |     |     {
 166 |     |         /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 167 |     |         assembly {
 168 |     |             // Compute and store the bytecode hash.
 169 |     |             mstore8(0x00, 0xff) // Write the prefix.
 170 |     |             mstore(0x35, hash)
 171 |     |             mstore(0x01, shl(96, deployer))
 172 |     |             mstore(0x15, salt)
 173 |     |             predicted := keccak256(0x00, 0x55)
 174 |     |             // Restore the part of the free memory pointer that has been overwritten.
 175 |     |             mstore(0x35, 0)
 176 |     |         }
 177 |     |     }
 178 |     | 
 179 |     |     /// @dev Reverts if `salt` does not start with either the zero address or the caller.
 180 |     |     function checkStartsWithCaller(bytes32 salt) internal view {
 181 |     |         /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 182 |     |         assembly {
 183 |     |             // If the salt does not start with the zero address or the caller.
 184 |     |             if iszero(or(iszero(shr(96, salt)), eq(caller(), shr(96, salt)))) {
 185 |     |                 // Store the function selector of `SaltDoesNotStartWithCaller()`.
 186 |     |                 mstore(0x00, 0x2f634836)
 187 |     |                 // Revert with (offset, size).
 188 |     |                 revert(0x1c, 0x04)
 189 |     |             }
 190 |     |         }
 191 |     |     }
 192 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/Samples.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import './math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   5 |     | import './utils/SafeCast.sol';
   6 |     | import '../interfaces/IPool.sol';
   7 |     | import '../interfaces/range/IRangePool.sol';
   8 |     | import '../interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | library Samples {
  11 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  12 |     | 
  13 |     |     uint8 internal constant TIME_DELTA_MAX = 6;
  14 |     | 
  15 |     |     error InvalidSampleLength();
  16 |     |     error SampleArrayUninitialized();
  17 |     |     error SampleLengthNotAvailable();
  18 |     | 
  19 |     |     event SampleRecorded(
  20 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum,
  21 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
  22 |     |     );
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     event SampleLengthIncreased(
  25 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNext
  26 |     |     );
  27 |     | 
  28 |     |     function initialize(
  29 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  30 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState memory state
  31 |     |     ) internal returns (
  32 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState memory
  33 |     |     )
  34 |     |     {
  35 |     |         samples[0] = PoolsharkStructs.Sample({
  36 |     |             blockTimestamp: uint32(block.timestamp),
  37 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
  38 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0
  39 |     |         });
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |         state.samples.length = 1;
  42 |     |         state.samples.lengthNext = 5;
  43 |     | 
  44 |     |         return state;
  45 |     |         /// @dev - TWAP length of 5 is safer for oracle manipulation
  46 |     |     }
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |     function save(
  49 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  50 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SampleState memory sampleState,
  51 |     |         uint128 startLiquidity, /// @dev - liquidity from start of block
  52 |     |         int24  tick
  53 |     |     ) internal returns (
  54 |     |         uint16 sampleIndexNew,
  55 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNew
  56 |     |     ) {
  57 |     |         // grab the latest sample
  58 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory newSample = samples[sampleState.index];
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         // early return if timestamp has not advanced 2 seconds
  61 |     |         if (newSample.blockTimestamp + 2 > uint32(block.timestamp))
  62 |     |             return (sampleState.index, sampleState.length);
  63 |     | 
  64 |     |         if (sampleState.lengthNext > sampleState.length
  65 |     |             && sampleState.index == (sampleState.length - 1)) {
  66 |     |             // increase sampleLengthNew if old size exceeded
  67 |     |             sampleLengthNew = sampleState.lengthNext;
  68 |     |         } else {
  69 |     |             sampleLengthNew = sampleState.length;
  70 |     |         }
  71 |     |         sampleIndexNew = (sampleState.index + 1) % sampleLengthNew;
  72 |     |         samples[sampleIndexNew] = _build(newSample, uint32(block.timestamp), tick, startLiquidity);
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         emit SampleRecorded(
  75 |     |             samples[sampleIndexNew].tickSecondsAccum,
  76 |     |             samples[sampleIndexNew].secondsPerLiquidityAccum
  77 |     |         );
  78 |     |     }
  79 |     | 
  80 |     |     function expand(
  81 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  82 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangePoolState storage pool,
  83 |     |         uint16 sampleLengthNext
  84 |     |     ) internal {
  85 |     |         if (sampleLengthNext <= pool.samples.lengthNext) return ;
  86 |     |         for (uint16 i = pool.samples.lengthNext; i < sampleLengthNext; i++) {
  87 |     |             samples[i].blockTimestamp = 1;
  88 |     |         }
  89 |     |         pool.samples.lengthNext = sampleLengthNext;
  90 |     |         emit SampleLengthIncreased(sampleLengthNext);
  91 |     |     }
  92 |     | 
  93 |     |     function get(
  94 |     |         address pool,
  95 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params
  96 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  97 |     |         int56[]   memory tickSecondsAccum,
  98 |     |         uint160[] memory secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
  99 |     |         uint160 averagePrice,
 100 |     |         uint128 averageLiquidity,
 101 |     |         int24 averageTick
 102 |     |     ) {
 103 |     |         if (params.sampleLength == 0) require(false, 'InvalidSampleLength()');
 104 |     |         if (params.secondsAgo.length == 0) require(false, 'SecondsAgoArrayEmpty()');
 105 |     |         uint256 size = params.secondsAgo.length > 1 ? params.secondsAgo.length : 2;
 106 |     |         uint32[] memory secondsAgo = new uint32[](size);
 107 |     |         if (params.secondsAgo.length == 1) {
 108 |     |             secondsAgo = new uint32[](2);
 109 |     |             secondsAgo[0] = params.secondsAgo[0];
 110 |     |             secondsAgo[1] = params.secondsAgo[0] + 2;
 111 |     |         }
 112 |     |         else secondsAgo = params.secondsAgo;
 113 |     | 
 114 |     |         if (secondsAgo[0] == secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]) require(false, 'SecondsAgoArrayValuesEqual()');
 115 |     | 
 116 |     |         tickSecondsAccum = new int56[](secondsAgo.length);
 117 |     |         secondsPerLiquidityAccum = new uint160[](secondsAgo.length);
 118 |     | 
 119 |     |         for (uint256 i = 0; i < secondsAgo.length; i++) {
 120 |     |             (
 121 |     |                 tickSecondsAccum[i],
 122 |     |                 secondsPerLiquidityAccum[i]
 123 |     |             ) = getSingle(
 124 |     |                 IPool(pool),
 125 |     |                 params,
 126 |     |                 secondsAgo[i]
 127 |     |             );
 128 |     |         }
 129 |     |         if (secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] > secondsAgo[0]) {
 130 |     |             averageTick = int24((tickSecondsAccum[0] - tickSecondsAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1]) 
 131 |     |                                 / int32(secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsAgo[0]));
 132 |     |             averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, params.constants);
 133 |     |             averageLiquidity = uint128((secondsPerLiquidityAccum[0] - secondsPerLiquidityAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1]) 
 134 |     |                                     * (secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsAgo[0]));
 135 |     |         } else {
 136 |     |             averageTick = int24((tickSecondsAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1] - tickSecondsAccum[0]) 
 137 |     |                                 / int32(secondsAgo[0] - secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]));
 138 |     |             averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, params.constants);
 139 |     |             averageLiquidity = uint128((secondsPerLiquidityAccum[secondsAgo.length - 1] - secondsPerLiquidityAccum[0]) 
 140 |     |                                     * (secondsAgo[0] - secondsAgo[secondsAgo.length - 1]));
 141 |     |         }
 142 |     |     }
 143 |     | 
 144 |     |     function _poolSample(
 145 |     |         IPool pool,
 146 |     |         uint256 sampleIndex
 147 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 148 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 149 |     |     ) {
 150 |     |         (
 151 |     |             uint32 blockTimestamp,
 152 |     |             int56 tickSecondsAccum,
 153 |     |             uint160 liquidityPerSecondsAccum
 154 |     |         ) = pool.samples(sampleIndex);
 155 |     | 
 156 |     |         return PoolsharkStructs.Sample(
 157 |     |             blockTimestamp,
 158 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 159 |     |             liquidityPerSecondsAccum
 160 |     |         );
 161 |     |     }
 162 |     | 
 163 |     |     function getSingle(
 164 |     |         IPool pool,
 165 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params,
 166 |     |         uint32 secondsAgo
 167 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 168 |     |         int56   tickSecondsAccum,
 169 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 170 |     |     ) {
 171 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory latest = _poolSample(pool, params.sampleIndex);
 172 |     | 
 173 |     |         if (secondsAgo == 0) {
 174 |     |             // if 2 seconds have elapsed build new sample
 175 |     |             if (latest.blockTimestamp + 2 <= uint32(block.timestamp)) {
 176 |     |                 latest = _build(
 177 |     |                     latest,
 178 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 179 |     |                     params.tick,
 180 |     |                     params.liquidity
 181 |     |                 );
 182 |     |             }
 183 |     |             // else use latest sample
 184 |     |             return (
 185 |     |                 latest.tickSecondsAccum,
 186 |     |                 latest.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 187 |     |             );
 188 |     |         }
 189 |     | 
 190 |     |         uint32 targetTime = uint32(block.timestamp) - secondsAgo;
 191 |     | 
 192 |     |         // should be getting samples
 193 |     |         (
 194 |     |             RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 195 |     |             RangePoolStructs.Sample memory secondSample
 196 |     |         ) = _getAdjacentSamples(
 197 |     |                 pool,
 198 |     |                 latest,
 199 |     |                 params,
 200 |     |                 targetTime
 201 |     |         );
 202 |     | 
 203 |     |         if (targetTime == firstSample.blockTimestamp) {
 204 |     |             // first sample
 205 |     |             return (
 206 |     |                 firstSample.tickSecondsAccum,
 207 |     |                 firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 208 |     |             );
 209 |     |         } else if (targetTime == secondSample.blockTimestamp) {
 210 |     |             // second sample
 211 |     |             return (
 212 |     |                 secondSample.tickSecondsAccum,
 213 |     |                 secondSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 214 |     |             );
 215 |     |         } else {
 216 |     |             // average two samples
 217 |     |             int32 sampleTimeDelta = int32(secondSample.blockTimestamp - firstSample.blockTimestamp);
 218 |     |             int56 targetDelta = int56(int32(targetTime - firstSample.blockTimestamp));
 219 |     |             return (
 220 |     |                 firstSample.tickSecondsAccum +
 221 |     |                     ((secondSample.tickSecondsAccum - firstSample.tickSecondsAccum) 
 222 |     |                     / sampleTimeDelta)
 223 |     |                     * targetDelta,
 224 |     |                 firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum +
 225 |     |                     uint160(
 226 |     |                         (uint256(
 227 |     |                             secondSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum - firstSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 228 |     |                         ) 
 229 |     |                         * uint256(uint56(targetDelta))) 
 230 |     |                         / uint32(sampleTimeDelta)
 231 |     |                     )
 232 |     |             );
 233 |     |         }
 234 |     |     }
 235 |     | 
 236 |     |     function getLatest(
 237 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 238 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 239 |     |         uint256 liquidity
 240 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 241 |     |         uint160 latestPrice,
 242 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 243 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum
 244 |     |     ) {
 245 |     |         uint32 timeDelta = timeElapsed(constants);
 246 |     |         (
 247 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 248 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 249 |     |         ) = getSingle(
 250 |     |                 IPool(address(this)), 
 251 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 252 |     |                     state.pool.samples.index,
 253 |     |                     state.pool.samples.length,
 254 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 255 |     |                     new uint32[](2),
 256 |     |                     state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 257 |     |                     liquidity.toUint128(),
 258 |     |                     constants
 259 |     |                 ),
 260 |     |                 0
 261 |     |         );
 262 |     |         // grab older sample for dynamic fee calculation
 263 |     |         (
 264 |     |             int56 tickSecondsAccumBase,
 265 |     |         ) = Samples.getSingle(
 266 |     |                 IPool(address(this)), 
 267 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 268 |     |                     state.pool.samples.index,
 269 |     |                     state.pool.samples.length,
 270 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 271 |     |                     new uint32[](2),
 272 |     |                     state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 273 |     |                     liquidity.toUint128(),
 274 |     |                     constants
 275 |     |                 ),
 276 |     |                 timeDelta
 277 |     |         );
 278 |     | 
 279 |     |         latestPrice = calculateLatestPrice(
 280 |     |             tickSecondsAccum,
 281 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase,
 282 |     |             timeDelta,
 283 |     |             TIME_DELTA_MAX,
 284 |     |             constants
 285 |     |         );
 286 |     |     }
 287 |     | 
 288 |     |     function calculateLatestPrice(
 289 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccum,
 290 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccumBase,
 291 |     |         uint32 timeDelta,
 292 |     |         uint32 timeDeltaMax,
 293 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 294 |     |     ) private pure returns (
 295 |     |         uint160 averagePrice
 296 |     |     ) {
 297 |     |         int56 tickSecondsAccumDiff = tickSecondsAccum - tickSecondsAccumBase;
 298 |     |         int24 averageTick;
 299 |     |         if (timeDelta == timeDeltaMax) {
 300 |     |             averageTick = int24(tickSecondsAccumDiff / int32(timeDelta));
 301 |     |         } else {
 302 |     |             averageTick = int24(tickSecondsAccum / int32(timeDelta));
 303 |     |         }
 304 |     |         averagePrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(averageTick, constants);
 305 |     |     }
 306 |     | 
 307 |     | 
 308 |     |     function timeElapsed(
 309 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 310 |     |     ) private view returns (
 311 |     |         uint32
 312 |     |     )    
 313 |     |     {
 314 |     |         return  uint32(block.timestamp) - constants.genesisTime >= TIME_DELTA_MAX
 315 |     |                     ? TIME_DELTA_MAX
 316 |     |                     : uint32(block.timestamp - constants.genesisTime);
 317 |     |     }
 318 |     | 
 319 |     |     function _lte(
 320 |     |         uint32 timeA,
 321 |     |         uint32 timeB
 322 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 323 |     |         uint32 currentTime = uint32(block.timestamp);
 324 |     |         if (timeA <= currentTime && timeB <= currentTime) return timeA <= timeB;
 325 |     | 
 326 |     |         uint256 timeAOverflow = timeA;
 327 |     |         uint256 timeBOverflow = timeB;
 328 |     | 
 329 |     |         if (timeA <= currentTime) {
 330 |     |             timeAOverflow = timeA + 2**32;
 331 |     |         }
 332 |     |         if (timeB <= currentTime) {
 333 |     |             timeBOverflow = timeB + 2**32;
 334 |     |         }
 335 |     | 
 336 |     |         return timeAOverflow <= timeBOverflow;
 337 |     |     }
 338 |     | 
 339 |     |     function _build(
 340 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory newSample,
 341 |     |         uint32  blockTimestamp,
 342 |     |         int24   tick,
 343 |     |         uint128 liquidity
 344 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 345 |     |          RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 346 |     |     ) {
 347 |     |         int56 timeDelta = int56(uint56(blockTimestamp - newSample.blockTimestamp));
 348 |     | 
 349 |     |         return
 350 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.Sample({
 351 |     |                 blockTimestamp: blockTimestamp,
 352 |     |                 tickSecondsAccum: newSample.tickSecondsAccum + int56(tick) * int32(timeDelta),
 353 |     |                 secondsPerLiquidityAccum: newSample.secondsPerLiquidityAccum +
 354 |     |                     ((uint160(uint56(timeDelta)) << 128) / (liquidity > 0 ? liquidity : 1))
 355 |     |             });
 356 |     |     }
 357 |     | 
 358 |     |     function _binarySearch(
 359 |     |         IPool pool,
 360 |     |         uint32 targetTime,
 361 |     |         uint16 sampleIndex,
 362 |     |         uint16 sampleLength
 363 |     |     ) private view returns (
 364 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 365 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory secondSample
 366 |     |     ) {
 367 |     |         uint256 oldIndex = (sampleIndex + 1) % sampleLength;
 368 |     |         uint256 newIndex = oldIndex + sampleLength - 1;             
 369 |     |         uint256 index;
 370 |     |         while (true) {
 371 |     |             // start in the middle
 372 |     |             index = (oldIndex + newIndex) / 2;
 373 |     | 
 374 |     |             // get the first sample
 375 |     |             firstSample = _poolSample(pool, index % sampleLength);
 376 |     | 
 377 |     |             // if sample is uninitialized
 378 |     |             if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == 0) {
 379 |     |                 // skip this index and continue
 380 |     |                 oldIndex = index + 1;
 381 |     |                 continue;
 382 |     |             }
 383 |     |             // else grab second sample
 384 |     |             secondSample = _poolSample(pool, (index + 1) % sampleLength);
 385 |     | 
 386 |     |             // check if target time within first and second sample
 387 |     |             bool targetAfterFirst   = _lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime);
 388 |     |             bool targetBeforeSecond = _lte(targetTime, secondSample.blockTimestamp);
 389 |     |             if (targetAfterFirst && targetBeforeSecond) break;
 390 |     |             if (!targetAfterFirst) newIndex = index - 1;
 391 |     |             else oldIndex = index + 1;
 392 |     |         }
 393 |     |     }
 394 |     | 
 395 |     |     function _getAdjacentSamples(
 396 |     |         IPool pool,
 397 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory firstSample,
 398 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams memory params,
 399 |     |         uint32 targetTime
 400 |     |     ) private view returns (
 401 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory,
 402 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory
 403 |     |     ) {
 404 |     |         if (_lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime)) {
 405 |     |             if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == targetTime) {
 406 |     |                 return (firstSample, PoolsharkStructs.Sample(0,0,0));
 407 |     |             } else {
 408 |     |                 return (firstSample, _build(firstSample, targetTime, params.tick, params.liquidity));
 409 |     |             }
 410 |     |         }
 411 |     |         firstSample = _poolSample(pool, (params.sampleIndex + 1) % params.sampleLength);
 412 |     |         if (firstSample.blockTimestamp == 0) {
 413 |     |             firstSample = _poolSample(pool, 0);
 414 |     |         }
 415 |     |         if(!_lte(firstSample.blockTimestamp, targetTime)) require(false, 'SampleLengthNotAvailable()');
 416 |     | 
 417 |     |         return _binarySearch(
 418 |     |             pool,
 419 |     |             targetTime,
 420 |     |             params.sampleIndex,
 421 |     |             params.sampleLength
 422 |     |         );
 423 |     |     }
 424 |     | }

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;

   4 |     | import './math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   5 |     | import '../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   6 |     | 
   7 |     | library TickMap {
   8 |     | 
   9 |     |     error TickIndexOverflow();
  10 |     |     error TickIndexUnderflow();
  11 |     |     error TickIndexBadSpacing();
  12 |     |     error BlockIndexOverflow();
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function get(
  15 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  16 |     |         int24 tick,
  17 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  18 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  19 |     |         bool exists
  20 |     |     ) {
  21 |     |         (
  22 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  23 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  24 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  25 |     | 
  26 |     |         // check if bit is already set
  27 |     |         uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] | 1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF);
  28 |     |         if (word == tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]) {
  29 |     |             return true;
  30 |     |         }
  31 |     |         return false;
  32 |     |     }
  33 |     | 
  34 |     |     function set(
  35 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  36 |     |         int24 tick,
  37 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  38 |     |     ) internal returns (
  39 |     |         bool exists
  40 |     |     ) {
  41 |     |         (
  42 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  43 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  44 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
  45 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |         // check if bit is already set
  48 |     |         uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] | 1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF);
  49 |     |         if (word == tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]) {
  50 |     |             return true;
  51 |     |         }
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |         tickMap.ticks[wordIndex]     = word; 
  54 |     |         tickMap.words[blockIndex]   |= 1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF); // same as modulus 255
  55 |     |         tickMap.blocks              |= 1 << blockIndex;
  56 |     |         return false;
  57 |     |     }
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |     function unset(
  60 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  61 |     |         int24 tick,
  62 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
  63 |     |     ) internal {
  64 |     |         (
  65 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  66 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  67 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
  68 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
  69 |     | 
  70 |     |         tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] &= ~(1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF));
  71 |     |         if (tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] == 0) {
  72 |     |             tickMap.words[blockIndex] &= ~(1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF));
  73 |     |             if (tickMap.words[blockIndex] == 0) {
  74 |     |                 tickMap.blocks &= ~(1 << blockIndex);
  75 |     |             }
  76 |     |         }
  77 |     |     }
  78 |     | 
  79 |     |     function previous(
  80 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  81 |     |         int24 tick,
  82 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
  83 |     |         bool inclusive
  84 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  85 |     |         int24 previousTick
  86 |     |     ) {
  87 |     |         unchecked {
  88 |     |             // rounds up to ensure relative position
  89 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0 || inclusive) {
  90 |     |                 if (tick < (ConstantProduct.maxTick(tickSpacing) - tickSpacing / 2)) {
  91 |     |                     /// @dev - ensures we cross when tick >= 0
  92 |     |                     if (tick >= 0) {
  93 |     |                         tick += tickSpacing / 2;
  94 |     |                     } else if (inclusive && tick % (tickSpacing / 2) == 0) {
  95 |     |                     /// @dev - ensures we cross when tick == tickAtPrice
  96 |     |                         tick += tickSpacing / 2;
  97 |     |                     }
  98 |     |                 }
  99 |     |             }
 100 |     |             (
 101 |     |               uint256 tickIndex,
 102 |     |               uint256 wordIndex,
 103 |     |               uint256 blockIndex
 104 |     |             ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
 105 |     | 
 106 |     |             uint256 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] & ((1 << (tickIndex & 0xFF)) - 1);
 107 |     |             if (word == 0) {
 108 |     |                 uint256 block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex] & ((1 << (wordIndex & 0xFF)) - 1);
 109 |     |                 if (block_ == 0) {
 110 |     |                     uint256 blockMap = tickMap.blocks & ((1 << blockIndex) - 1);
 111 |     |                     if (blockMap == 0) return tick;
 112 |     | 
 113 |     |                     blockIndex = _msb(blockMap);
 114 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex];
 115 |     |                 }
 116 |     |                 wordIndex = (blockIndex << 8) | _msb(block_);
 117 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex];
 118 |     |             }
 119 |     |             previousTick = _tick((wordIndex << 8) | _msb(word), tickSpacing);
 120 |     |         }
 121 |     |     }
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |     function next(
 124 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 125 |     |         int24 tick,
 126 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
 127 |     |         bool inclusive
 128 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 129 |     |         int24 nextTick
 130 |     |     ) {
 131 |     |         unchecked {
 132 |     |             /// @dev - handles tickAtPrice being past tickSpacing / 2
 133 |     |             if (inclusive && tick % tickSpacing != 0) {
 134 |     |                 // e.g. tick is 5 we subtract 1 to look ahead at 5
 135 |     |                 if (tick > 0 && (tick % tickSpacing <= (tickSpacing / 2)))
 136 |     |                     tick -= 1;
 137 |     |                 // e.g. tick is -5 we subtract 1 to look ahead at -5
 138 |     |                 else if (tick < 0 && (tick % tickSpacing <= -(tickSpacing / 2)))
 139 |     |                     tick -= 1;
 140 |     |                 // e.g. tick = 7 and tickSpacing = 10 we sub 5 to look ahead at 5
 141 |     |                 // e.g. tick = -2 and tickSpacing = 10 we sub 5 to look ahead at -5
 142 |     |                 else
 143 |     |                     tick -= tickSpacing / 2;
 144 |     |             }
 145 |     |             /// @dev - handles negative ticks rounding up
 146 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0) {
 147 |     |                 if (tick < 0)
 148 |     |                     if (tick > (ConstantProduct.minTick(tickSpacing) + tickSpacing / 2))
 149 |     |                         tick -= tickSpacing / 2;
 150 |     |             }
 151 |     |             (
 152 |     |               uint256 tickIndex,
 153 |     |               uint256 wordIndex,
 154 |     |               uint256 blockIndex
 155 |     |             ) = getIndices(tick, tickSpacing);
 156 |     |             uint256 word;
 157 |     |             if ((tickIndex & 0xFF) != 255) {
 158 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex] & ~((1 << ((tickIndex & 0xFF) + 1)) - 1);
 159 |     |             }
 160 |     |             if (word == 0) {
 161 |     |                 uint256 block_;
 162 |     |                 if ((blockIndex & 0xFF) != 255) {
 163 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex] & ~((1 << ((wordIndex & 0xFF) + 1)) - 1);
 164 |     |                 }
 165 |     |                 if (block_ == 0) {
 166 |     |                     uint256 blockMap = tickMap.blocks & ~((1 << blockIndex + 1) - 1);
 167 |     |                     if (blockMap == 0) return tick;
 168 |     |                     blockIndex = _lsb(blockMap);
 169 |     |                     block_ = tickMap.words[blockIndex];
 170 |     |                 }
 171 |     |                 wordIndex = (blockIndex << 8) | _lsb(block_);
 172 |     |                 word = tickMap.ticks[wordIndex];
 173 |     |             }
 174 |     |             nextTick = _tick((wordIndex << 8) | _lsb(word), tickSpacing);
 175 |     |         }
 176 |     |     }
 177 |     | 
 178 |     |     function getIndices(
 179 |     |         int24 tick,
 180 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 181 |     |     ) public pure returns (
 182 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
 183 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
 184 |     |             uint256 blockIndex
 185 |     |         )
 186 |     |     {
 187 |     |         unchecked {
 188 |     |             if (tick > ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK) require(false, ' TickIndexOverflow()');
 189 |     |             if (tick < ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK) require(false, 'TickIndexUnderflow()');
 190 |     |             if (tick % (tickSpacing / 2) != 0) tick = round(tick, tickSpacing / 2);
 191 |     |             tickIndex = uint256(int256((round(tick, tickSpacing / 2) 
 192 |     |                                         - round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, tickSpacing / 2)) 
 193 |     |                                         / (tickSpacing / 2)));
 194 |     |             wordIndex = tickIndex >> 8;   // 2^8 ticks per word
 195 |     |             blockIndex = tickIndex >> 16; // 2^8 words per block
 196 |     |             if (blockIndex > 255) require(false, 'BlockIndexOverflow()');
 197 |     |         }
 198 |     |     }
 199 |     | 
 200 |     | 
 201 |     | 
 202 |     |     function _tick (
 203 |     |         uint256 tickIndex,
 204 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 205 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 206 |     |         int24 tick
 207 |     |     ) {
 208 |     |         unchecked {
 209 |     |             if (tickIndex > uint24(round(ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK, tickSpacing) * 2) * 2) 
 210 |     |                 require(false, 'TickIndexOverflow()');
 211 |     |             tick = int24(int256(tickIndex) * (tickSpacing / 2) + round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, tickSpacing / 2));
 212 |     |         }
 213 |     |     }
 214 |     | 
 215 |     |     function _msb(
 216 |     |         uint256 x
 217 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 218 |     |         uint8 r
 219 |     |     ) {
 220 |     |         unchecked {
 221 |     |             assert(x > 0);
 222 |     |             if (x >= 0x100000000000000000000000000000000) {
 223 |     |                 x >>= 128;
 224 |     |                 r += 128;
 225 |     |             }
 226 |     |             if (x >= 0x10000000000000000) {
 227 |     |                 x >>= 64;
 228 |     |                 r += 64;
 229 |     |             }
 230 |     |             if (x >= 0x100000000) {
 231 |     |                 x >>= 32;
 232 |     |                 r += 32;
 233 |     |             }
 234 |     |             if (x >= 0x10000) {
 235 |     |                 x >>= 16;
 236 |     |                 r += 16;
 237 |     |             }
 238 |     |             if (x >= 0x100) {
 239 |     |                 x >>= 8;
 240 |     |                 r += 8;
 241 |     |             }
 242 |     |             if (x >= 0x10) {
 243 |     |                 x >>= 4;
 244 |     |                 r += 4;
 245 |     |             }
 246 |     |             if (x >= 0x4) {
 247 |     |                 x >>= 2;
 248 |     |                 r += 2;
 249 |     |             }
 250 |     |             if (x >= 0x2) r += 1;
 251 |     |         }
 252 |     |     }
 253 |     | 
 254 |     |     function _lsb(
 255 |     |         uint256 x
 256 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 257 |     |         uint8 r
 258 |     |     ) {
 259 |     |         unchecked {
 260 |     |             assert(x > 0); // if x is 0 return 0
 261 |     |             r = 255;
 262 |     |             if (x & type(uint128).max > 0) {
 263 |     |                 r -= 128;
 264 |     |             } else {
 265 |     |                 x >>= 128;
 266 |     |             }
 267 |     |             if (x & type(uint64).max > 0) {
 268 |     |                 r -= 64;
 269 |     |             } else {
 270 |     |                 x >>= 64;
 271 |     |             }
 272 |     |             if (x & type(uint32).max > 0) {
 273 |     |                 r -= 32;
 274 |     |             } else {
 275 |     |                 x >>= 32;
 276 |     |             }
 277 |     |             if (x & type(uint16).max > 0) {
 278 |     |                 r -= 16;
 279 |     |             } else {
 280 |     |                 x >>= 16;
 281 |     |             }
 282 |     |             if (x & type(uint8).max > 0) {
 283 |     |                 r -= 8;
 284 |     |             } else {
 285 |     |                 x >>= 8;
 286 |     |             }
 287 |     |             if (x & 0xf > 0) {
 288 |     |                 r -= 4;
 289 |     |             } else {
 290 |     |                 x >>= 4;
 291 |     |             }
 292 |     |             if (x & 0x3 > 0) {
 293 |     |                 r -= 2;
 294 |     |             } else {
 295 |     |                 x >>= 2;
 296 |     |             }
 297 |     |             if (x & 0x1 > 0) r -= 1;
 298 |     |         }
 299 |     |     }
 300 |     | 
 301 |     |     function round(
 302 |     |         int24 tick,
 303 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
 304 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 305 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 306 |     |     ) {
 307 |     |         return tick / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
 308 |     |     }
 309 |     | 
 310 |     |     function roundHalf(
 311 |     |         int24 tick,
 312 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 313 |     |         uint256 price
 314 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 315 |     |         int24 roundedTick,
 316 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice
 317 |     |     ) {
 318 |     |         //pool.tickAtPrice -99.5
 319 |     |         //pool.tickAtPrice -100
 320 |     |         //-105
 321 |     |         //-95
 322 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 323 |     |         roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 324 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 325 |     |             return (roundedTick, roundedTickPrice);
 326 |     |         if (roundedTick > 0) {
 327 |     |             roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 328 |     |         } else if (roundedTick < 0) {
 329 |     |             if (roundedTickPrice < price)
 330 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 331 |     |             else
 332 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 333 |     |         } else {
 334 |     |             if (price > roundedTickPrice) {
 335 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 336 |     |             } else if (price < roundedTickPrice) {
 337 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 338 |     |             }
 339 |     |         }
 340 |     |     }
 341 |     | 
 342 |     |     function roundAhead(
 343 |     |         int24 tick,
 344 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 345 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 346 |     |         uint256 price
 347 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 348 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 349 |     |     ) {
 350 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 351 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 352 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 353 |     |             return roundedTick;
 354 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 355 |     |             // round up if positive
 356 |     |             if (roundedTick > 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick >= 0))
 357 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 358 |     |             else if (tick % constants.tickSpacing == 0) {
 359 |     |                 // handle price at -99.5 and tickAtPrice == -100
 360 |     |                 if (tick < 0 && roundedTickPrice < price) {
 361 |     |                     roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 362 |     |                 }
 363 |     |             }
 364 |     |         } else {
 365 |     |             // round down if negative
 366 |     |             if (roundedTick < 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick < 0))
 367 |     |             /// @dev - strictly less due to TickMath always rounding to lesser values
 368 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing;
 369 |     |         }
 370 |     |     }
 371 |     | 
 372 |     |     function roundBack(
 373 |     |         int24 tick,
 374 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 375 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 376 |     |         uint256 price
 377 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 378 |     |         int24 roundedTick
 379 |     |     ) {
 380 |     |         roundedTick = tick / constants.tickSpacing * constants.tickSpacing;
 381 |     |         uint160 roundedTickPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(roundedTick, constants);
 382 |     |         if (price == roundedTickPrice)
 383 |     |             return roundedTick;
 384 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 385 |     |             // round down if negative
 386 |     |             if (roundedTick < 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick < 0))
 387 |     |                 roundedTick -= constants.tickSpacing;
 388 |     |         } else {
 389 |     |             // round up if positive
 390 |     |             if (roundedTick > 0 || (roundedTick == 0 && tick >= 0))
 391 |     |                 roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 392 |     |             else if (tick % constants.tickSpacing == 0) {
 393 |     |                 // handle price at -99.5 and tickAtPrice == -100
 394 |     |                 if (tick < 0 && roundedTickPrice < price) {
 395 |     |                     roundedTick += constants.tickSpacing;
 396 |     |                 }
 397 |     |             }
 398 |     |         }
 399 |     |     }
