  53 |     |         uint128 feeAmount,
  54 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice,
  55 |     |         bool indexed zeroForOne,
  56 |     |         bool indexed exactIn
  57 |     |     );
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |     event SyncRangeTick(
  60 |     |         uint200 feeGrowthOutside0,
  61 |     |         uint200 feeGrowthOutside1,
  62 |     |         int24 tick
  63 |     |     );
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |     function initialize(
  66 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  67 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  68 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  69 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
  70 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
  71 |     |         uint160 startPrice
  72 |     |     ) internal returns (
  73 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory  
  74 |     |     )
  75 |     |     {
  76 |     |         // state should only be initialized once
  77 |     |         if (state.pool0.price > 0) require (false, 'PoolAlreadyInitialized()');
  78 |     | 
  79 |     |         // initialize state
  80 |     |         state.epoch = 1;
  81 |     |         state.positionIdNext = 1;
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |         // check price bounds
  84 |     |         if (startPrice < constants.bounds.min || startPrice >= constants.bounds.max) require(false, 'StartPriceInvalid()');
  85 |     | 
  86 |     |         // initialize range ticks
  87 |     |         TickMap.set(rangeTickMap, ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  88 |     |         TickMap.set(rangeTickMap, ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  89 |     |         
  90 |     |         // initialize limit ticks
  91 |     |         TickMap.set(limitTickMap, ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  92 |     |         TickMap.set(limitTickMap, ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing), constants.tickSpacing);
  93 |     | 
  94 |     |         // initialize price
  95 |     |         state.pool.price = startPrice;
  96 |     |         state.pool0.price = startPrice;
  97 |     |         state.pool1.price = startPrice;
  98 |     | 
  99 |     |         int24 startTick = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(startPrice, constants);
 100 |     |         state.pool.tickAtPrice = startTick;
 101 |     |         state.pool0.tickAtPrice = startTick;
 102 |     |         state.pool1.tickAtPrice = startTick;
 103 |     | 
 104 |     |         // intialize samples
 105 |     |         state.pool = Samples.initialize(samples, state.pool);
 106 |     | 
 107 |     |         // emit event
 108 |     |         emit Initialize(
 109 |     |             ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing),
 110 |     |             ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing),
 111 |     |             state.pool0.price,
 112 |     |             state.pool0.tickAtPrice
 113 |     |         );
 114 |     | 
 115 |     |         return state;
 116 |     |     }
 117 |     |     
 118 |     |     function swap(
 119 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 120 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
 121 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 122 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 123 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params,
 124 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
 125 |     |     ) internal returns (
 126 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 127 |     |     )
 128 |     |     {   
 129 |     |         // if price == priceAtTick
 130 |     |         // cross range tick if present
 131 |     |         // in _cross if price == priceAtTick && amountLeft == 0
 132 |     |         // don't cross the range tick
 133 |     |         // start with range price
 134 |     |         cache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 135 |     |         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 136 |     | 
 137 |     |         cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, true);
 138 |     | 
 139 |     |         uint128 startLiquidity = cache.liquidity.toUint128();
 140 |     | 
 141 |     |         // set crossTick/crossPrice based on the best between limit and range
 142 |     |         // grab sample for accumulators
 143 |     |         cache = PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache({
 144 |     |             state: cache.state,
 145 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 146 |     |             price: cache.price,
 147 |     |             liquidity: cache.liquidity,
 148 |     |             amountLeft: params.amount,
 149 |     |             input:  0,
 150 |     |             output: 0,
 151 |     |             crossPrice: cache.crossPrice,
 152 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0,
 153 |     |             feeAmount: 0,
 154 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
 155 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase: 0,
 156 |     |             crossTick: cache.crossTick,
 157 |     |             crossStatus: cache.crossStatus,
 158 |     |             limitActive: cache.limitActive,
 159 |     |             exactIn: params.exactIn,
 160 |     |             cross: true,
 161 |     |             averagePrice: 0
 162 |     |         });
 163 |     |         // grab latest price and sample
 164 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample memory latest = Samples._poolSample(IPool(address(this)), cache.state.pool.samples.index);
 165 |     |         if (latest.blockTimestamp + 2 <= uint32(block.timestamp)) {
 166 |     |                 latest = Samples._build(
 167 |     |                     latest,
 168 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 169 |     |                     cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 170 |     |                     cache.liquidity.toUint128()
 171 |     |                 );
 172 |     |                 emit BuildNewSample(
 173 |     |                     latest.blockTimestamp,
 174 |     |                     latest.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 175 |     |                 );
 176 |     |             } else {
 177 |     |                 emit UseOldSample(
 178 |     |                     latest.blockTimestamp,
 179 |     |                     latest.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 180 |     |                 );
 181 |     |             }
 182 |     |         (
 183 |     |             cache.averagePrice,
 184 |     |             cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 185 |     |             cache.tickSecondsAccum
 186 |     |          ) = Samples.getLatest(cache.state, cache.constants, cache.state.pool.liquidity);
 187 |     | 
 188 |     |         // grab latest sample and store in cache for _cross
 189 |     |         while (cache.cross) {
 190 |     |             // handle price being at cross tick
 191 |     |             cache = _quoteSingle(cache, params.priceLimit, params.zeroForOne);
 192 |     |             if (cache.cross) {
 193 |     |                 cache = _cross(
 194 |     |                     ticks,
 195 |     |                     rangeTickMap,
 196 |     |                     limitTickMap,
 197 |     |                     cache,
 198 |     |                     params
 199 |     |                 );
 200 |     |             }
 201 |     |         }
 202 |     |         /// @dev - write oracle entry after start of block
 203 |     |         (
 204 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples.index,
 205 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples.length
 206 |     |         ) = Samples.save(
 207 |     |             samples,
 208 |     |             cache.state.pool.samples,
 209 |     |             startLiquidity,
 210 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice
 211 |     |         );
 212 |     |         // pool liquidity should be updated along the way
 213 |     |         cache.state.pool.price = cache.price.toUint160();
 214 |     | 
 215 |     |         if (cache.price != cache.crossPrice) {
 216 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(cache.price.toUint160(), cache.constants);
 217 |     |         } else {
 218 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice = cache.crossTick;
 219 |     |         }
 220 |     |         if (cache.limitActive) {
 221 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 222 |     |                 cache.state.pool1.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 223 |     |                 cache.state.pool1.tickAtPrice = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 224 |     |             } else {
 225 |     |                 cache.state.pool0.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 226 |     |                 cache.state.pool0.tickAtPrice = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 227 |     |             }
 228 |     |         }
 229 |     |         emit Swap(
 230 |     |             params.to,
 231 |     |             cache.input,
 232 |     |             cache.output,
 233 |     |             cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
 234 |     |             cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
 235 |     |             cache.price.toUint160(),
 236 |     |             cache.liquidity.toUint128(),
 237 |     |             cache.feeAmount,
 238 |     |             cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 239 |     |             params.zeroForOne,
 240 |     |             params.exactIn
 241 |     |         );
 242 |     |         return cache;
 243 |     |     }
 244 |     | 
 245 |     |     function quote(
 246 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 247 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 248 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 249 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.QuoteParams memory params,
 250 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
 251 |     |     ) internal returns (
 252 |     |         uint256,
 253 |     |         uint256,
 254 |     |         uint160
 255 |     |     ) {
 256 |     |         // start with range price
 257 |     |         cache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
 258 |     |         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 259 |     | 
 260 |     |         cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, true);
 261 |     |         
 262 |     |         // set crossTick/crossPrice based on the best between limit and range
 263 |     |         // grab sample for accumulators
 264 |     |         cache = PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache({
 265 |     |             state: cache.state,
 266 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 267 |     |             price: cache.price,
 268 |     |             liquidity: cache.liquidity,
 269 |     |             amountLeft: params.amount,
 270 |     |             input:  0,
 271 |     |             output: 0,
 272 |     |             crossPrice: cache.crossPrice,
 273 |     |             secondsPerLiquidityAccum: 0,
 274 |     |             feeAmount: 0,
 275 |     |             tickSecondsAccum: 0,
 276 |     |             tickSecondsAccumBase: 0,
 277 |     |             crossTick: cache.crossTick,
 278 |     |             crossStatus: cache.crossStatus,
 279 |     |             limitActive: cache.limitActive,
 280 |     |             exactIn: params.exactIn,
 281 |     |             cross: true,
 282 |     |             averagePrice: 0
 283 |     |         });
 284 |     |         // grab latest price and sample
 285 |     |         (
 286 |     |             cache.averagePrice,
 287 |     |             cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 288 |     |             cache.tickSecondsAccum
 289 |     |          ) = Samples.getLatest(cache.state, cache.constants, cache.liquidity);
 290 |     |         while (cache.cross) {
 291 |     |             cache = _quoteSingle(cache, params.priceLimit, params.zeroForOne);
 292 |     |             if (cache.cross) {
 293 |     |                 cache = _pass(
 294 |     |                     ticks,
 295 |     |                     rangeTickMap,
 296 |     |                     limitTickMap,
 297 |     |                     cache,
 298 |     |                     params
 299 |     |                 );
 300 |     |             }
 301 |     |         }
 302 |     |         return (
 303 |     |             cache.input,
 304 |     |             cache.output,
 305 |     |             cache.price.toUint160()
 306 |     |         );
 307 |     |     }
 308 |     | 
 309 |     |     function _quoteSingle(
 310 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 311 |     |         uint160 priceLimit,
 312 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 313 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 314 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 315 |     |     ) {
 316 |     |         if ((zeroForOne ? priceLimit >= cache.price
 317 |     |                         : priceLimit <= cache.price) ||
 318 |     |             (zeroForOne && cache.price == cache.constants.bounds.min) ||
 319 |     |             (!zeroForOne && cache.price == cache.constants.bounds.max) ||
 320 |     |             (cache.amountLeft == 0 && cache.liquidity > 0))
 321 |     |         {
 322 |     |             cache.cross = false;
 323 |     |             return cache;
 324 |     |         }
 325 |     |         uint256 nextPrice = cache.crossPrice;
 326 |     |          uint256 amountIn; uint256 amountOut;
 327 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 328 |     |             // Trading token 0 (x) for token 1 (y).
 329 |     |             // price  is decreasing.
 330 |     |             if (nextPrice < priceLimit) {
 331 |     |                 nextPrice = priceLimit;
 332 |     |             }
 333 |     |             uint256 amountMax = cache.exactIn ? ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, true)
 334 |     |                                               : ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, false);
 335 |     |             if (cache.amountLeft < amountMax) {
 336 |     |                 // calculate price after swap
 337 |     |                 uint256 newPrice = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(
 338 |     |                     cache.price,
 339 |     |                     cache.liquidity,
 340 |     |                     cache.amountLeft,
 341 |     |                     zeroForOne,
 342 |     |                     cache.exactIn
 343 |     |                 );
 344 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 345 |     |                     amountIn = cache.amountLeft;
 346 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, newPrice, uint256(cache.price), false);
 347 |     |                 } else {
 348 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, newPrice, uint256(cache.price), true);
 349 |     |                     amountOut = cache.amountLeft;
 350 |     |                 }
 351 |     |                 cache.amountLeft = 0;
 352 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 353 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(newPrice);
 354 |     |             } else {
 355 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 356 |     |                     amountIn = amountMax;
 357 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, false);
 358 |     | 
 359 |     |                 } else {
 360 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, nextPrice, cache.price, true);
 361 |     |                     amountOut = amountMax;
 362 |     |                 }
 363 |     |                 cache.amountLeft -= amountMax;
 364 |     |                 if (nextPrice == cache.crossPrice) cache.cross = true;
 365 |     |                 else cache.cross = false;
 366 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(nextPrice);
 367 |     |             }
 368 |     |         } else {
 369 |     |             // Price is increasing.
 370 |     |             if (nextPrice > priceLimit) {
 371 |     |                 nextPrice = priceLimit;
 372 |     |             }
 373 |     |             uint256 amountMax = cache.exactIn ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, uint256(cache.price), nextPrice, true)
 374 |     |                                               : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, uint256(cache.price), nextPrice, false);
 375 |     |             if (cache.amountLeft < amountMax) {
 376 |     |                 uint256 newPrice = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(
 377 |     |                     cache.price,
 378 |     |                     cache.liquidity,
 379 |     |                     cache.amountLeft,
 380 |     |                     zeroForOne,
 381 |     |                     cache.exactIn
 382 |     |                 );
 383 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 384 |     |                     amountIn = cache.amountLeft;
 385 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, cache.price, newPrice, false);
 386 |     |                 } else {
 387 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, cache.price, newPrice, true);
 388 |     |                     amountOut = cache.amountLeft;
 389 |     |                 }
 390 |     |                 cache.amountLeft = 0;
 391 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 392 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(newPrice);
 393 |     |             } else {
 394 |     |                 if (cache.exactIn) {
 395 |     |                     amountIn = amountMax;
 396 |     |                     amountOut = ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidity, cache.price, nextPrice, false);
 397 |     |                 } else {
 398 |     |                     amountIn = ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidity, cache.price, nextPrice, true);
 399 |     |                     amountOut = amountMax;
 400 |     |                 }
 401 |     |                 cache.amountLeft -= amountMax;
 402 |     |                 if (nextPrice == cache.crossPrice) cache.cross = true;
 403 |     |                 else cache.cross = false;
 404 |     |                 cache.price = uint160(nextPrice);
 405 |     |             }
 406 |     |         }
 407 |     |         cache = FeeMath.calculate(cache, amountIn, amountOut, zeroForOne);
 408 |     |         return cache;
 409 |     |     }
 410 |     | 
 411 |     |     function _cross(
 412 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 413 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 414 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 415 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 416 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params
 417 |     |     ) internal returns (
 418 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 419 |     |     ) {
 420 |     | 
 421 |     |         // crossing range ticks
 422 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & RANGE_TICK) > 0) {
 423 |     |             if (!params.zeroForOne || (cache.amountLeft > 0 && params.priceLimit < cache.crossPrice)) {
 424 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory crossTick = ticks[cache.crossTick].range;
 425 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertFeeGrowthOutsideUnderflows(cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0, crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0);
 426 |     |                 crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0       = cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0 - crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 427 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertFeeGrowthOutsideUnderflows(cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1, crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1);
 428 |     |                 crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1       = cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1 - crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 429 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertTickSecondsAccumWithinBounds(cache.tickSecondsAccum, crossTick.tickSecondsAccumOutside);
 430 |     |                 crossTick.tickSecondsAccumOutside = cache.tickSecondsAccum - crossTick.tickSecondsAccumOutside;
 431 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertSecondsPerLiquidityAccumUnderflows(cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum, crossTick.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside, cache.crossTick);
 432 |     |                 crossTick.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside = cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum - crossTick.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside;
 433 |     |                 ticks[cache.crossTick].range = crossTick;
 434 |     |                 int128 liquidityDelta = crossTick.liquidityDelta;
 435 |     |                 emit SyncRangeTick(
 436 |     |                     crossTick.feeGrowthOutside0,
 437 |     |                     crossTick.feeGrowthOutside1,
 438 |     |                     cache.crossTick
 439 |     |                 );
 440 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 441 |     |                     unchecked {
 442 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0){
 443 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-1");
 444 |     |                             // removing liquidity
 445 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(liquidityDelta);
 446 |     |                         } else {
 447 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-2");
 448 |     |                             // adding liquidity
 449 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(-liquidityDelta); 
 450 |     |                         }
 451 |     |                     }
 452 |     |                 } else {
 453 |     |                     unchecked {
 454 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 455 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-3");
 456 |     |                             // adding liquidity
 457 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 458 |     |                         } else {
 459 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-4");
 460 |     |                             // removing liquidity
 461 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 462 |     |                         }
 463 |     |                     }
 464 |     |                 }
 465 |     |             } else {
 466 |     |                 // if zeroForOne && amountLeft == 0 skip crossing the tick
 467 |     |                 /// @dev - this is so users can safely add liquidity with lower or upper at the pool price 
 468 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 469 |     |             }
 470 |     |             /// @dev - price and tickAtPrice updated at end of loop
 471 |     |         }
 472 |     |         // crossing limit tick
 473 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_TICK) > 0) {
 474 |     |             // cross limit tick
 475 |     |             EpochMap.set(cache.crossTick, !params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, limitTickMap, cache.constants);
 476 |     |             int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.liquidityDelta;
 477 |     | 
 478 |     |             if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 479 |     |                 cache.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 480 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool1.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 481 |     |                 else cache.state.pool0.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 482 |     |             }
 483 |     |             else {
 484 |     |                 cache.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 485 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool1.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 486 |     |                 else cache.state.pool0.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 487 |     |             }
 488 |     |             // zero out liquidityDelta and priceAt
 489 |     |             ticks[cache.crossTick].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 490 |     |             LimitTicks.clear(ticks, cache.constants, limitTickMap, cache.crossTick);
 491 |     |             /// @dev - price and tickAtPrice updated at end of loop
 492 |     |         }
 493 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_POOL) > 0) {
 494 |     |             // add limit pool
 495 |     |             uint128 liquidityDelta = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool1.liquidity
 496 |     |                                                     : cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 497 |     | 
 498 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) cache.liquidity += liquidityDelta;
 499 |     |         }
 500 |     |         if (cache.cross)
 501 |     |             cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, false);
 502 |     | 
 503 |     |         return cache;
 504 |     |     }
 505 |     | 
 506 |     |     function _pass(
 507 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 508 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 509 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 510 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 511 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.QuoteParams memory params
 512 |     |     ) internal returns (
 513 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
 514 |     |     ) {
 515 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & RANGE_TICK) > 0) {
 516 |     |             if (!params.zeroForOne || cache.amountLeft > 0) {
 517 |     |                 int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].range.liquidityDelta;
 518 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 519 |     |                     unchecked {
 520 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0){
 521 |     |                             // start of position boundary
 522 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-1");
 523 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(liquidityDelta);
 524 |     |                         } else {
 525 |     |                             // end of position boundary
 526 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-2");
 527 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(-liquidityDelta); 
 528 |     |                         }
 529 |     |                     }
 530 |     |                 } else {
 531 |     |                     unchecked {
 532 |     |                         if (liquidityDelta >= 0) {
 533 |     |                             // start of position boundary
 534 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-3");
 535 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 536 |     |                         } else {
 537 |     |                             // end of position boundary
 538 |     |                             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-4");
 539 |     |                             cache.state.pool.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 540 |     |                         }
 541 |     |                     }
 542 |     |                 }
 543 |     |             } else {
 544 |     |                 cache.cross = false;
 545 |     |             }
 546 |     |         }
 547 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_TICK) > 0) {
 548 |     |             // cross limit tick
 549 |     |             int128 liquidityDelta = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.liquidityDelta;
 550 |     | 
 551 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) {
 552 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 553 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool1.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-5");
 554 |     |                     cache.state.pool1.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 555 |     |                 } else {
 556 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityOverflows(cache.state.pool0.liquidity, uint128(liquidityDelta), "TKS-6");
 557 |     |                     cache.state.pool0.liquidity += uint128(liquidityDelta);
 558 |     |                 }
 559 |     |             } 
 560 |     |             else {
 561 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 562 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool1.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-7");
 563 |     |                     cache.state.pool1.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 564 |     |                 } else {
 565 |     |                     EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.state.pool0.liquidity, uint128(-liquidityDelta), "TKS-8");
 566 |     |                     cache.state.pool0.liquidity -= uint128(-liquidityDelta);
 567 |     |                 }
 568 |     |             }
 569 |     |         }
 570 |     |         if ((cache.crossStatus & LIMIT_POOL) > 0) {
 571 |     |             // add limit pool
 572 |     |             uint128 liquidityDelta = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool1.liquidity
 573 |     |                                                     : cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 574 |     | 
 575 |     |             if (liquidityDelta > 0) {
 576 |     |                 cache.liquidity += liquidityDelta;
 577 |     |             }
 578 |     |         }
 579 |     | 
 580 |     |         if (cache.cross)
 581 |     |             cache = _iterate(ticks, rangeTickMap, limitTickMap, cache, params.zeroForOne, false);
 582 |     | 
 583 |     |         return cache;
 584 |     |     }
 585 |     | 
 586 |     |     function _iterate(
 587 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 588 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
 589 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
 590 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
 591 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 592 |     |         bool inclusive
 593 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 594 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory 
 595 |     |     )    
 596 |     |     {
 597 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 598 |     |             if (cache.price > cache.state.pool1.price) {
 599 |     |                 // load range pool
 600 |     |                 cache.limitActive = false;
 601 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity;
 602 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 603 |     |                 // next range tick vs. limit pool price
 604 |     |                 cache.crossTick = TickMap.previous(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 605 |     |                 cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 606 |     |                 if (cache.state.pool1.price >= cache.crossPrice) {
 607 |     |                     // cross into limit pool
 608 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_POOL;
 609 |     |                     if (cache.state.pool1.price == cache.crossPrice)
 610 |     |                         // also cross range tick
 611 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 612 |     |                     else {
 613 |     |                         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool1.tickAtPrice;
 614 |     |                         cache.crossPrice = cache.state.pool1.price;
 615 |     |                     }
 616 |     |                 }
 617 |     |                 else {
 618 |     |                     // cross only range tick
 619 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 620 |     |                 }
 621 |     |             } else {
 622 |     |                 // load range and limit pools
 623 |     |                 cache.limitActive = true;
 624 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity + cache.state.pool1.liquidity;
 625 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 626 |     |                 int24 rangeTickAhead; int24 limitTickAhead;
 627 |     |                 if (cache.crossStatus == LIMIT_POOL &&
 628 |     |                         cache.crossTick % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 629 |     |                         TickMap.get(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing))
 630 |     |                 {
 631 |     |                     limitTickAhead = cache.crossTick;
 632 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = cache.crossTick - cache.constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 633 |     |                 } else {
 634 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = TickMap.previous(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 635 |     |                     limitTickAhead = TickMap.previous(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 636 |     |                 }
 637 |     |                 // next range tick vs. next limit tick
 638 |     |                 
 639 |     |                 if (rangeTickAhead >= limitTickAhead) {
 640 |     |                     cache.crossTick = rangeTickAhead;
 641 |     |                     // cross range tick
 642 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 643 |     |                     if (rangeTickAhead == limitTickAhead)
 644 |     |                         // also cross limit tick
 645 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 646 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 647 |     |                 } else {
 648 |     |                     // only cross limit tick
 649 |     |                     cache.crossTick = limitTickAhead;
 650 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_TICK;
 651 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants)
 652 |     |                                                                                  : ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt;
 653 |     |                 }
 654 |     |             }
 655 |     |         } else {
 656 |     |             if (cache.price < cache.state.pool0.price) {
 657 |     |                 // load range pool
 658 |     |                 cache.limitActive = false;
 659 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity;
 660 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 661 |     |                 // next range tick vs. limit pool price
 662 |     |                 cache.crossTick = TickMap.next(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 663 |     |                 cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 664 |     |                 if (cache.state.pool0.price <= cache.crossPrice) {
 665 |     |                     // cross into limit pool
 666 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = LIMIT_POOL;
 667 |     |                     if (cache.state.pool0.price == cache.crossPrice)
 668 |     |                         // also cross range tick
 669 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 670 |     |                     else {
 671 |     |                         cache.crossTick = cache.state.pool0.tickAtPrice;
 672 |     |                         cache.crossPrice = cache.state.pool0.price;
 673 |     |                     }
 674 |     |                 }
 675 |     |                 else {
 676 |     |                     // cross only range tick
 677 |     |                     cache.crossStatus = RANGE_TICK;
 678 |     |                 }
 679 |     |             } else {
 680 |     |                 // load range and limit pools
 681 |     |                 cache.limitActive = true;
 682 |     |                 cache.liquidity = cache.state.pool.liquidity + cache.state.pool0.liquidity;
 683 |     |                 (cache.crossTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(cache.crossTick, cache.constants, cache.price);
 684 |     |                 // next range tick vs. next limit tick
 685 |     |                 int24 rangeTickAhead; int24 limitTickAhead;
 686 |     |                 if (cache.crossStatus == LIMIT_POOL &&
 687 |     |                         cache.crossTick % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 688 |     |                         TickMap.get(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing))
 689 |     |                 {
 690 |     |                     limitTickAhead = cache.crossTick;
 691 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = cache.crossTick + cache.constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 692 |     |                 } else {
 693 |     |                     rangeTickAhead = TickMap.next(rangeTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 694 |     |                     limitTickAhead = TickMap.next(limitTickMap, cache.crossTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, inclusive);
 695 |     |                 }
 696 |     |                 if (rangeTickAhead <= limitTickAhead) {
 697 |     |                     cache.crossTick = rangeTickAhead;
 698 |     |                     // cross range tick
 699 |     |                     cache.crossStatus |= RANGE_TICK;
 700 |     |                     if (rangeTickAhead == limitTickAhead)
 701 |     |                         // also cross limit tick
 702 |     |                         cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 703 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants);
 704 |     |                 } else {
 705 |     |                     // only cross limit tick
 706 |     |                     cache.crossTick = limitTickAhead;
 707 |     |                     cache.crossStatus |= LIMIT_TICK;
 708 |     |                     cache.crossPrice = ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.crossTick, cache.constants)
 709 |     |                                                                                  : ticks[cache.crossTick].limit.priceAt;
 710 |     |                 }
 711 |     |             }
 712 |     |         }
 713 |     |         return cache;
 714 |     |     }
 715 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/Claims.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import './EpochMap.sol';
   6 |     | import '../TickMap.sol';
   7 |     | import '../utils/String.sol';

  10 |     | library Claims {
  11 |     | 
  12 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function validate(
  15 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  16 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  17 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
  18 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
  19 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  20 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
  21 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
  22 |     |     ) {
  23 |     |         // validate position liquidity
  24 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > cache.position.liquidity) require (false, 'NotEnoughPositionLiquidity()');
  25 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
  26 |     |             require(false, 'NoPositionLiquidityFound()');
  27 |     |         }
  28 |     |         
  29 |     |         if (params.claim < cache.position.lower ||
  30 |     |                 params.claim > cache.position.upper)
  31 |     |             require (false, 'InvalidClaimTick()');
  32 |     | 
  33 |     |         uint32 claimTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(params.claim, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  34 |     | 
  35 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne){
  36 |     |             if (cache.pool.price >= cache.priceClaim) {
  37 |     |                 if (cache.pool.price <= cache.priceUpper) {
  38 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.pool.price;
  39 |     |                     params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(cache.pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
  40 |     |                     claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  41 |     |                 } else {
  42 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceUpper;
  43 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.upper;
  44 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  45 |     |                 }
  46 |     |                 claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  47 |     |             } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
  48 |     |                 if (cache.claimTick.priceAt == 0) {
  49 |     |                     require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt1()');
  50 |     |                 }
  51 |     |                 cache.priceClaim = cache.claimTick.priceAt;
  52 |     |             }
  53 |     |         } else {
  54 |     |             if (cache.pool.price <= cache.priceClaim) {
  55 |     |                 if (cache.pool.price >= cache.priceLower) {
  56 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.pool.price;
  57 |     |                     params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(cache.pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
  58 |     |                     claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  59 |     |                 } else {
  60 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceLower;
  61 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.lower;
  62 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  63 |     | 
  64 |     |                 }
  65 |     |                 claimTickEpoch = cache.state.epoch;
  66 |     |             } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
  67 |     |                 if (cache.claimTick.priceAt == 0) {
  68 |     |                     require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt2()');
  69 |     |                 }
  70 |     |                 cache.priceClaim = cache.claimTick.priceAt;
  71 |     |             }
  72 |     |         }
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         // validate claim tick
  75 |     |         if (params.claim == (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
  76 |     |             // set params.amount to 0 for event emitted at end
  77 |     |             cache.liquidityBurned = 0;
  78 |     |              if (claimTickEpoch <= cache.position.epochLast)
  79 |     |                 require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt3()');
  80 |     |         } else if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
  81 |     |             /// @dev - partway claim is valid as long as liquidity is not being removed
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |             // if we cleared the final tick of their position, this is the wrong claim tick
  84 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
  85 |     |                 uint32 endTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(cache.position.upper, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  86 |     |                 if (endTickEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
  87 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.upper;
  88 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceUpper;
  89 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.upper].limit;
  90 |     |                     cache.liquidityBurned = cache.position.liquidity;
  91 |     |                 } else {
  92 |     |                     int24 claimTickNext = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.claim, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  93 |     |                     uint32 claimTickNextEpoch = EpochMap.get(claimTickNext, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  94 |     |                     ///@dev - next swapEpoch should not be greater
  95 |     |                     if (claimTickNextEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
  96 |     |                         require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt5()');
  97 |     |                     }
  98 |     |                 }
  99 |     |             } else {
 100 |     |                 uint32 endTickEpoch = EpochMap.get(cache.position.lower, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
 101 |     |                 if (endTickEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
 102 |     |                     params.claim = cache.position.lower;
 103 |     |                     cache.priceClaim = cache.priceLower;
 104 |     |                     cache.claimTick = ticks[cache.position.lower].limit;
 105 |     |                     cache.liquidityBurned = cache.position.liquidity;
 106 |     |                 } else {
 107 |     |                     int24 claimTickNext = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.claim, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
 108 |     |                     uint32 claimTickNextEpoch = EpochMap.get(claimTickNext, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
 109 |     |                     ///@dev - next swapEpoch should not be greater
 110 |     |                     if (claimTickNextEpoch > cache.position.epochLast) {
 111 |     |                         require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt5()');
 112 |     |                     }
 113 |     |                 }
 114 |     |             }
 115 |     |         }
 116 |     |         /// @dev - start tick does not overwrite position and final tick clears position
 117 |     |         if (params.claim != cache.position.upper && params.claim != cache.position.lower) {
 118 |     |             // check epochLast on claim tick
 119 |     |             if (claimTickEpoch <= cache.position.epochLast)
 120 |     |                 require (false, 'WrongTickClaimedAt7()');
 121 |     |         }
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |         // early return if no update and amount burned is 0
 124 |     |         //TODO: after we've cycled through claim ticks and there are no position updates just revert - DONE
 125 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.lower
 126 |     |                               : params.claim == cache.position.upper) {
 127 |     |             if (cache.liquidityBurned == 0)
 128 |     |                 require(false, 'NoPositionUpdates()');
 129 |     |         }
 130 |     | 
 131 |     |         return (params, cache);
 132 |     |     }
 133 |     | 
 134 |     |     function getDeltas(
 135 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 136 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 137 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 138 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 139 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 140 |     |     ) {
 141 |     |         // if half tick priceAt > 0 add amountOut to amountOutClaimed
 142 |     |         // set claimPriceLast if zero
 143 |     |         if (!cache.position.crossedInto) {
 144 |     |             cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 145 |     |         }
 146 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.GetDeltasLocals memory locals;
 147 |     | 
 148 |     |         if (params.claim % constants.tickSpacing != 0)
 149 |     |         // this should pass price at the claim tick
 150 |     |             locals.previousFullTick = TickMap.roundBack(params.claim, constants, params.zeroForOne, ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.claim, constants));
 151 |     |         else
 152 |     |             locals.previousFullTick = params.claim;
 153 |     |         locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 154 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? locals.previousFullTick > cache.position.lower
 155 |     |                               : locals.previousFullTick < cache.position.upper) {
 156 |     |             
 157 |     |             // claim amounts up to latest full tick crossed
 158 |     |             cache.amountIn += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.position.liquidity, cache.priceLower, locals.pricePrevious, false)
 159 |     |                                                         : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.position.liquidity, locals.pricePrevious, cache.priceUpper, false));
 160 |     |         }
 161 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 162 |     |            // if tick hasn't been set back calculate amountIn
 163 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceClaim > locals.pricePrevious
 164 |     |                                   : cache.priceClaim < locals.pricePrevious) {
 165 |     |                 // allow partial tick claim if removing liquidity
 166 |     |                 cache.amountIn += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidityBurned, locals.pricePrevious, cache.priceClaim, false)
 167 |     |                                                             : ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceClaim, locals.pricePrevious, false));
 168 |     |             }
 169 |     |             // use priceClaim if tick hasn't been set back
 170 |     |             // else use claimPriceLast to calculate amountOut
 171 |     |             if (params.claim != (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
 172 |     |                 cache.amountOut += uint128(params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getDx(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceClaim, cache.priceUpper, false)
 173 |     |                                                              : ConstantProduct.getDy(cache.liquidityBurned, cache.priceLower, cache.priceClaim, false));
 174 |     |             }
 175 |     |         }
 176 |     |         // take protocol fee if needed
 177 |     |         if (cache.pool.protocolFillFee > 0 && cache.amountIn > 0) {
 178 |     |             uint128 protocolFeeAmount = OverflowMath.mulDiv(cache.amountIn, cache.pool.protocolFillFee, 1e4).toUint128();
 179 |     |             cache.amountIn -= protocolFeeAmount;
 180 |     |             cache.pool.protocolFees += protocolFeeAmount;
 181 |     |         }
 182 |     |         return cache;
 183 |     |     }
 184 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/EpochMap.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   6 |     | 
   7 |     | library EpochMap {
   8 |     |     event SyncLimitTick(
   9 |     |         uint32 epoch,
  10 |     |         int24 tick,
  11 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  12 |     |     );
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     function set(
  15 |     |         int24  tick,
  16 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  17 |     |         uint256 epoch,
  18 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  19 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
  20 |     |     ) internal {
  21 |     |         (
  22 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  23 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  24 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  25 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  26 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, constants);
  27 |     |         // assert epoch isn't bigger than max uint32
  28 |     |         uint256 epochValue = zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex]
  29 |     |                                         : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex];
  30 |     |         // clear previous value
  31 |     |         epochValue &=  ~(((1 << 9) - 1) << ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32));
  32 |     |         // add new value to word
  33 |     |         epochValue |= epoch << ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32);
  34 |     |         // store word in map
  35 |     |         zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex] = epochValue
  36 |     |                    : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex] = epochValue;
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |         emit SyncLimitTick(uint32(epoch), tick, zeroForOne);
  39 |     |     }
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |     function get(
  42 |     |         int24 tick,
  43 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  44 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  45 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
  46 |     |     ) internal view returns (
  47 |     |         uint32 epoch
  48 |     |     ) {
  49 |     |         (
  50 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  51 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  52 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  53 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  54 |     |         ) = getIndices(tick, constants);
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |         uint256 epochValue = zeroForOne ? tickMap.epochs0[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex]
  57 |     |                                         : tickMap.epochs1[volumeIndex][blockIndex][wordIndex];
  58 |     |         // right shift so first 8 bits are epoch value
  59 |     |         epochValue >>= ((tickIndex & 0x7) * 32);
  60 |     |         // clear other bits
  61 |     |         epochValue &= ((1 << 32) - 1);
  62 |     |         return uint32(epochValue);
  63 |     |     }
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |     function getIndices(
  66 |     |         int24 tick,
  67 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
  68 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  69 |     |             uint256 tickIndex,
  70 |     |             uint256 wordIndex,
  71 |     |             uint256 blockIndex,
  72 |     |             uint256 volumeIndex
  73 |     |         )
  74 |     |     {
  75 |     |         unchecked {
  76 |     |             if (tick > ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing)) require (false, 'TickIndexOverflow()');
  77 |     |             if (tick < ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing)) require (false, 'TickIndexUnderflow()');
  78 |     |             if (tick % (constants.tickSpacing / 2) != 0) {
  79 |     |                 require (false, 'TickIndexInvalid()');
  80 |     |             } 
  81 |     |             tickIndex = uint256(int256((_round(tick, constants.tickSpacing / 2) 
  82 |     |                                         - _round(ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK, constants.tickSpacing / 2)) 
  83 |     |                                         / (constants.tickSpacing / 2)));
  84 |     |             wordIndex = tickIndex >> 3;        // 2^3 epochs per word
  85 |     |             blockIndex = tickIndex >> 11;      // 2^8 words per block
  86 |     |             volumeIndex = tickIndex >> 19;     // 2^8 blocks per volume
  87 |     |             if (blockIndex > 2046) require (false, 'BlockIndexOverflow()');
  88 |     |         }
  89 |     |     }
  90 |     | 
  91 |     |     function _round(
  92 |     |         int24 tick,
  93 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  94 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  95 |     |         int24 roundedTick
  96 |     |     ) {
  97 |     |         return tick / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
  98 |     |     }
  99 |     | }
 100 |     |
