  14 |     | 
  15 |     | /// @notice Position management library for ranged liquidity.
  16 |     | /// @notice Position management library for ranged liquidity.
  17 |     | library LimitPositions {
  18 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  19 |     | 
  20 |     |     event BurnLimit(
  21 |     |         address indexed to,
  22 |     |         uint32 positionId,
  23 |     |         int24 lower,
  24 |     |         int24 upper,
  25 |     |         int24 oldClaim,
  26 |     |         int24 newClaim,
  27 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  28 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
  29 |     |         uint128 tokenInClaimed,
  30 |     |         uint128 tokenOutBurned
  31 |     |     );
  32 |     | 
  33 |     |     function resize(
  34 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  35 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  36 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  37 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  38 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  39 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  40 |     |     ) internal returns (
  41 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory,
  42 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory
  43 |     |     )
  44 |     |     {
  45 |     |         ConstantProduct.checkTicks(params.lower, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing);
  46 |     | 
  47 |     |         cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
  48 |     |         cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
  49 |     |         cache.mintSize = uint256(params.mintPercent) * uint256(params.amount) / 1e28;
  50 |     | 
  51 |     |         // calculate L constant
  52 |     |         cache.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
  53 |     |             cache.priceLower,
  54 |     |             cache.priceUpper,
  55 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper,
  56 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(params.amount),
  57 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? uint256(params.amount) : 0
  58 |     |         );
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) require (false, 'NoLiquidityBeingAdded()');
  61 |     |         // calculate price limit by using half of input
  62 |     |         {
  63 |     |             cache.priceLimit = params.zeroForOne ? ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(cache.priceUpper, cache.liquidityMinted, params.amount / 2, true, true)
  64 |     |                                                  : ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(cache.priceLower, cache.liquidityMinted, params.amount / 2, false, true);
  65 |     |             if (cache.priceLimit == 0) require (false, 'PriceLimitZero()');
  66 |     |             // get tick at price
  67 |     |             cache.tickLimit = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(cache.priceLimit.toUint160(), cache.constants);
  68 |     |             // round to nearest tick spacing
  69 |     |             cache.priceLimit = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.tickLimit, cache.constants);
  70 |     |         }
  71 |     | 
  72 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory swapCache;
  73 |     |         swapCache.state = cache.state;
  74 |     |         swapCache.constants = cache.constants;
  75 |     |         swapCache.price = cache.state.pool.price;
  76 |     | 
  77 |     |         // swap zero if no liquidity near market price
  78 |     |         if (cache.state.pool.liquidity == 0 && 
  79 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? swapCache.price > cache.priceLower
  80 |     |                                : swapCache.price < cache.priceUpper)) {
  81 |     |             swapCache = Ticks.swap(
  82 |     |                 ticks,
  83 |     |                 samples,
  84 |     |                 rangeTickMap,
  85 |     |                 limitTickMap,
  86 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams({
  87 |     |                     to: params.to,
  88 |     |                     priceLimit: (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower 
  89 |     |                                                    : cache.priceUpper).toUint160(),
  90 |     |                     amount: 0,
  91 |     |                     //TODO: handle exactOut
  92 |     |                     exactIn: true,
  93 |     |                     zeroForOne: params.zeroForOne,
  94 |     |                     callbackData: abi.encodePacked(bytes1(0x0))
  95 |     |                 }),
  96 |     |                 swapCache
  97 |     |             );
  98 |     |         }
  99 |     | 
 100 |     |         // only swap if priceLimit is beyond current pool price
 101 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLimit < swapCache.price
 102 |     |                               : cache.priceLimit > swapCache.price) {
 103 |     |             // swap and save the pool state
 104 |     |             swapCache = Ticks.swap(
 105 |     |                 ticks,
 106 |     |                 samples,
 107 |     |                 rangeTickMap,
 108 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 109 |     |                 PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams({
 110 |     |                     to: params.to,
 111 |     |                     priceLimit: cache.priceLimit.toUint160(),
 112 |     |                     amount: params.amount,
 113 |     |                     //TODO: handle exactOut
 114 |     |                     exactIn: true,
 115 |     |                     zeroForOne: params.zeroForOne,
 116 |     |                     callbackData: abi.encodePacked(bytes1(0x0))
 117 |     |                 }),
 118 |     |                 swapCache
 119 |     |             );
 120 |     |             // subtract from remaining input amount
 121 |     |             params.amount -= uint128(swapCache.input);
 122 |     | 
 123 |     |         }
 124 |     |         // save to cache
 125 |     |         cache.swapCache = swapCache;
 126 |     |         cache.state = swapCache.state;
 127 |     | 
 128 |     |         if (params.amount < cache.mintSize) params.amount = 0;
 129 |     |         // move start tick based on amount filled in swap
 130 |     |         if ((params.amount > 0 && swapCache.input > 0) ||
 131 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower < swapCache.price
 132 |     |                                : cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price)
 133 |     |         ) {
 134 |     |             // move the tick limit based on pool.tickAtPrice
 135 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower < swapCache.price
 136 |     |                                   : cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price) {
 137 |     |                 cache.tickLimit = swapCache.state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 138 |     |             }
 139 |     |             // round ahead tickLimit to avoid crossing epochs
 140 |     |             cache.tickLimit = TickMap.roundAhead(cache.tickLimit, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, swapCache.price);
 141 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 142 |     |                 if (cache.priceLower < swapCache.price) {
 143 |     |                     // if rounding goes past limit trim position
 144 |     |                     /// @dev - if swap didn't go to limit user would be 100% filled
 145 |     |                     params.lower = cache.tickLimit;
 146 |     |                     cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 147 |     |                 }
 148 |     |                 if (params.lower >= params.upper && 
 149 |     |                     params.lower < ConstantProduct.maxTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing) - cache.constants.tickSpacing
 150 |     |                 ) {
 151 |     |                     params.upper = params.lower + cache.constants.tickSpacing;
 152 |     |                 }
 153 |     |                 cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 154 |     |             } else {
 155 |     |                 if (cache.priceUpper > swapCache.price) {
 156 |     |                     // if rounding goes past limit trim position
 157 |     |                     params.upper = cache.tickLimit;
 158 |     |                     cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 159 |     |                 }
 160 |     |                 if (params.upper <= params.lower && 
 161 |     |                     params.lower > ConstantProduct.minTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing) + cache.constants.tickSpacing
 162 |     |                 ) {
 163 |     |                     params.lower = params.upper - cache.constants.tickSpacing;
 164 |     |                 }
 165 |     |                 cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 166 |     |             }
 167 |     |             if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
 168 |     |                 cache.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
 169 |     |                     cache.priceLower,
 170 |     |                     cache.priceUpper,
 171 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper,
 172 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? 0 : uint256(params.amount),
 173 |     |                     params.zeroForOne ? uint256(params.amount) : 0
 174 |     |                 );
 175 |     |                  if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) {
 176 |     |                     // skip minting
 177 |     |                     params.amount = 0;
 178 |     |                  }
 179 |     |             } else {
 180 |     |                 // skip minting
 181 |     |                 params.amount = 0;
 182 |     |                 cache.liquidityMinted = 0;
 183 |     |             }
 184 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
 185 |     |         }
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |         /// @dev - for safety
 188 |     |         if (params.lower >= params.upper) {
 189 |     |             // zero out amount transferred in
 190 |     |             params.amount = 0;
 191 |     |         }
 192 |     | 
 193 |     |         return (
 194 |     |             params,
 195 |     |             cache
 196 |     |         );
 197 |     |     }
 198 |     | 
 199 |     |     function add(
 200 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 201 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 202 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 203 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params
 204 |     |     ) internal returns (
 205 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory,
 206 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory
 207 |     |     ) {
 208 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) return (cache.pool, cache.position);
 209 |     | 
 210 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 211 |     |             cache.position.epochLast = cache.state.epoch;
 212 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1; // increment for future swaps
 213 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).mint(
 214 |     |                 params.to,
 215 |     |                 params.positionId,
 216 |     |                 1,
 217 |     |                 cache.constants
 218 |     |             );
 219 |     |         } else {
 220 |     |             // safety check in case we somehow get here
 221 |     |             if (
 222 |     |                 params.zeroForOne
 223 |     |                     ? EpochMap.get(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants)
 224 |     |                             > cache.position.epochLast
 225 |     |                     : EpochMap.get(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants)
 226 |     |                             > cache.position.epochLast
 227 |     |             ) {
 228 |     |                 require (false, 'PositionAlreadyEntered()');
 229 |     |             }
 230 |     |             /// @auditor maybe this shouldn't be a revert but rather just not mint the position?
 231 |     |         }
 232 |     |         
 233 |     |         // add liquidity to ticks
 234 |     |         LimitTicks.insert(
 235 |     |             ticks,
 236 |     |             tickMap,
 237 |     |             cache,
 238 |     |             params
 239 |     |         );
 240 |     | 
 241 |     |         // update liquidity global
 242 |     |         cache.state.liquidityGlobal += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 243 |     | 
 244 |     |         cache.position.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 245 |     | 
 246 |     |         return (cache.pool, cache.position);
 247 |     |     }
 248 |     | 
 249 |     |     function update(
 250 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 251 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 252 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 253 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params
 254 |     |     ) internal returns (
 255 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
 256 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 257 |     |     )
 258 |     |     {
 259 |     |         (
 260 |     |             params,
 261 |     |             cache
 262 |     |         ) = _deltas(
 263 |     |             ticks,
 264 |     |             tickMap,
 265 |     |             params,
 266 |     |             cache
 267 |     |         );
 268 |     | 
 269 |     |         // update pool liquidity
 270 |     |         if (cache.priceClaim == cache.pool.price && cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 271 |     |             // handle pool.price at edge of range
 272 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceClaim < cache.priceUpper
 273 |     |                                   : cache.priceClaim > cache.priceLower)
 274 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(cache.pool.liquidity, cache.liquidityBurned, "PLU-3");
 275 |     |                 cache.pool.liquidity -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 276 |     |         }
 277 |     | 
 278 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > 0) {
 279 |     |             if (params.claim == (params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : cache.position.lower)) {
 280 |     |                 // if claim is final tick no liquidity to remove
 281 |     |                 cache.removeLower = false;
 282 |     |                 cache.removeUpper = false;
 283 |     |             } else {
 284 |     |                 // else remove liquidity from final tick
 285 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.removeUpper = true 
 286 |     |                                   : cache.removeLower = true;
 287 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 288 |     | 
 289 |     |                     if (params.claim == cache.position.lower && 
 290 |     |                         cache.pool.price < cache.priceLower
 291 |     |                     ) {
 292 |     |                         // full tick price was touched
 293 |     |                         cache.removeLower = true;
 294 |     |                     } else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 && 
 295 |     |                                     cache.pool.price < cache.priceClaim)
 296 |     |                         // half tick was created
 297 |     |                         cache.removeLower = true;
 298 |     |                 } else {
 299 |     |                     if (params.claim == cache.position.upper &&
 300 |     |                         cache.pool.price > cache.priceUpper
 301 |     |                     )
 302 |     |                         // full tick price was touched
 303 |     |                         cache.removeUpper = true;
 304 |     |                     else if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0 &&
 305 |     |                                     cache.pool.price > cache.priceClaim)
 306 |     |                         // half tick was created
 307 |     |                         cache.removeUpper = true;
 308 |     |                 }
 309 |     |             }
 310 |     |             LimitTicks.remove(
 311 |     |                 ticks,
 312 |     |                 tickMap,
 313 |     |                 params,
 314 |     |                 cache,
 315 |     |                 cache.constants
 316 |     |             );
 317 |     |             // update position liquidity
 318 |     |             cache.position.liquidity -= uint128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 319 |     |             // update global liquidity
 320 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.liquidityBurned, "LGU-2");
 321 |     |             cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 322 |     |         }
 323 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.upper
 324 |     |                               : params.claim == cache.position.lower) {
 325 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.position.liquidity, "LGU-3");
 326 |     |             cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.position.liquidity;
 327 |     |             cache.position.liquidity = 0;
 328 |     |         }
 329 |     |         // clear out old position
 330 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim != cache.position.lower 
 331 |     |                               : params.claim != cache.position.upper) {
 332 |     |             /// @dev - this also clears out position end claims
 333 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne ? params.claim == cache.position.lower 
 334 |     |                                   : params.claim == cache.position.upper) {
 335 |     |                 // subtract remaining position liquidity out from global
 336 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(cache.state.liquidityGlobal, cache.position.liquidity, "LGU-4");
 337 |     |                 cache.state.liquidityGlobal -= cache.position.liquidity;
 338 |     |             }
 339 |     |         }
 340 |     |         // clear position if empty
 341 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 342 |     |             cache.position.epochLast = 0;
 343 |     |             cache.position.crossedInto = false;
 344 |     |         }
 345 |     | 
 346 |     |         // round back claim tick for storage
 347 |     |         if (params.claim % cache.constants.tickSpacing != 0) {
 348 |     |             cache.claim = params.claim;
 349 |     |             params.claim = TickMap.roundBack(params.claim, cache.constants, params.zeroForOne, cache.priceClaim);
 350 |     |         }
 351 |     |         
 352 |     |         emit BurnLimit(
 353 |     |             params.to,
 354 |     |             params.positionId,
 355 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 356 |     |             cache.position.upper,
 357 |     |             cache.claim,
 358 |     |             params.claim,
 359 |     |             params.zeroForOne,
 360 |     |             cache.liquidityBurned,
 361 |     |             cache.amountIn,
 362 |     |             cache.amountOut
 363 |     |         );
 364 |     | 
 365 |     |         // save pool to state in memory
 366 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne) cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool;
 367 |     |         else cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 368 |     | 
 369 |     |         return (params, cache);
 370 |     |     }
 371 |     | 
 372 |     |     function snapshot(
 373 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 374 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 375 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 376 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params
 377 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 378 |     |         uint128 amountIn,
 379 |     |         uint128 amountOut
 380 |     |     ) {
 381 |     |         (
 382 |     |             params,
 383 |     |             cache
 384 |     |         ) = _deltas(
 385 |     |             ticks,
 386 |     |             tickMap,
 387 |     |             params,
 388 |     |             cache
 389 |     |         );
 390 |     | 
 391 |     |         return (cache.amountIn, cache.amountOut);
 392 |     |     }
 393 |     | 
 394 |     |     function _deltas(
 395 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 396 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 397 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 398 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
 399 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 400 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory,
 401 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 402 |     |     ) {
 403 |     |         cache = LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache({
 404 |     |             state: cache.state,
 405 |     |             pool: params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1,
 406 |     |             claimTick: ticks[params.claim].limit,
 407 |     |             position: cache.position,
 408 |     |             constants: cache.constants,
 409 |     |             priceLower: ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.lower, cache.constants),
 410 |     |             priceClaim: ticks[params.claim].limit.priceAt == 0 ? ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.claim, cache.constants)
 411 |     |                                                                : ticks[params.claim].limit.priceAt,
 412 |     |             priceUpper: ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.upper, cache.constants),
 413 |     |             liquidityBurned: _convert(cache.position.liquidity, params.burnPercent),
 414 |     |             amountIn: 0,
 415 |     |             amountOut: 0,
 416 |     |             claim: params.claim,
 417 |     |             removeLower: false,
 418 |     |             removeUpper: false
 419 |     |         });
 420 |     | 
 421 |     |         // check claim is valid
 422 |     |         (params, cache) = Claims.validate(
 423 |     |             ticks,
 424 |     |             tickMap,
 425 |     |             params,
 426 |     |             cache
 427 |     |         );
 428 |     | 
 429 |     |         // calculate position deltas
 430 |     |         cache = Claims.getDeltas(params, cache, cache.constants);
 431 |     | 
 432 |     |         return (params, cache);
 433 |     |     }
 434 |     | 
 435 |     |     function _convert(
 436 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
 437 |     |         uint128 percent
 438 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 439 |     |         uint128
 440 |     |     ) {
 441 |     |         // convert percentage to liquidity amount
 442 |     |         if (percent > 1e38) percent = 1e38;
 443 |     |         if (liquidity == 0 && percent > 0) require (false, 'PositionNotFound()');
 444 |     |         return uint128(uint256(liquidity) * uint256(percent) / 1e38);
 445 |     |     }
 446 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/LimitTicks.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolFactory.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../interfaces/limit/ILimitPool.sol';
   7 |     | import '../math/ConstantProduct.sol';
   8 |     | import './LimitPositions.sol';
   9 |     | import '../math/OverflowMath.sol';
  10 |     | import '../TickMap.sol';
  11 |     | import './EpochMap.sol';
  12 |     | import '../Samples.sol';
  13 |     | import '../utils/SafeCast.sol';
  14 |     | 
  15 |     | /// @notice Tick management library for limit pools
  16 |     | library LimitTicks {
  17 |     |     error LiquidityOverflow();
  18 |     |     error LiquidityUnderflow();
  19 |     |     error InvalidLowerTick();
  20 |     |     error InvalidUpperTick();
  21 |     |     error InvalidPositionAmount();
  22 |     |     error InvalidPositionBounds();
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  25 |     | 
  26 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q96 = 0x1000000000000000000000000;
  27 |     | 
  28 |     |     event SyncLimitLiquidity(
  29 |     |         uint128 liquidityAdded,
  30 |     |         int24 tick,
  31 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  32 |     |     );
  33 |     | 
  34 |     |     function validate(
  35 |     |         int24 lower,
  36 |     |         int24 upper,
  37 |     |         int24 tickSpacing
  38 |     |     ) internal pure {
  39 |     |         if (lower % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  40 |     |         if (lower <= ConstantProduct.MIN_TICK) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  41 |     |         if (upper % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  42 |     |         if (upper >= ConstantProduct.MAX_TICK) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  43 |     |         if (lower >= upper) require(false, 'InvalidPositionBounds()');
  44 |     |     }
  45 |     | 
  46 |     |     function insert(
  47 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  48 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  49 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
  50 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params
  51 |     |     ) internal {
  52 |     |         /// @dev - validation of ticks is in Positions.validate
  53 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0)
  54 |     |             require(false, 'NoLiquidityBeingAdded()');
  55 |     |         if (cache.state.liquidityGlobal + cache.liquidityMinted > uint128(type(int128).max))
  56 |     |             require(false, 'LiquidityOverflow()');
  57 |     | 
  58 |     |         int256 liquidityMinted = int256(cache.liquidityMinted);
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         // check if adding liquidity necessary
  61 |     |         if (!params.zeroForOne || cache.priceLower > cache.pool.price) {
  62 |     |             // sets bit in map
  63 |     |             if(!TickMap.set(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing)){
  64 |     |                 // inherit epoch 
  65 |     |                 int24 tickAhead;
  66 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  67 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  68 |     |                 } else {
  69 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.lower, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  70 |     |                 }
  71 |     |                 uint32 epochAhead = EpochMap.get(tickAhead, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  72 |     |                 EpochMap.set(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, epochAhead, tickMap, cache.constants);
  73 |     |             }
  74 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickLower = ticks[params.lower].limit;
  75 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
  76 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityDelta += int128(liquidityMinted);
  77 |     |             } else {
  78 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityDelta -= int128(liquidityMinted);
  79 |     |             }
  80 |     |             tickLower.liquidityAbsolute += cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128();
  81 |     |             ticks[params.lower].limit = tickLower;
  82 |     |         } else {
  83 |     |             /// @dev - i.e. if zeroForOne && cache.priceLower <= cache.pool.price
  84 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
  85 |     |             // mark epoch on undercut tick
  86 |     |             EpochMap.set(params.lower, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
  87 |     |         }
  88 |     | 
  89 |     |         if (params.zeroForOne || cache.priceUpper < cache.pool.price) {
  90 |     |             if(!TickMap.set(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
  91 |     |                 int24 tickAhead;
  92 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  93 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.next(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  94 |     |                 } else {
  95 |     |                     tickAhead  = TickMap.previous(tickMap, params.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing, false);
  96 |     |                 }
  97 |     |                 uint32 epochAhead = EpochMap.get(tickAhead, params.zeroForOne, tickMap, cache.constants);
  98 |     |                 EpochMap.set(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, epochAhead, tickMap, cache.constants);
  99 |     |             }
 100 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickUpper = ticks[params.upper].limit;
 101 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 102 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityDelta -= int128(liquidityMinted);
 103 |     |             } else {
 104 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityDelta += int128(liquidityMinted);
 105 |     |             }
 106 |     |             tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute += cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128();
 107 |     |             ticks[params.upper].limit = tickUpper;
 108 |     |         } else {
 109 |     |             /// @dev - i.e. if !zeroForOne && cache.priceUpper >= cache.pool.price
 110 |     |             cache.state.epoch += 1;
 111 |     |             // mark epoch on undercut tick
 112 |     |             EpochMap.set(params.upper, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 113 |     |         }
 114 |     |     }
 115 |     | 
 116 |     |     function insertSingle(
 117 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
 118 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 119 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 120 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 121 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool,
 122 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 123 |     |     ) internal returns (
 124 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory
 125 |     |     ){
 126 |     |         /// @auditor - would be smart to protect against the case of epochs crossing
 127 |     |         (
 128 |     |             int24 tickToSave,
 129 |     |             uint160 roundedPrice
 130 |     |         ) = TickMap.roundHalf(pool.tickAtPrice, constants, pool.price);
 131 |     |         // update tick to save
 132 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.LimitTick memory tick = ticks[tickToSave].limit;
 133 |     |         /// @auditor - tick.priceAt will be zero for tick % tickSpacing == 0
 134 |     |         if (tick.priceAt == 0) {
 135 |     |             if (pool.price != (params.zeroForOne ? cache.priceLower : cache.priceUpper)) {
 136 |     |                 TickMap.set(tickMap, tickToSave, constants.tickSpacing);
 137 |     |             }
 138 |     |             EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 139 |     |         }
 140 |     |         // skip if we are at the nearest full tick
 141 |     |         if(pool.price != roundedPrice) {
 142 |     |             // if empty just save the pool price
 143 |     |             if (tick.priceAt == 0) {
 144 |     |                 tick.priceAt = pool.price;
 145 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertTickAtPriceDivisibleByTickSpacing(tickToSave, ticks[tickToSave].limit.priceAt, constants.tickSpacing);
 146 |     |             }
 147 |     |             else {
 148 |     |                 // we need to blend the two partial fills into a single tick
 149 |     |                 LimitPoolStructs.InsertSingleLocals memory locals;
 150 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 151 |     |                     // 0 -> 1 positions price moves up so nextFullTick is greater
 152 |     |                     locals.previousFullTick = tickToSave - constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 153 |     |                     locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 154 |     |                     // calculate amountOut filled across both partial fills
 155 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact = ConstantProduct.getDy(pool.liquidity, locals.pricePrevious, pool.price, false);
 156 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact += ConstantProduct.getDy(uint128(tick.liquidityDelta), locals.pricePrevious, tick.priceAt, false);
 157 |     |                     // add current pool liquidity to partial tick
 158 |     |                     uint128 combinedLiquidity = pool.liquidity + uint128(tick.liquidityDelta);
 159 |     |                     // advance price based on combined fill
 160 |     |                     tick.priceAt = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(uint256(locals.pricePrevious), combinedLiquidity, locals.amountOutExact, false, true).toUint160();
 161 |     |                     // dx to the next tick is less than before the tick blend
 162 |     |                     EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 163 |     |                 } else {
 164 |     |                     // 0 -> 1 positions price moves up so nextFullTick is lesser
 165 |     |                     locals.previousFullTick = tickToSave + constants.tickSpacing / 2;
 166 |     |                     locals.pricePrevious = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(locals.previousFullTick, constants);
 167 |     |                     // calculate amountOut filled across both partial fills
 168 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact = ConstantProduct.getDx(pool.liquidity, pool.price, locals.pricePrevious, false);
 169 |     |                     locals.amountOutExact += ConstantProduct.getDx(uint128(tick.liquidityDelta), tick.priceAt, locals.pricePrevious, false);
 170 |     |                     // add current pool liquidity to partial tick
 171 |     |                     uint128 combinedLiquidity = pool.liquidity + uint128(tick.liquidityDelta);
 172 |     |                     // advance price based on combined fill
 173 |     |                     tick.priceAt = ConstantProduct.getNewPrice(uint256(locals.pricePrevious), combinedLiquidity, locals.amountOutExact, true, true).toUint160();
 174 |     |                     // mark epoch for second partial fill positions
 175 |     |                     EpochMap.set(tickToSave, params.zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, constants);
 176 |     |                 }
 177 |     |             }
 178 |     |         }
 179 |     |         // invariant => if we save liquidity to tick clear pool liquidity
 180 |     |         if ((tickToSave != (params.zeroForOne ? params.lower : params.upper))) {
 181 |     |             tick.liquidityDelta += int128(pool.liquidity);
 182 |     |             tick.liquidityAbsolute += pool.liquidity;
 183 |     |             emit SyncLimitLiquidity(pool.liquidity, tickToSave, params.zeroForOne);
 184 |     |             pool.liquidity = 0;
 185 |     |         }
 186 |     |         ticks[tickToSave].limit = tick;
 187 |     |         return pool;
 188 |     |     }
 189 |     | 
 190 |     |     function remove(
 191 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 192 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 193 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
 194 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 195 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 196 |     |     ) internal {
 197 |     |         // set ticks based on claim and zeroForOne
 198 |     |         int24 lower = params.zeroForOne ? params.claim : cache.position.lower;
 199 |     |         int24 upper = params.zeroForOne ? cache.position.upper : params.claim;
 200 |     |         {    
 201 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickLower = ticks[lower].limit;
 202 |     |             
 203 |     |             if (cache.removeLower) {
 204 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 205 |     |                     tickLower.liquidityDelta -= int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 206 |     |                 } else {
 207 |     |                     tickLower.liquidityDelta += int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 208 |     |                 }
 209 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickLower.liquidityAbsolute, cache.liquidityBurned, 'TSL-1');
 210 |     |                 tickLower.liquidityAbsolute -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 211 |     |                 ticks[lower].limit = tickLower;
 212 |     |                 clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, lower);
 213 |     |             }
 214 |     |         }
 215 |     |         {
 216 |     |             PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick memory tickUpper = ticks[upper].limit;
 217 |     |             if (cache.removeUpper) {
 218 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
 219 |     |                     tickUpper.liquidityDelta += int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 220 |     |                 } else {
 221 |     |                     tickUpper.liquidityDelta -= int128(cache.liquidityBurned);
 222 |     |                 }
 223 |     |                 EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute, cache.liquidityBurned, 'TSL-2');
 224 |     |                 tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute -= cache.liquidityBurned;
 225 |     |                 ticks[upper].limit = tickUpper;
 226 |     |                 clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, upper);
 227 |     |             }
 228 |     |         }
 229 |     |     }
 230 |     | 
 231 |     |      function unlock(
 232 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 233 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory pool,
 234 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 235 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 236 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 237 |     |     ) internal returns (
 238 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory,
 239 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitPoolState memory
 240 |     |     )
 241 |     |     {
 242 |     |         if (pool.liquidity > 0) return (cache, pool);
 243 |     | 
 244 |     |         (int24 startTick,) = TickMap.roundHalf(pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants, pool.price);
 245 |     | 
 246 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 247 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = TickMap.next(tickMap, startTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, true);
 248 |     |             if (pool.tickAtPrice < ConstantProduct.maxTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
 249 |     |                 EpochMap.set(pool.tickAtPrice, zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 250 |     |             }
 251 |     |         } else {
 252 |     |             /// @dev - roundedUp true since liquidity could be equal to the current pool tickAtPrice
 253 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = TickMap.previous(tickMap, startTick, cache.constants.tickSpacing, true);
 254 |     |             if (pool.tickAtPrice > ConstantProduct.minTick(cache.constants.tickSpacing)) {
 255 |     |                 EpochMap.set(pool.tickAtPrice, zeroForOne, cache.state.epoch, tickMap, cache.constants);
 256 |     |             }
 257 |     |         }
 258 |     | 
 259 |     |         // increment pool liquidity
 260 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertPositiveLiquidityOnUnlock(ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.liquidityDelta);
 261 |     |         pool.liquidity += uint128(ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.liquidityDelta);
 262 |     |         int24 tickToClear = pool.tickAtPrice;
 263 |     |         uint160 tickPriceAt = ticks[pool.tickAtPrice].limit.priceAt;
 264 |     | 
 265 |     |         if (tickPriceAt == 0) {
 266 |     |             // if full tick crossed
 267 |     |             pool.price = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(pool.tickAtPrice, cache.constants);
 268 |     |         } else {
 269 |     |             // if half tick crossed
 270 |     |             pool.price = tickPriceAt;
 271 |     |             pool.tickAtPrice = ConstantProduct.getTickAtPrice(tickPriceAt, cache.constants);
 272 |     |         }
 273 |     | 
 274 |     |         // zero out tick
 275 |     |         ticks[tickToClear].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 276 |     |         clear(ticks, cache.constants, tickMap, tickToClear);
 277 |     | 
 278 |     |         return (cache, pool);
 279 |     |     }
 280 |     | 
 281 |     |     function clear(
 282 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 283 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 284 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 285 |     |         int24 tickToClear
 286 |     |     ) internal {
 287 |     |         if (_empty(ticks[tickToClear])) {
 288 |     |             if (tickToClear != ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing) &&
 289 |     |                 tickToClear != ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing)) {
 290 |     |                 ticks[tickToClear].limit = PoolsharkStructs.LimitTick(0,0,0);
 291 |     |                 TickMap.unset(tickMap, tickToClear, constants.tickSpacing);
 292 |     |             }
 293 |     |         }
 294 |     |     }
 295 |     | 
 296 |     |     function _empty(
 297 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.Tick memory tick
 298 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 299 |     |         bool
 300 |     |     ) {
 301 |     |         if (tick.limit.liquidityAbsolute != 0) {
 302 |     |             return false;
 303 |     |         }
 304 |     |         return true;
 305 |     |     }
 306 |     | }
 307 |     |

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../../interfaces/IPositionERC1155.sol';
   6 |     | import '../LimitPositions.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../utils/Collect.sol';
   8 |     | import '../../utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | library BurnLimitCall {
  11 |     |     event BurnLimit(
  12 |     |         address indexed to,
  13 |     |         uint32 positionId,
  14 |     |         int24 lower,
  15 |     |         int24 upper,
  16 |     |         int24 oldClaim,
  17 |     |         int24 newClaim,
  18 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  19 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
  20 |     |         uint128 tokenInClaimed,
  21 |     |         uint128 tokenOutBurned
  22 |     |     );
  23 |     | 
  24 |     |     function perform(
  25 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  26 |     |             storage positions,
  27 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  28 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  29 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  30 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
  31 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
  32 |     |     ) internal {
  33 |     |         // check for invalid receiver
  34 |     |         if (params.to == address(0))
  35 |     |             require(false, 'CollectToZeroAddress()');
  36 |     | 
  37 |     |         // initialize cache
  38 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  39 |     |         cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |         // check positionId owner
  42 |     |         if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  43 |     |             require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  44 |     |         
  45 |     |         // update position
  46 |     |         (
  47 |     |             params,
  48 |     |             cache
  49 |     |         ) = LimitPositions.update(
  50 |     |             ticks,
  51 |     |             tickMap,
  52 |     |             cache,
  53 |     |             params
  54 |     |         );
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |         // save position before transfer
  57 |     |         if ((params.zeroForOne ? params.claim != cache.position.upper
  58 |     |                                : params.claim != cache.position.lower)) {
  59 |     |             if (cache.position.liquidity > 0) {
  60 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  61 |     |                     cache.position.lower = params.claim;
  62 |     |                 } else {
  63 |     |                     cache.position.upper = params.claim;
  64 |     |                 }
  65 |     |                 positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
  66 |     |             } else {
  67 |     |                 IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  68 |     |                 delete positions[params.positionId];
  69 |     |             }
  70 |     |         } else {
  71 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  72 |     |             delete positions[params.positionId];
  73 |     |         }
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |         // save state before transfer call
  76 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
  77 |     |         
  78 |     |         cache = Collect.burnLimit(
  79 |     |             cache,
  80 |     |             params
  81 |     |         );
  82 |     |     }
  83 |     | 
  84 |     |     function save(
  85 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
  86 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  87 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  88 |     |     ) internal {
  89 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
  90 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
  91 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
  92 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  93 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
  94 |     |         } else {
  95 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  96 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
  97 |     |         }
  98 |     |     }
  99 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/limit/pool/MintLimitCall.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../LimitPositions.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../utils/Collect.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   8 |     | 
   9 |     | library MintLimitCall {
  10 |     |     event MintLimit(
  11 |     |         address indexed to,
  12 |     |         int24 lower,
  13 |     |         int24 upper,
  14 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  15 |     |         uint32 positionId,
  16 |     |         uint32 epochLast,
  17 |     |         uint128 amountIn,
  18 |     |         uint128 amountFilled,
  19 |     |         uint128 liquidityMinted
  20 |     |     );
  21 |     | 
  22 |     |     event SyncLimitPool(
  23 |     |         uint160 price,
  24 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
  25 |     |         uint32 epoch,
  26 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice,
  27 |     |         bool isPool0
  28 |     |     );
  29 |     | 
  30 |     |     function perform(
  31 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  32 |     |             storage positions,
  33 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  34 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  35 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  36 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  37 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  38 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  39 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  40 |     |     ) internal {
  41 |     |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
  42 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  43 |     |                 // check for balance held
  44 |     |                 require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  45 |     |             cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  46 |     |         }
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  49 |     | 
  50 |     |         // resize position if necessary
  51 |     |         (params, cache) = LimitPositions.resize(
  52 |     |             ticks,
  53 |     |             samples,
  54 |     |             rangeTickMap,
  55 |     |             limitTickMap,
  56 |     |             params,
  57 |     |             cache
  58 |     |         );
  59 |     | 
  60 |     |         // save state for reentrancy safety
  61 |     |         save(cache, globalState, !params.zeroForOne);
  62 |     | 
  63 |     |         // transfer in token amount
  64 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferIn(
  65 |     |                                  params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0 
  66 |     |                                                    : cache.constants.token1,
  67 |     |                                  params.amount + cache.swapCache.input
  68 |     |                                 );
  69 |     |         // transfer out if swap output 
  70 |     |         if (cache.swapCache.output > 0) {
  71 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceeded(
  72 |     |                 (params.zeroForOne ? balance(cache.constants.token1) : balance(cache.constants.token0)),
  73 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
  74 |     |             );
  75 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(
  76 |     |                 params.to,
  77 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1 
  78 |     |                                   : cache.constants.token0,
  79 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
  80 |     |             );
  81 |     |         }
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |         // mint position if amount is left
  84 |     |         if (params.amount > 0 && cache.liquidityMinted > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
  85 |     |             // check if new position created
  86 |     |             if (params.positionId == 0 ||                       // new position
  87 |     |                     params.lower != cache.position.lower ||     // lower mismatch
  88 |     |                     params.upper != cache.position.upper) {     // upper mismatch
  89 |     |                 LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory newPosition;
  90 |     |                 newPosition.lower = params.lower;
  91 |     |                 newPosition.upper = params.upper;
  92 |     |                 // use new position in cache
  93 |     |                 cache.position = newPosition;
  94 |     |                 params.positionId = cache.state.positionIdNext;
  95 |     |                 cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
  96 |     |             }
  97 |     |             cache.pool = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1;
  98 |     |             // bump to the next tick if there is no liquidity
  99 |     |             if (cache.pool.liquidity == 0) {
 100 |     |                 /// @dev - this makes sure to have liquidity unlocked if undercutting
 101 |     |                 (cache, cache.pool) = LimitTicks.unlock(cache, cache.pool, ticks, limitTickMap, params.zeroForOne);
 102 |     |             }
 103 |     | 
 104 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 105 |     |                 uint160 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 106 |     |                 if (priceLower <= cache.pool.price) {
 107 |     |                     // save liquidity if active
 108 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 109 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 110 |     |                     }
 111 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceLower;
 112 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.lower;
 113 |     |                     /// @auditor - double check liquidity is set correctly for this in insertSingle
 114 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 115 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 116 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 117 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 118 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 119 |     |                 }
 120 |     |             } else {
 121 |     |                 uint160 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 122 |     |                 if (priceUpper >= cache.pool.price) {
 123 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 124 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 125 |     |                     }
 126 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceUpper;
 127 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.upper;
 128 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 129 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 130 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 131 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 132 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 133 |     |                 }
 134 |     |             }
 135 |     |             (cache.pool, cache.position) = LimitPositions.add(
 136 |     |                 cache,
 137 |     |                 ticks,
 138 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 139 |     |                 params
 140 |     |             );
 141 |     | 
 142 |     |             // save position to storage
 143 |     |             positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
 144 |     | 
 145 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool : cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 146 |     | 
 147 |     |             emit MintLimit(
 148 |     |                 params.to,
 149 |     |                 params.lower,
 150 |     |                 params.upper,
 151 |     |                 params.zeroForOne,
 152 |     |                 params.positionId,
 153 |     |                 cache.position.epochLast,
 154 |     |                 uint128(params.amount + cache.swapCache.input),
 155 |     |                 uint128(cache.swapCache.output),
 156 |     |                 uint128(cache.liquidityMinted)
 157 |     |             );
 158 |     |         }
 159 |     | 
 160 |     |         // save lp side for safe reentrancy
 161 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
 162 |     |     }
 163 |     | 
 164 |     |     function balance(
 165 |     |         address token
 166 |     |     ) private view returns (uint256) {
 167 |     |         (
 168 |     |             bool success,
 169 |     |             bytes memory data
 170 |     |         ) = token.staticcall(
 171 |     |                                     abi.encodeWithSelector(
 172 |     |                                         IERC20Minimal.balanceOf.selector,
 173 |     |                                         address(this)
 174 |     |                                     )
 175 |     |                                 );
 176 |     |         require(success && data.length >= 32);
 177 |     |         return abi.decode(data, (uint256));
 178 |     |     }
 179 |     | 
 180 |     |     function save(
 181 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache,
 182 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 183 |     |         bool zeroForOne
 184 |     |     ) internal {
 185 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
 186 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
 187 |     |         globalState.positionIdNext = cache.state.positionIdNext;
 188 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
 189 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 190 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
 191 |     |         } else {
 192 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 193 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
 194 |     |         }
 195 |     |     }
 196 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/math/ConstantProduct.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import './OverflowMath.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   7 |     | 
   8 |     | /// @notice Math library that facilitates ranged liquidity calculations.
   9 |     | library ConstantProduct {
  10 | *   |     uint256 internal constant Q96 = 0x1000000000000000000000000;
  11 |     | 
  12 |     |     struct PriceBounds {
  13 |     |         uint160 min;
  14 |     |         uint160 max;
  15 |     |     }
  16 |     | 
  17 |     |     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
  18 |     |     ///////////////////////// DYDX MATH /////////////////////////
  19 |     |     /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
  20 |     | 
  21 |     |     function getDy(
  22 |     |         uint256 liquidity,
  23 |     |         uint256 priceLower,
  24 |     |         uint256 priceUpper,
  25 |     |         bool roundUp
  26 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 dy) {
  27 |     |         unchecked {
  28 |     |             if (liquidity == 0) return 0;
  29 |     |             if (roundUp) {
  30 |     |                 dy = OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(liquidity, priceUpper - priceLower, Q96);
  31 |     |             } else {
  32 |     |                 dy = OverflowMath.mulDiv(liquidity, priceUpper - priceLower, Q96);
  33 |     |             }
  34 |     |         }
  35 |     |     }
  36 |     | 
  37 |     |     function getDx(
  38 |     |         uint256 liquidity,
  39 |     |         uint256 priceLower,
  40 |     |         uint256 priceUpper,
  41 |     |         bool roundUp
  42 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 dx) {
  43 |     |         unchecked {
  44 |     |             if (liquidity == 0) return 0;
  45 |     |             if (roundUp) {
  46 |     |                 dx = OverflowMath.divRoundingUp(
  47 |     |                         OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(
  48 |     |                             liquidity << 96, 
  49 |     |                             priceUpper - priceLower,
  50 |     |                             priceUpper
  51 |     |                         ),
  52 |     |                         priceLower
  53 |     |                 );
  54 |     |             } else {
  55 |     |                 dx = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
  56 |     |                         liquidity << 96,
  57 |     |                         priceUpper - priceLower,
  58 |     |                         priceUpper
  59 |     |                 ) / priceLower;
  60 |     |             }
  61 |     |         }
  62 |     |     }
  63 |     | 
  64 | *   |     function getLiquidityForAmounts(
  65 |     |         uint256 priceLower,
  66 |     |         uint256 priceUpper,
  67 |     |         uint256 currentPrice,
  68 |     |         uint256 dy,
  69 |     |         uint256 dx
  70 | *   |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 liquidity) {
  71 |     |         unchecked {
  72 | *   |             if (priceUpper <= currentPrice) {
  73 | *   |                 liquidity = OverflowMath.mulDiv(dy, Q96, priceUpper - priceLower);
  74 | *   |             } else if (currentPrice <= priceLower) {
  75 | *   |                 liquidity = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
  76 | *   |                     dx,
  77 | *   |                     OverflowMath.mulDiv(priceLower, priceUpper, Q96),
  78 | *   |                     priceUpper - priceLower
  79 |     |                 );
  80 | *   |             } else {
  81 | *   |                 uint256 liquidity0 = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
  82 | *   |                     dx,
  83 | *   |                     OverflowMath.mulDiv(priceUpper, currentPrice, Q96),
  84 | *   |                     priceUpper - currentPrice
  85 |     |                 );
  86 | *   |                 uint256 liquidity1 = OverflowMath.mulDiv(dy, Q96, currentPrice - priceLower);
  87 | *   |                 liquidity = liquidity0 < liquidity1 ? liquidity0 : liquidity1;
  88 |     |             }
  89 |     |         }
  90 |     |     }
  91 |     | 
  92 |     |     function getAmountsForLiquidity(
  93 |     |         uint256 priceLower,
  94 |     |         uint256 priceUpper,
  95 |     |         uint256 currentPrice,
  96 |     |         uint256 liquidityAmount,
  97 |     |         bool roundUp
  98 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint128 token0amount, uint128 token1amount) {
  99 |     |         if (priceUpper <= currentPrice) {
 100 |     |             token1amount = uint128(getDy(liquidityAmount, priceLower, priceUpper, roundUp));
 101 |     |         } else if (currentPrice <= priceLower) {
 102 |     |             token0amount = uint128(getDx(liquidityAmount, priceLower, priceUpper, roundUp));
 103 |     |         } else {
 104 |     |             token0amount = uint128(getDx(liquidityAmount, currentPrice, priceUpper, roundUp));
 105 |     |             token1amount = uint128(getDy(liquidityAmount, priceLower, currentPrice, roundUp));
 106 |     |         }
 107 |     |         if (token0amount > uint128(type(int128).max)) require(false, 'AmountsOutOfBounds()');
 108 |     |         if (token1amount > uint128(type(int128).max)) require(false, 'AmountsOutOfBounds()');
 109 |     |     }
 110 |     | 
 111 |     |     function getNewPrice(
 112 |     |         uint256 price,
 113 |     |         uint256 liquidity,
 114 |     |         uint256 amount,
 115 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
 116 |     |         bool exactIn
 117 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 118 |     |         uint256 newPrice
 119 |     |     ) {
 120 |     |         if (exactIn) {
 121 |     |             if (zeroForOne) {
 122 |     |                 uint256 liquidityPadded = liquidity << 96;
 123 |     |                 newPrice = OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(
 124 |     |                         liquidityPadded,
 125 |     |                         price,
 126 |     |                         liquidityPadded + price * amount
 127 |     |                     );
 128 |     |             } else {
 129 |     |                 newPrice = price + (amount << 96) / liquidity;
 130 |     |             }
 131 |     |         } else {
 132 |     |             if (zeroForOne) {
 133 |     |                 newPrice = price - 
 134 |     |                         OverflowMath.divRoundingUp(amount << 96, liquidity);
 135 |     |             } else {
 136 |     |                 uint256 liquidityPadded = uint256(liquidity) << 96;
 137 |     |                 newPrice = OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(
 138 |     |                         liquidityPadded, 
 139 |     |                         price,
 140 |     |                         liquidityPadded - uint256(price) * amount
 141 |     |                 );
 142 |     |             }
 143 |     |         }
 144 |     |     }
 145 |     | 
 146 |     |     function getPrice(
 147 |     |         uint256 sqrtPrice
 148 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 price) {
 149 |     |         if (sqrtPrice >= 2 ** 48)
 150 |     |             price = OverflowMath.mulDiv(sqrtPrice, sqrtPrice, 2 ** 96);
 151 |     |         else
 152 |     |             price = sqrtPrice;
 153 |     |     }

 159 | *   |     int24 internal constant MIN_TICK = -887272;   /// @dev - tick for price of 2^-128
 160 | *   |     int24 internal constant MAX_TICK = -MIN_TICK; /// @dev - tick for price of 2^128
 161 |     |

 163 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 164 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 165 |     |         int24 tick
 166 |     |     ) {
 167 |     |         return MIN_TICK / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
 168 |     |     }
 169 |     | 
 170 | *   |     function maxTick(
 171 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 172 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 173 | *   |         int24 tick
 174 |     |     ) {
 175 | *   |         return MAX_TICK / tickSpacing * tickSpacing;
 176 |     |     }
