 178 |     |     function priceBounds(
 179 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 180 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 181 |     |         uint160,
 182 |     |         uint160
 183 |     |     ) {
 184 |     |         return (minPrice(tickSpacing), maxPrice(tickSpacing));
 185 |     |     }
 186 |     | 
 187 |     |     function minPrice(
 188 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 189 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 190 |     |         uint160 price
 191 |     |     ) {
 192 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables  memory constants;
 193 |     |         constants.tickSpacing = tickSpacing;
 194 |     |         return getPriceAtTick(minTick(tickSpacing), constants);
 195 |     |     }
 196 |     | 
 197 |     |     function maxPrice(
 198 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 199 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 200 |     |         uint160 price
 201 |     |     ) {
 202 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables  memory constants;
 203 |     |         constants.tickSpacing = tickSpacing;
 204 |     |         return getPriceAtTick(maxTick(tickSpacing), constants);
 205 |     |     }
 206 |     | 
 207 |     |     function checkTicks(
 208 |     |         int24 lower,
 209 |     |         int24 upper,
 210 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
 211 |     |     ) internal pure
 212 |     |     {
 213 |     |         if (lower < minTick(tickSpacing)) require (false, 'LowerTickOutOfBounds()');
 214 |     |         if (upper > maxTick(tickSpacing)) require (false, 'UpperTickOutOfBounds()');
 215 |     |         if (lower % tickSpacing != 0) require (false, 'LowerTickOutsideTickSpacing()');
 216 |     |         if (upper % tickSpacing != 0) require (false, 'UpperTickOutsideTickSpacing()');
 217 |     |         if (lower >= upper) require (false, 'LowerUpperTickOrderInvalid()');
 218 |     |     }
 219 |     | 
 220 |     |     function checkPrice(
 221 |     |         uint160 price,
 222 |     |         PriceBounds memory bounds
 223 |     |     ) internal pure {
 224 |     |         if (price < bounds.min || price >= bounds.max) require (false, 'PriceOutOfBounds()');
 225 |     |     }
 226 |     | 
 227 |     |     /// @notice Calculates sqrt(1.0001^tick) * 2^96.
 228 |     |     /// @dev Throws if |tick| > max tick.
 229 |     |     /// @param tick The input tick for the above formula.
 230 |     |     /// @return price Fixed point Q64.96 number representing the sqrt of the ratio of the two assets (token1/token0)
 231 |     |     /// at the given tick.
 232 | *   |     function getPriceAtTick(
 233 |     |         int24 tick,
 234 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 235 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 236 | *   |         uint160 price
 237 | *   |     ) {
 238 | *   |         uint256 absTick = tick < 0 ? uint256(-int256(tick)) : uint256(int256(tick));
 239 | *   |         if (absTick > uint256(uint24(maxTick(constants.tickSpacing)))) require (false, 'TickOutOfBounds()');
 240 | *   |         unchecked {
 241 | *   |             uint256 ratio = absTick & 0x1 != 0
 242 |     |                 ? 0xfffcb933bd6fad37aa2d162d1a594001
 243 | *   |                 : 0x100000000000000000000000000000000;
 244 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x2 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xfff97272373d413259a46990580e213a) >> 128;
 245 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x4 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xfff2e50f5f656932ef12357cf3c7fdcc) >> 128;
 246 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x8 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xffe5caca7e10e4e61c3624eaa0941cd0) >> 128;
 247 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x10 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xffcb9843d60f6159c9db58835c926644) >> 128;
 248 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x20 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xff973b41fa98c081472e6896dfb254c0) >> 128;
 249 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x40 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xff2ea16466c96a3843ec78b326b52861) >> 128;
 250 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x80 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xfe5dee046a99a2a811c461f1969c3053) >> 128;
 251 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x100 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xfcbe86c7900a88aedcffc83b479aa3a4) >> 128;
 252 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x200 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xf987a7253ac413176f2b074cf7815e54) >> 128;
 253 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x400 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xf3392b0822b70005940c7a398e4b70f3) >> 128;
 254 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x800 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xe7159475a2c29b7443b29c7fa6e889d9) >> 128;
 255 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x1000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xd097f3bdfd2022b8845ad8f792aa5825) >> 128;
 256 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x2000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0xa9f746462d870fdf8a65dc1f90e061e5) >> 128;
 257 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x4000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x70d869a156d2a1b890bb3df62baf32f7) >> 128;
 258 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x8000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x31be135f97d08fd981231505542fcfa6) >> 128;
 259 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x10000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x9aa508b5b7a84e1c677de54f3e99bc9) >> 128;
 260 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x20000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x5d6af8dedb81196699c329225ee604) >> 128;
 261 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x40000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x2216e584f5fa1ea926041bedfe98) >> 128;
 262 | *   |             if (absTick & 0x80000 != 0) ratio = (ratio * 0x48a170391f7dc42444e8fa2) >> 128;
 263 |     | 
 264 | *   |             if (tick > 0) ratio = type(uint256).max / ratio;
 265 |     |             // This divides by 1<<32 rounding up to go from a Q128.128 to a Q128.96.
 266 |     |             // We then downcast because we know the result always fits within 160 bits due to our tick input constraint.
 267 |     |             // We round up in the division so getTickAtPrice of the output price is always consistent.
 268 | *   |             price = uint160((ratio >> 32) + (ratio % (1 << 32) == 0 ? 0 : 1));
 269 |     |         }
 270 |     |     }
 271 |     | 
 272 |     |     /// @notice Calculates the greatest tick value such that getRatioAtTick(tick) <= ratio.
 273 |     |     /// @param price The sqrt ratio for which to compute the tick as a Q64.96.
 274 |     |     /// @return tick The greatest tick for which the ratio is less than or equal to the input ratio.
 275 |     |     function getTickAtPrice(
 276 |     |         uint160 price,
 277 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables  memory constants
 278 |     |     ) internal pure returns (int24 tick) {
 279 |     |         // Second inequality must be < because the price can never reach the price at the max tick.
 280 |     |         if (price < constants.bounds.min || price > constants.bounds.max)
 281 |     |             require (false, 'PriceOutOfBounds()');
 282 |     |         uint256 ratio = uint256(price) << 32;
 283 |     | 
 284 |     |         uint256 r = ratio;
 285 |     |         uint256 msb = 0;
 286 |     | 
 287 |     |         assembly {
 288 |     |             let f := shl(7, gt(r, 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF))
 289 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 290 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 291 |     |         }
 292 |     |         assembly {
 293 |     |             let f := shl(6, gt(r, 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF))
 294 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 295 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 296 |     |         }
 297 |     |         assembly {
 298 |     |             let f := shl(5, gt(r, 0xFFFFFFFF))
 299 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 300 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 301 |     |         }
 302 |     |         assembly {
 303 |     |             let f := shl(4, gt(r, 0xFFFF))
 304 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 305 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 306 |     |         }
 307 |     |         assembly {
 308 |     |             let f := shl(3, gt(r, 0xFF))
 309 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 310 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 311 |     |         }
 312 |     |         assembly {
 313 |     |             let f := shl(2, gt(r, 0xF))
 314 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 315 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 316 |     |         }
 317 |     |         assembly {
 318 |     |             let f := shl(1, gt(r, 0x3))
 319 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 320 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 321 |     |         }
 322 |     |         assembly {
 323 |     |             let f := gt(r, 0x1)
 324 |     |             msb := or(msb, f)
 325 |     |         }
 326 |     | 
 327 |     |         if (msb >= 128) r = ratio >> (msb - 127);
 328 |     |         else r = ratio << (127 - msb);
 329 |     | 
 330 |     |         int256 log_2 = (int256(msb) - 128) << 64;
 331 |     | 
 332 |     |         assembly {
 333 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 334 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 335 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(63, f))
 336 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 337 |     |         }
 338 |     |         assembly {
 339 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 340 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 341 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(62, f))
 342 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 343 |     |         }
 344 |     |         assembly {
 345 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 346 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 347 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(61, f))
 348 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 349 |     |         }
 350 |     |         assembly {
 351 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 352 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 353 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(60, f))
 354 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 355 |     |         }
 356 |     |         assembly {
 357 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 358 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 359 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(59, f))
 360 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 361 |     |         }
 362 |     |         assembly {
 363 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 364 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 365 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(58, f))
 366 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 367 |     |         }
 368 |     |         assembly {
 369 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 370 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 371 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(57, f))
 372 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 373 |     |         }
 374 |     |         assembly {
 375 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 376 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 377 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(56, f))
 378 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 379 |     |         }
 380 |     |         assembly {
 381 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 382 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 383 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(55, f))
 384 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 385 |     |         }
 386 |     |         assembly {
 387 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 388 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 389 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(54, f))
 390 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 391 |     |         }
 392 |     |         assembly {
 393 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 394 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 395 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(53, f))
 396 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 397 |     |         }
 398 |     |         assembly {
 399 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 400 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 401 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(52, f))
 402 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 403 |     |         }
 404 |     |         assembly {
 405 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 406 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 407 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(51, f))
 408 |     |             r := shr(f, r)
 409 |     |         }
 410 |     |         assembly {
 411 |     |             r := shr(127, mul(r, r))
 412 |     |             let f := shr(128, r)
 413 |     |             log_2 := or(log_2, shl(50, f))
 414 |     |         }
 415 |     | 
 416 |     |         int256 log_sqrt10001 = log_2 * 255738958999603826347141; // 128.128 number
 417 |     | 
 418 |     |         int24 tickLow = int24((log_sqrt10001 - 3402992956809132418596140100660247210) >> 128);
 419 |     |         int24 tickHi = int24((log_sqrt10001 + 291339464771989622907027621153398088495) >> 128);
 420 |     | 
 421 |     |         tick = tickLow == tickHi ? tickLow : getPriceAtTick(tickHi, constants) <= price
 422 |     |             ? tickHi
 423 |     |             : tickLow;
 424 |     |     }
 425 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/math/OverflowMath.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | /// @notice Math library that facilitates multiplication and division that can have overflow of an intermediate value without any loss of precision.
   5 |     | library OverflowMath {
   6 |     | 
   7 |     |     // @dev no underflow or overflow checks
   8 |     |     function divRoundingUp(uint256 x, uint256 y) internal pure returns (uint256 z) {
   9 |     |         assembly {
  10 |     |             z := add(div(x, y), gt(mod(x, y), 0))
  11 |     |         }
  12 |     |     }
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     /// @notice Calculates floor(a×b÷denominator) with full precision - throws if result overflows an uint256 or denominator == 0.
  15 |     |     /// @param a The multiplicand.
  16 |     |     /// @param b The multiplier.
  17 |     |     /// @param denominator The divisor.
  18 |     |     /// @return result The 256-bit result.
  19 |     |     /// @dev Credit to Remco Bloemen under MIT license https://xn--2-umb.com/21/muldiv.
  20 | *   |     function mulDiv(
  21 |     |         uint256 a,
  22 |     |         uint256 b,
  23 |     |         uint256 denominator
  24 | *   |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 result) {
  25 |     |         unchecked {
  26 |     |             // 512-bit multiply [prod1 prod0] = a * b.
  27 |     |             // Compute the product mod 2**256 and mod 2**256 - 1,
  28 |     |             // then use the Chinese Remainder Theorem to reconstruct
  29 |     |             // the 512 bit result. The result is stored in two 256
  30 |     |             // variables such that product = prod1 * 2**256 + prod0.
  31 | *   |             uint256 prod0; // Least significant 256 bits of the product.
  32 | *   |             uint256 prod1; // Most significant 256 bits of the product.
  33 | *   |             assembly {
  34 | *   |                 let mm := mulmod(a, b, not(0))
  35 | *   |                 prod0 := mul(a, b)
  36 | *   |                 prod1 := sub(sub(mm, prod0), lt(mm, prod0))
  37 |     |             }
  38 |     |             // Handle non-overflow cases, 256 by 256 division.
  39 | *   |             if (prod1 == 0) {
  40 | *   |                 require(denominator > 0);
  41 |     |                 assembly {
  42 | *   |                     result := div(prod0, denominator)
  43 |     |                 }
  44 | *   |                 return result;
  45 |     |             }
  46 |     |             // Make sure the result is less than 2**256 -
  47 |     |             // also prevents denominator == 0.
  48 | *   |             require(denominator > prod1);
  49 |     |             ///////////////////////////////////////////////
  50 |     |             // 512 by 256 division.
  51 |     |             ///////////////////////////////////////////////
  52 |     |             // Make division exact by subtracting the remainder from [prod1 prod0] -
  53 |     |             // compute remainder using mulmod.
  54 | *   |             uint256 remainder;
  55 |     |             assembly {
  56 | *   |                 remainder := mulmod(a, b, denominator)
  57 |     |             }
  58 |     |             // Subtract 256 bit number from 512 bit number.
  59 |     |             assembly {
  60 | *   |                 prod1 := sub(prod1, gt(remainder, prod0))
  61 | *   |                 prod0 := sub(prod0, remainder)
  62 |     |             }
  63 |     |             // Factor powers of two out of denominator -
  64 |     |             // compute largest power of two divisor of denominator
  65 |     |             // (always >= 1).
  66 | *   |             uint256 twos = uint256(-int256(denominator)) & denominator;
  67 |     |             // Divide denominator by power of two.
  68 |     |             assembly {
  69 | *   |                 denominator := div(denominator, twos)
  70 |     |             }
  71 |     |             // Divide [prod1 prod0] by the factors of two.
  72 |     |             assembly {
  73 | *   |                 prod0 := div(prod0, twos)
  74 |     |             }
  75 |     |             // Shift in bits from prod1 into prod0. For this we need
  76 |     |             // to flip `twos` such that it is 2**256 / twos -
  77 |     |             // if twos is zero, then it becomes one.
  78 |     |             assembly {
  79 | *   |                 twos := add(div(sub(0, twos), twos), 1)
  80 |     |             }
  81 | *   |             prod0 |= prod1 * twos;
  82 |     |             // Invert denominator mod 2**256 -
  83 |     |             // now that denominator is an odd number, it has an inverse
  84 |     |             // modulo 2**256 such that denominator * inv = 1 mod 2**256.
  85 |     |             // Compute the inverse by starting with a seed that is correct
  86 |     |             // for four bits. That is, denominator * inv = 1 mod 2**4.
  87 | *   |             uint256 inv = (3 * denominator) ^ 2;
  88 |     |             // Now use Newton-Raphson iteration to improve the precision.
  89 |     |             // Thanks to Hensel's lifting lemma, this also works in modular
  90 |     |             // arithmetic, doubling the correct bits in each step.
  91 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**8.
  92 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**16.
  93 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**32.
  94 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**64.
  95 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**128.
  96 | *   |             inv *= 2 - denominator * inv; // Inverse mod 2**256.
  97 |     |             // Because the division is now exact we can divide by multiplying
  98 |     |             // with the modular inverse of denominator. This will give us the
  99 |     |             // correct result modulo 2**256. Since the precoditions guarantee
 100 |     |             // that the outcome is less than 2**256, this is the final result.
 101 |     |             // We don't need to compute the high bits of the result and prod1
 102 |     |             // is no longer required.
 103 | *   |             result = prod0 * inv;
 104 | *   |             return result;
 105 |     |         }
 106 |     |     }
 107 |     | 
 108 |     |     /// @notice Calculates ceil(a×b÷denominator) with full precision - throws if result overflows an uint256 or denominator == 0.
 109 |     |     /// @param a The multiplicand.
 110 |     |     /// @param b The multiplier.
 111 |     |     /// @param denominator The divisor.
 112 |     |     /// @return result The 256-bit result.
 113 |     |     function mulDivRoundingUp(
 114 |     |         uint256 a,
 115 |     |         uint256 b,
 116 |     |         uint256 denominator
 117 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 result) {
 118 |     |         result = mulDiv(a, b, denominator);
 119 |     |         unchecked {
 120 |     |             if (mulmod(a, b, denominator) != 0) {
 121 |     |                 if (result >= type(uint256).max) require (false, 'MaxUintExceeded()');
 122 |     |                 result++;
 123 |     |             }
 124 |     |         }
 125 |     |     }
 126 |     | }
 127 |     | 

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/pool/FeesCall.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
  5 |     | import '../../interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolManager.sol';
  6 |     | import '../utils/SafeTransfers.sol';
  7 |     | 
  8 |     | library FeesCall {
  9 |     | 
 10 |     |     // protocol fee ceilings
 11 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE = 1e4; // max protocol swap fee of 100%
 12 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE = 1e2; // max protocol fill fee of 1%
 13 |     | 
 14 |     |     // protocol fee flags
 15 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0 = 2**0;
 16 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1 = 2**1;
 17 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0 = 2**2;
 18 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1 = 2**3;
 19 |     | 
 20 |     |     /// @dev - LimitPoolManager (i.e. constants.owner) emits events in aggregate
 21 |     | 
 22 |     |     function perform(
 23 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 24 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.FeesParams memory params,
 25 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 26 |     |     ) internal returns (
 27 |     |         uint128 token0Fees,
 28 |     |         uint128 token1Fees
 29 |     |     ) {
 30 |     |         // swap fee token0
 31 |     |         if ((params.setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0) > 0) {
 32 |     |             if (params.protocolSwapFee0 > MAX_PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE)
 33 |     |                 require(false, 'ProtocolSwapFeeCeilingExceeded()');
 34 |     |             globalState.pool.protocolSwapFee0 = params.protocolSwapFee0;
 35 |     |         }
 36 |     |         // swap fee token1
 37 |     |         if ((params.setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1) > 0) {
 38 |     |             if (params.protocolSwapFee1 > MAX_PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE)
 39 |     |                 require(false, 'ProtocolSwapFeeCeilingExceeded()');
 40 |     |             globalState.pool.protocolSwapFee1 = params.protocolSwapFee1;
 41 |     |         }
 42 |     |         // fill fee token0
 43 |     |         if ((params.setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0) > 0) {
 44 |     |             if (params.protocolFillFee0 > MAX_PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE)
 45 |     |                 require(false, 'ProtocolFillFeeCeilingExceeded()');
 46 |     |             globalState.pool1.protocolFillFee = params.protocolFillFee0;
 47 |     |         }
 48 |     |         // fill fee token1
 49 |     |         if ((params.setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1) > 0) {
 50 |     |             if (params.protocolFillFee1 > MAX_PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE)
 51 |     |                 require(false, 'ProtocolFillFeeCeilingExceeded()');
 52 |     |             globalState.pool0.protocolFillFee = params.protocolFillFee1;
 53 |     |         }
 54 |     |         address feeTo = ILimitPoolManager(constants.owner).feeTo();
 55 |     | 
 56 |     |         // token0 fees stored on pool1 for swaps and fills
 57 |     |         token0Fees = globalState.pool1.protocolFees;
 58 |     |         // token1 fees stored on pool0 for swaps and fills
 59 |     |         token1Fees = globalState.pool0.protocolFees;
 60 |     |         globalState.pool0.protocolFees = 0;
 61 |     |         globalState.pool1.protocolFees = 0;
 62 |     | 
 63 |     |         if (token0Fees > 0)
 64 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(feeTo, constants.token0, token0Fees);
 65 |     |         if (token1Fees > 0)
 66 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(feeTo, constants.token1, token1Fees);
 67 |     | 
 68 |     |         return (token0Fees, token1Fees);
 69 |     |     }
 70 |     | }
 71 |     |

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/callbacks/ILimitPoolSwapCallback.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../interfaces/IERC20Minimal.sol';
   7 |     | import '../Ticks.sol';
   8 |     | import '../utils/Collect.sol';
   9 |     | import '../utils/SafeTransfers.sol';
  10 |     | 
  11 |     | library SwapCall {
  12 |     |     event Swap(
  13 |     |         address indexed recipient,
  14 |     |         bool zeroForOne,
  15 |     |         uint256 amountIn,
  16 |     |         uint256 amountOut,
  17 |     |         uint160 price,
  18 |     |         uint128 liquidity,
  19 |     |         uint128 feeAmount,
  20 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice
  21 |     |     );
  22 |     | 
  23 |     |     function perform(
  24 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  25 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  26 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage rangeTickMap,
  27 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  28 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  29 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params,
  30 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
  31 |     |     ) internal returns (
  32 |     |         int256,
  33 |     |         int256
  34 |     |     ) {
  35 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  36 |     |         cache = Ticks.swap(
  37 |     |             ticks,
  38 |     |             samples,
  39 |     |             rangeTickMap,
  40 |     |             limitTickMap,
  41 |     |             params,
  42 |     |             cache
  43 |     |         );
  44 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
  45 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceeded(
  46 |     |             (params.zeroForOne ? balance(cache.constants.token1) : balance(cache.constants.token0)),
  47 |     |             cache.output
  48 |     |         );
  49 |     |         // transfer output amount
  50 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferOut(
  51 |     |             params.to, 
  52 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1
  53 |     |                               : cache.constants.token0,
  54 |     |             cache.output
  55 |     |         );
  56 |     | 
  57 |     |         // check balance and execute callback
  58 |     |         uint256 balanceStart = balance(params, cache);
  59 |     |         ILimitPoolSwapCallback(msg.sender).limitPoolSwapCallback(
  60 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? -int256(cache.input) : int256(cache.output),
  61 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? int256(cache.output) : -int256(cache.input),
  62 |     |             params.callbackData
  63 |     |         );
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |         // check balance requirements after callback
  66 |     |         if (balance(params, cache) < balanceStart + cache.input)
  67 |     |             require(false, 'SwapInputAmountTooLow()');
  68 |     | 
  69 |     |         return (
  70 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? 
  71 |     |                 (
  72 |     |                     -int256(cache.input),
  73 |     |                      int256(cache.output)
  74 |     |                 )
  75 |     |               : (
  76 |     |                      int256(cache.output),
  77 |     |                     -int256(cache.input)
  78 |     |                 )
  79 |     |         );
  80 |     |     }
  81 |     | 
  82 |     |     function save(
  83 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
  84 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  85 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  86 |     |     ) internal {
  87 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
  88 |     |         globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  89 |     |         if (zeroForOne)
  90 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
  91 |     |         else
  92 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
  93 |     |     }
  94 |     | 
  95 |     |     function balance(
  96 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapParams memory params,
  97 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache
  98 |     |     ) private view returns (uint256) {
  99 |     |         (
 100 |     |             bool success,
 101 |     |             bytes memory data
 102 |     |         ) = (params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0
 103 |     |                                : cache.constants.token1)
 104 |     |                                .staticcall(
 105 |     |                                     abi.encodeWithSelector(
 106 |     |                                         IERC20Minimal.balanceOf.selector,
 107 |     |                                         address(this)
 108 |     |                                     )
 109 |     |                                 );
 110 |     |         require(success && data.length >= 32);
 111 |     |         return abi.decode(data, (uint256));
 112 |     |     }
 113 |     | 
 114 |     |     function balance(
 115 |     |         address token
 116 |     |     ) private view returns (uint256) {
 117 |     |         (
 118 |     |             bool success,
 119 |     |             bytes memory data
 120 |     |         ) = token.staticcall(
 121 |     |                                     abi.encodeWithSelector(
 122 |     |                                         IERC20Minimal.balanceOf.selector,
 123 |     |                                         address(this)
 124 |     |                                     )
 125 |     |                                 );
 126 |     |         require(success && data.length >= 32);
 127 |     |         return abi.decode(data, (uint256));
 128 |     |     }
 129 |     | }

  14 |     | /// @notice Position management library for ranged liquidity.
  15 |     | library RangePositions {

  17 |     |     using SafeCast for uint128;
  18 |     |     using SafeCast for int256;
  19 |     |     using SafeCast for int128;
  20 |     | 
  21 |     |     error NotEnoughPositionLiquidity();
  22 |     |     error InvalidClaimTick();
  23 |     |     error LiquidityOverflow();
  24 |     |     error WrongTickClaimedAt();
  25 |     |     error NoLiquidityBeingAdded();
  26 |     |     error PositionNotUpdated();
  27 |     |     error InvalidLowerTick();
  28 |     |     error InvalidUpperTick();
  29 |     |     error InvalidPositionAmount();
  30 |     |     error InvalidPositionBoundsOrder();
  31 |     |     error NotImplementedYet();
  32 |     | 
  33 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q96 = 0x1000000000000000000000000;
  34 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q128 = 0x100000000000000000000000000000000;
  35 |     | 
  36 |     |     event BurnRange(
  37 |     |         address indexed recipient,
  38 |     |         uint256 indexed positionId,
  39 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
  40 |     |         int128 amount0,
  41 |     |         int128 amount1
  42 |     |     );
  43 |     | 
  44 |     |     event CompoundRange(
  45 |     |         uint32 indexed positionId,
  46 |     |         uint128 liquidityCompounded
  47 |     |     );
  48 |     | 
  49 |     |     function validate(
  50 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeParams memory params,
  51 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory cache
  52 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  53 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeParams memory,
  54 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory
  55 |     |     ) {
  56 |     |         RangeTicks.validate(cache.position.lower, cache.position.upper, cache.constants.tickSpacing);
  57 |     | 
  58 |     |         cache.liquidityMinted = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
  59 |     |             cache.priceLower,
  60 |     |             cache.priceUpper,
  61 |     |             cache.state.pool.price,
  62 |     |             params.amount1,
  63 |     |             params.amount0
  64 |     |         );
  65 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted == 0) require(false, 'NoLiquidityBeingAdded()');
  66 |     |         (params.amount0, params.amount1) = ConstantProduct.getAmountsForLiquidity(
  67 |     |             cache.priceLower,
  68 |     |             cache.priceUpper,
  69 |     |             cache.state.pool.price,
  70 |     |             cache.liquidityMinted,
  71 |     |             true
  72 |     |         );
  73 |     |         if (cache.liquidityMinted > uint128(type(int128).max)) require(false, 'LiquidityOverflow()');
  74 |     | 
  75 |     |         return (params, cache);
  76 |     |     }
  77 |     | 
  78 |     |     function add(
  79 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  80 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  81 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  82 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory cache,
  83 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeParams memory params
  84 |     |     ) internal returns (
  85 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory
  86 |     |     ) {
  87 |     |         if (params.amount0 == 0 && params.amount1 == 0) return cache;
  88 |     | 
  89 |     |         cache.state = RangeTicks.insert(
  90 |     |             ticks,
  91 |     |             samples,
  92 |     |             tickMap,
  93 |     |             cache.state,
  94 |     |             cache.constants,
  95 |     |             cache.position.lower,
  96 |     |             cache.position.upper,
  97 |     |             cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128()
  98 |     |         );
  99 |     |         (
 100 |     |             cache.position.feeGrowthInside0Last,
 101 |     |             cache.position.feeGrowthInside1Last
 102 |     |         ) = rangeFeeGrowth(
 103 |     |             ticks[cache.position.lower].range,
 104 |     |             ticks[cache.position.upper].range,
 105 |     |             cache.state,
 106 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 107 |     |             cache.position.upper
 108 |     |         );
 109 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 110 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).mint(
 111 |     |                 params.to,
 112 |     |                 params.positionId,
 113 |     |                 1,
 114 |     |                 cache.constants
 115 |     |             );
 116 |     |         }
 117 |     |         cache.position.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 118 |     |         return cache;
 119 |     |     }
 120 |     | 
 121 |     |     function remove(
 122 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 123 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
 124 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 125 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeParams memory params,
 126 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeCache memory cache
 127 |     |     ) internal returns (
 128 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeCache memory
 129 |     |     ) {
 130 |     |         cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.lower, cache.constants);
 131 |     |         cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.upper, cache.constants);
 132 |     |         cache.liquidityBurned = uint256(params.burnPercent) * cache.position.liquidity / 1e38;
 133 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned  == 0) {
 134 |     |             return cache;
 135 |     |         }
 136 |     |         if (cache.liquidityBurned > cache.position.liquidity) require(false, 'NotEnoughPositionLiquidity()');
 137 |     |         {
 138 |     |             uint128 amount0Removed; uint128 amount1Removed;
 139 |     |             (amount0Removed, amount1Removed) = ConstantProduct.getAmountsForLiquidity(
 140 |     |                 cache.priceLower,
 141 |     |                 cache.priceUpper,
 142 |     |                 cache.state.pool.price,
 143 |     |                 cache.liquidityBurned ,
 144 |     |                 false
 145 |     |             );
 146 |     |             cache.amount0 += amount0Removed.toInt128();
 147 |     |             cache.amount1 += amount1Removed.toInt128();
 148 |     |             cache.position.liquidity -= cache.liquidityBurned.toUint128();
 149 |     |         }
 150 |     |         cache.state = RangeTicks.remove(
 151 |     |             ticks,
 152 |     |             samples,
 153 |     |             tickMap,
 154 |     |             cache.state,
 155 |     |             cache.constants,
 156 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 157 |     |             cache.position.upper,
 158 |     |             uint128(cache.liquidityBurned)
 159 |     |         );
 160 |     |         emit BurnRange(
 161 |     |             params.to,
 162 |     |             params.positionId,
 163 |     |             uint128(cache.liquidityBurned),
 164 |     |             cache.amount0,
 165 |     |             cache.amount1
 166 |     |         );
 167 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0) {
 168 |     |             cache.position.feeGrowthInside0Last = 0;
 169 |     |             cache.position.feeGrowthInside1Last = 0;
 170 |     |             cache.position.lower = 0;
 171 |     |             cache.position.upper = 0;
 172 |     |         }
 173 |     |         return cache;
 174 |     |     }
 175 |     | 
 176 |     |     function compound(
 177 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 178 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 179 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
 180 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 181 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 182 |     |         RangePoolStructs.RangePosition memory position,
 183 |     |         RangePoolStructs.CompoundRangeParams memory params
 184 |     |     ) internal returns (
 185 |     |         RangePoolStructs.RangePosition memory,
 186 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory,
 187 |     |         int128,
 188 |     |         int128
 189 |     |     ) {
 190 |     |         // price tells you the ratio so you need to swap into the correct ratio and add liquidity
 191 |     |         uint256 liquidityAmount = ConstantProduct.getLiquidityForAmounts(
 192 |     |             params.priceLower,
 193 |     |             params.priceUpper,
 194 |     |             state.pool.price,
 195 |     |             params.amount1,
 196 |     |             params.amount0
 197 |     |         );
 198 |     |         if (liquidityAmount > 0) {
 199 |     |             state = RangeTicks.insert(
 200 |     |                 ticks,
 201 |     |                 samples,
 202 |     |                 tickMap,
 203 |     |                 state,
 204 |     |                 constants,
 205 |     |                 position.lower,
 206 |     |                 position.upper,
 207 |     |                 uint128(liquidityAmount)
 208 |     |             );
 209 |     |             uint256 amount0; uint256 amount1;
 210 |     |             (amount0, amount1) = ConstantProduct.getAmountsForLiquidity(
 211 |     |                 params.priceLower,
 212 |     |                 params.priceUpper,
 213 |     |                 state.pool.price,
 214 |     |                 liquidityAmount,
 215 |     |                 true
 216 |     |             );
 217 |     |             params.amount0 -= (amount0 <= params.amount0) ? uint128(amount0) : params.amount0;
 218 |     |             params.amount1 -= (amount1 <= params.amount1) ? uint128(amount1) : params.amount1;
 219 |     |             position.liquidity += uint128(liquidityAmount);
 220 |     |         }
 221 |     |         emit CompoundRange(
 222 |     |             params.positionId,
 223 |     |             uint128(liquidityAmount)
 224 |     |         );
 225 |     |         return (position, state, params.amount0.toInt128(), params.amount1.toInt128());
 226 |     |     }
 227 |     | 
 228 |     |     function update(
 229 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 230 |     |         RangePoolStructs.RangePosition memory position,
 231 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 232 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 233 |     |         RangePoolStructs.UpdateParams memory params
 234 |     |     ) internal returns (
 235 |     |         RangePoolStructs.RangePosition memory,
 236 |     |         int128,
 237 |     |         int128
 238 |     |     ) {
 239 |     |         RangePoolStructs.RangePositionCache memory cache;
 240 |     |         /// @dev - only true if burn call
 241 |     |         if (params.burnPercent > 0) {
 242 |     |             cache.liquidityAmount = uint256(params.burnPercent) * position.liquidity / 1e38;
 243 |     |             if (position.liquidity == cache.liquidityAmount)
 244 |     |                 IPositionERC1155(constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, constants);
 245 |     |         }
 246 |     | 
 247 |     |         (uint256 rangeFeeGrowth0, uint256 rangeFeeGrowth1) = rangeFeeGrowth(
 248 |     |             ticks[position.lower].range,
 249 |     |             ticks[position.upper].range,
 250 |     |             state,
 251 |     |             position.lower,
 252 |     |             position.upper
 253 |     |         );
 254 |     | 
 255 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertFeeGrowthInsideUnderflows(rangeFeeGrowth0, position.feeGrowthInside0Last);
 256 |     | 
 257 |     |         int128 amount0Fees = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
 258 |     |             rangeFeeGrowth0 - position.feeGrowthInside0Last,
 259 |     |             uint256(position.liquidity),
 260 |     |             Q128
 261 |     |         ).toInt256().toInt128();
 262 |     | 
 263 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertFeeGrowthInsideUnderflows(rangeFeeGrowth1, position.feeGrowthInside1Last);
 264 |     | 
 265 |     |         int128 amount1Fees = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
 266 |     |             rangeFeeGrowth1 - position.feeGrowthInside1Last,
 267 |     |             position.liquidity,
 268 |     |             Q128
 269 |     |         ).toInt256().toInt128();
 270 |     | 
 271 |     |         position.feeGrowthInside0Last = rangeFeeGrowth0;
 272 |     |         position.feeGrowthInside1Last = rangeFeeGrowth1;
 273 |     | 
 274 |     |         return (position, amount0Fees, amount1Fees);
 275 |     |     }
 276 |     | 
 277 |     |     function rangeFeeGrowth(
 278 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory lowerTick,
 279 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory upperTick,
 280 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 281 |     |         int24 lower,
 282 |     |         int24 upper
 283 |     |     ) internal pure returns (uint256 feeGrowthInside0, uint256 feeGrowthInside1) {
 284 |     | 
 285 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthGlobal0 = state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0;
 286 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthGlobal1 = state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1;
 287 |     | 
 288 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthBelow0;
 289 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthBelow1;
 290 |     |         if (state.pool.tickAtPrice >= lower) {
 291 |     |             feeGrowthBelow0 = lowerTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 292 |     |             feeGrowthBelow1 = lowerTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 293 |     |         } else {
 294 |     |             feeGrowthBelow0 = feeGrowthGlobal0 - lowerTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 295 |     |             feeGrowthBelow1 = feeGrowthGlobal1 - lowerTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 296 |     |         }
 297 |     | 
 298 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthAbove0;
 299 |     |         uint256 feeGrowthAbove1;
 300 |     |         if (state.pool.tickAtPrice < upper) {
 301 |     |             feeGrowthAbove0 = upperTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 302 |     |             feeGrowthAbove1 = upperTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 303 |     |         } else {
 304 |     |             feeGrowthAbove0 = feeGrowthGlobal0 - upperTick.feeGrowthOutside0;
 305 |     |             feeGrowthAbove1 = feeGrowthGlobal1 - upperTick.feeGrowthOutside1;
 306 |     |         }
 307 |     |         feeGrowthInside0 = feeGrowthGlobal0 - feeGrowthBelow0 - feeGrowthAbove0;
 308 |     |         feeGrowthInside1 = feeGrowthGlobal1 - feeGrowthBelow1 - feeGrowthAbove1;
 309 |     |     }
 310 |     | 
 311 |     |     function snapshot(
 312 |     |         mapping(uint256 => RangePoolStructs.RangePosition)
 313 |     |             storage positions,
 314 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 315 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 316 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 317 |     |         uint32 positionId
 318 |     |     ) internal view returns (
 319 |     |         int56   tickSecondsAccum,
 320 |     |         uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 321 |     |         uint128 feesOwed0,
 322 |     |         uint128 feesOwed1
 323 |     |     ) {
 324 |     |         RangePoolStructs.SnapshotRangeCache memory cache;
 325 |     |         cache.position = positions[positionId];
 326 |     | 
 327 |     |         // early return if position empty
 328 |     |         if (cache.position.liquidity == 0)
 329 |     |             return (0,0,0,0);
 330 |     | 
 331 |     |         cache.price = state.pool.price;
 332 |     |         cache.liquidity = state.pool.liquidity;
 333 |     |         cache.samples = state.pool.samples;
 334 |     | 
 335 |     |         // grab lower tick
 336 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory tickLower = ticks[cache.position.lower].range;
 337 |     |         
 338 |     |         // grab upper tick
 339 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory tickUpper = ticks[cache.position.upper].range;
 340 |     | 
 341 |     |         cache.tickSecondsAccumLower =  tickLower.tickSecondsAccumOutside;
 342 |     |         cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumLower = tickLower.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside;
 343 |     | 
 344 |     |         // if both have never been crossed into return 0
 345 |     |         cache.tickSecondsAccumUpper = tickUpper.tickSecondsAccumOutside;
 346 |     |         cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumUpper = tickUpper.secondsPerLiquidityAccumOutside;
 347 |     |         cache.constants = constants;
 348 |     | 
 349 |     |         (uint256 rangeFeeGrowth0, uint256 rangeFeeGrowth1) = rangeFeeGrowth(
 350 |     |             tickLower,
 351 |     |             tickUpper,
 352 |     |             state,
 353 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 354 |     |             cache.position.upper
 355 |     |         );
 356 |     | 
 357 |     |         // calcuate fees earned
 358 |     |         cache.amount0 += uint128(
 359 |     |             OverflowMath.mulDiv(
 360 |     |                 rangeFeeGrowth0 - cache.position.feeGrowthInside0Last,
 361 |     |                 cache.position.liquidity,
 362 |     |                 Q128
 363 |     |             )
 364 |     |         );
 365 |     |         cache.amount1 += uint128(
 366 |     |             OverflowMath.mulDiv(
 367 |     |                 rangeFeeGrowth1 - cache.position.feeGrowthInside1Last,
 368 |     |                 cache.position.liquidity,
 369 |     |                 Q128
 370 |     |             )
 371 |     |         );
 372 |     | 
 373 |     |         cache.tick = state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 374 |     |         if (cache.position.lower >= cache.tick) {
 375 |     |             return (
 376 |     |                 cache.tickSecondsAccumLower - cache.tickSecondsAccumUpper,
 377 |     |                 cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumLower - cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumUpper,
 378 |     |                 cache.amount0,
 379 |     |                 cache.amount1
 380 |     |             );
 381 |     |         } else if (cache.position.upper >= cache.tick) {
 382 |     |             cache.blockTimestamp = uint32(block.timestamp);
 383 |     |             (
 384 |     |                 cache.tickSecondsAccum,
 385 |     |                 cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 386 |     |             ) = Samples.getSingle(
 387 |     |                 IPool(address(this)), 
 388 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 389 |     |                     cache.samples.index,
 390 |     |                     cache.samples.length,
 391 |     |                     uint32(block.timestamp),
 392 |     |                     new uint32[](2),
 393 |     |                     cache.tick,
 394 |     |                     cache.liquidity,
 395 |     |                     cache.constants
 396 |     |                 ),
 397 |     |                 0
 398 |     |             );
 399 |     |             return (
 400 |     |                 cache.tickSecondsAccum 
 401 |     |                   - cache.tickSecondsAccumLower 
 402 |     |                   - cache.tickSecondsAccumUpper,
 403 |     |                 cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 404 |     |                   - cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumLower
 405 |     |                   - cache.secondsPerLiquidityAccumUpper,
 406 |     |                 cache.amount0,
 407 |     |                 cache.amount1
 408 |     |             );
 409 |     |         }
 410 |     |     }
 411 |     | }
 412 |     | 

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/range/RangeTicks.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../interfaces/range/IRangePoolFactory.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../interfaces/range/IRangePool.sol';
   8 |     | import './math/FeeMath.sol';
   9 |     | import './RangePositions.sol';
  10 |     | import '../math/OverflowMath.sol';
  11 |     | import '../math/ConstantProduct.sol';
  12 |     | import '../TickMap.sol';
  13 |     | import '../Samples.sol';
  14 |     | import '../../test/echidna/EchidnaAssertions.sol';
  15 |     | 
  16 |     | /// @notice Tick management library for range pools
  17 |     | library RangeTicks {
  18 |     |     error LiquidityOverflow();
  19 |     |     error LiquidityUnderflow();
  20 |     |     error InvalidLowerTick();
  21 |     |     error InvalidUpperTick();
  22 |     |     error InvalidPositionAmount();
  23 |     |     error InvalidPositionBounds();
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     event Initialize(
  26 |     |         uint160 startPrice,
  27 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice,
  28 |     |         int24 minTick,
  29 |     |         int24 maxTick
  30 |     |     );
  31 |     | 
  32 |     |     event SyncRangeTick(
  33 |     |         uint200 feeGrowthOutside0,
  34 |     |         uint200 feeGrowthOutside1,
  35 |     |         int24 tick
  36 |     |     );
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q96 = 0x1000000000000000000000000;
  39 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q128 = 0x100000000000000000000000000000000;
  40 |     | 
  41 |     |     function validate(
  42 |     |         int24 lower,
  43 |     |         int24 upper,
  44 |     |         int16 tickSpacing
  45 |     |     ) internal pure {
  46 |     |         if (lower % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  47 |     |         if (lower < ConstantProduct.minTick(tickSpacing)) require(false, 'InvalidLowerTick()');
  48 |     |         if (upper % tickSpacing != 0) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  49 |     |         if (upper > ConstantProduct.maxTick(tickSpacing)) require(false, 'InvalidUpperTick()');
  50 |     |         if (lower >= upper) require(false, 'InvalidPositionBounds()');
  51 |     |     }
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |     function insert(
  54 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  55 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  56 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  57 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
  58 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
  59 |     |         int24 lower,
  60 |     |         int24 upper,
  61 |     |         uint128 amount
  62 |     |     ) internal returns (PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory) {
  63 |     |         validate(lower, upper, constants.tickSpacing);
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |         // check for amount to overflow liquidity delta & global
  66 |     |         if (amount == 0)
  67 |     |             require(false, 'NoLiquidityBeingAdded()');
  68 |     |         if (state.liquidityGlobal + amount > uint128(type(int128).max))
  69 |     |             require(false, 'LiquidityOverflow()');
  70 |     | 
  71 |     |         // get tick at price
  72 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice = state.pool.tickAtPrice;
  73 |     | 
  74 |     |         if(TickMap.set(tickMap, lower, constants.tickSpacing)) {
  75 |     |             ticks[lower].range.liquidityDelta += int128(amount);
  76 |     |             ticks[lower].range.liquidityAbsolute += amount;
  77 |     |         } else {
  78 |     |             if (lower <= tickAtPrice) {
  79 |     |                 (
  80 |     |                     int56 tickSecondsAccum,
  81 |     |                     uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
  82 |     |                 ) = Samples.getSingle(
  83 |     |                         IPool(address(this)), 
  84 |     |                         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
  85 |     |                             state.pool.samples.index,
  86 |     |                             state.pool.samples.length,
  87 |     |                             uint32(block.timestamp),
  88 |     |                             new uint32[](2),
  89 |     |                             state.pool.tickAtPrice,
  90 |     |                             state.pool.liquidity,
  91 |     |                             constants
  92 |     |                         ),
  93 |     |                         0
  94 |     |                 );
  95 |     |                 ticks[lower].range = PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick(
  96 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
  97 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
  98 |     |                     secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
  99 |     |                     tickSecondsAccum,
 100 |     |                     int128(amount),             // liquidityDelta
 101 |     |                     amount                      // liquidityAbsolute
 102 |     |                 );
 103 |     |                 emit SyncRangeTick(
 104 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
 105 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
 106 |     |                     lower
 107 |     |                 );
 108 |     |             } else {
 109 |     |                 ticks[lower].range.liquidityDelta = int128(amount);
 110 |     |                 ticks[lower].range.liquidityAbsolute += amount;
 111 |     |             }
 112 |     |         }
 113 |     |         if(TickMap.set(tickMap, upper, constants.tickSpacing)) {
 114 |     |             ticks[upper].range.liquidityDelta -= int128(amount);
 115 |     |             ticks[upper].range.liquidityAbsolute += amount;
 116 |     |         } else {
 117 |     |             if (upper <= tickAtPrice) {
 118 |     | 
 119 |     |                 (
 120 |     |                     int56 tickSecondsAccum,
 121 |     |                     uint160 secondsPerLiquidityAccum
 122 |     |                 ) = Samples.getSingle(
 123 |     |                         IPool(address(this)), 
 124 |     |                         RangePoolStructs.SampleParams(
 125 |     |                             state.pool.samples.index,
 126 |     |                             state.pool.samples.length,
 127 |     |                             uint32(block.timestamp),
 128 |     |                             new uint32[](2),
 129 |     |                             state.pool.tickAtPrice,
 130 |     |                             state.pool.liquidity,
 131 |     |                             constants
 132 |     |                         ),
 133 |     |                         0
 134 |     |                 );
 135 |     |                 ticks[upper].range = PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick(
 136 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
 137 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
 138 |     |                     secondsPerLiquidityAccum,
 139 |     |                     tickSecondsAccum,
 140 |     |                     -int128(amount),
 141 |     |                     amount
 142 |     |                 );
 143 |     |                 emit SyncRangeTick(
 144 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0,
 145 |     |                     state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1,
 146 |     |                     upper
 147 |     |                 );
 148 |     |             } else {
 149 |     |                 ticks[upper].range.liquidityDelta = -int128(amount);
 150 |     |                 ticks[upper].range.liquidityAbsolute = amount;
 151 |     |             }
 152 |     |         }
 153 |     |         if (tickAtPrice >= lower && tickAtPrice < upper) {
 154 |     |             // write an oracle entry
 155 |     |             (state.pool.samples.index, state.pool.samples.length) = Samples.save(
 156 |     |                 samples,
 157 |     |                 state.pool.samples,
 158 |     |                 state.pool.liquidity,
 159 |     |                 state.pool.tickAtPrice
 160 |     |             );
 161 |     |             // update pool liquidity
 162 |     |             state.pool.liquidity += amount;
 163 |     |         }
 164 |     |         // update global liquidity
 165 |     |         state.liquidityGlobal += amount;
 166 |     | 
 167 |     |         return state;
 168 |     |     }
 169 |     | 
 170 |     |     function remove(
 171 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 172 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
 173 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 174 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory state,
 175 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants, 
 176 |     |         int24 lower,
 177 |     |         int24 upper,
 178 |     |         uint128 amount
 179 |     |     ) internal returns (PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState memory) {
 180 |     |         validate(lower, upper, constants.tickSpacing);
 181 |     |         //check for amount to overflow liquidity delta & global
 182 |     |         if (amount == 0) return state;
 183 |     |         if (amount > uint128(type(int128).max)) require(false, 'LiquidityUnderflow()');
 184 |     |         if (amount > state.liquidityGlobal) require(false, 'LiquidityUnderflow()');
 185 |     | 
 186 |     |         // get pool tick at price
 187 |     |         int24 tickAtPrice = state.pool.tickAtPrice;
 188 |     | 
 189 |     |         // update lower liquidity values
 190 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory tickLower = ticks[lower].range;
 191 |     |         unchecked {
 192 |     |             tickLower.liquidityDelta -= int128(amount);
 193 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickLower.liquidityAbsolute, amount, 'RTKS-1');
 194 |     |             tickLower.liquidityAbsolute -= amount;
 195 |     |         }
 196 |     |         ticks[lower].range = tickLower;
 197 |     |         // try to clear tick if possible
 198 |     |         clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, lower);
 199 |     | 
 200 |     |         // update upper liquidity values
 201 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick memory tickUpper = ticks[upper].range;
 202 |     |         unchecked {
 203 |     |             tickUpper.liquidityDelta += int128(amount);
 204 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityAbsoluteUnderflows(tickLower.liquidityAbsolute, amount, 'RTKS-2');
 205 |     |             tickUpper.liquidityAbsolute -= amount;
 206 |     |         }
 207 |     |         ticks[upper].range = tickUpper;
 208 |     |         // try to clear tick if possible
 209 |     |         clear(ticks, constants, tickMap, upper);
 210 |     | 
 211 |     |         if (tickAtPrice >= lower && tickAtPrice < upper) {
 212 |     |             // write an oracle entry
 213 |     |             (state.pool.samples.index, state.pool.samples.length) = Samples.save(
 214 |     |                 samples,
 215 |     |                 state.pool.samples,
 216 |     |                 state.pool.liquidity,
 217 |     |                 tickAtPrice
 218 |     |             );
 219 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityUnderflows(state.pool.liquidity, amount, 'RTKS-3');
 220 |     |             state.pool.liquidity -= amount;  
 221 |     |         }
 222 |     |         EchidnaAssertions.assertLiquidityGlobalUnderflows(state.liquidityGlobal, amount, 'RTKS-4');
 223 |     |         state.liquidityGlobal -= amount;
 224 |     | 
 225 |     |         return state;
 226 |     |     }
 227 |     | 
 228 |     |     function clear(
 229 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
 230 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 231 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
 232 |     |         int24 tickToClear
 233 |     |     ) internal {
 234 |     |         if (_empty(ticks[tickToClear])) {
 235 |     |             if (tickToClear != ConstantProduct.maxTick(constants.tickSpacing) &&
 236 |     |                     tickToClear != ConstantProduct.minTick(constants.tickSpacing)) {
 237 |     |                 ticks[tickToClear].range = PoolsharkStructs.RangeTick(0,0,0,0,0,0);
 238 |     |                 TickMap.unset(tickMap, tickToClear, constants.tickSpacing);
 239 |     |             }
 240 |     |         }
 241 |     |     }
 242 |     | 
 243 |     |     function _empty(
 244 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.Tick memory tick
 245 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
 246 |     |         bool
 247 |     |     ) {
 248 |     |         if (tick.range.liquidityAbsolute != 0) {
 249 |     |             return false;
 250 |     |         }
 251 |     |         return true;
 252 |     |     }
 253 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/range/math/FeeMath.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: GPLv3
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../Samples.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../utils/SafeCast.sol';
   6 |     | import "../../math/OverflowMath.sol";
   7 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/PoolsharkStructs.sol';
   8 |     | import "../../../interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol";
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | /// @notice Math library that facilitates fee handling.
  11 |     | library FeeMath {
  12 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  13 |     | 
  14 |     |     uint256 internal constant FEE_DELTA_CONST = 0;
  15 |     |     //TODO: change FEE_DELTA_CONST before launch
  16 |     |     // uint256 internal constant FEE_DELTA_CONST = 5000;
  17 |     |     uint256 internal constant Q128 = 0x100000000000000000000000000000000;
  18 |     | 
  19 |     |     struct CalculateLocals {
  20 |     |         uint256 price;
  21 |     |         uint256 minPrice;
  22 |     |         uint256 lastPrice;
  23 |     |         uint256 swapFee;
  24 |     |         uint256 feeAmount;
  25 |     |         uint256 protocolFee;
  26 |     |         uint256 protocolFeesAccrued;
  27 |     |         uint256 amountRange;
  28 |     |         bool feeDirection;
  29 |     |     }
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |     function calculate(
  32 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory cache,
  33 |     |         uint256 amountIn,
  34 |     |         uint256 amountOut,
  35 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  36 |     |     ) internal pure returns (
  37 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.SwapCache memory
  38 |     |     )
  39 |     |     {
  40 |     |         CalculateLocals memory locals;
  41 |     |         if (cache.state.pool.liquidity != 0) {
  42 |     |             // calculate dynamic fee
  43 |     |             {
  44 |     |                 locals.minPrice = ConstantProduct.getPrice(cache.constants.bounds.min);
  45 |     |                 // square prices to take delta
  46 |     |                 locals.price = ConstantProduct.getPrice(cache.price);
  47 |     |                 locals.lastPrice = ConstantProduct.getPrice(cache.averagePrice);
  48 |     |                 if (locals.price < locals.minPrice)
  49 |     |                     locals.price = locals.minPrice;
  50 |     |                 if (locals.lastPrice < locals.minPrice)
  51 |     |                     locals.lastPrice = locals.minPrice;
  52 |     |                 // delta is % modifier on the swapFee
  53 |     |                 uint256 delta = OverflowMath.mulDiv(
  54 |     |                         FEE_DELTA_CONST / uint16(cache.constants.tickSpacing), // higher FEE_DELTA_CONST means
  55 |     |                         (                                                      // more aggressive dynamic fee
  56 |     |                             locals.price > locals.lastPrice
  57 |     |                                 ? locals.price - locals.lastPrice
  58 |     |                                 : locals.lastPrice - locals.price
  59 |     |                         ) * 1_000_000,
  60 |     |                         locals.lastPrice 
  61 |     |                 );
  62 |     |                 // max fee increase at 5x
  63 |     |                 if (delta > 4_000_000) delta = 4_000_000;
  64 |     |                 // true means increased fee for zeroForOne = true
  65 |     |                 locals.feeDirection = locals.price < locals.lastPrice;
  66 |     |                 // adjust fee based on direction
  67 |     |                 if (zeroForOne == locals.feeDirection) {
  68 |     |                     // if swapping away from twap price, increase fee
  69 |     |                     locals.swapFee = cache.constants.swapFee + OverflowMath.mulDiv(delta,cache.constants.swapFee, 1e6);
  70 |     |                 } else if (delta < 1e6) {
  71 |     |                     // if swapping towards twap price, decrease fee
  72 |     |                     locals.swapFee = cache.constants.swapFee - OverflowMath.mulDiv(delta,cache.constants.swapFee, 1e6);
  73 |     |                 } else {
  74 |     |                     // if swapping towards twap price and delta > 100%, set fee to zero
  75 |     |                     locals.swapFee = 0;
  76 |     |                 }
  77 |     |                 // console.log('price movement', locals.lastPrice, locals.price);
  78 |     |                 // console.log('swap fee adjustment',cache.constants.swapFee + delta * cache.constants.swapFee / 1e6);
  79 |     |             }
  80 |     |             if (cache.exactIn) {
  81 |     |                 // calculate output from range liquidity
  82 |     |                 locals.amountRange = OverflowMath.mulDiv(amountOut, cache.state.pool.liquidity, cache.liquidity);
  83 |     |                 // take enough fees to cover fee growth
  84 |     |                 locals.feeAmount = OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(locals.amountRange, locals.swapFee, 1e6);
  85 |     |                 amountOut -= locals.feeAmount;
  86 |     |             } else {
  87 |     |                 // calculate input from range liquidity
  88 |     |                 locals.amountRange = OverflowMath.mulDiv(amountIn, cache.state.pool.liquidity, cache.liquidity);
  89 |     |                 // take enough fees to cover fee growth
  90 |     |                 locals.feeAmount = OverflowMath.mulDivRoundingUp(locals.amountRange, locals.swapFee, 1e6);
  91 |     |                 amountIn += locals.feeAmount;
  92 |     |             }
  93 |     |             // add to total fees paid for swap
  94 |     |             cache.feeAmount += locals.feeAmount.toUint128();
  95 |     |             // load protocol fee from cache
  96 |     |             // zeroForOne && exactIn   = fee on token1
  97 |     |             // zeroForOne && !exactIn  = fee on token0
  98 |     |             // !zeroForOne && !exactIn = fee on token1
  99 |     |             // !zeroForOne && exactIn  = fee on token0
 100 |     |             locals.protocolFee = (zeroForOne == cache.exactIn) ? cache.state.pool.protocolSwapFee1 
 101 |     |                                                                : cache.state.pool.protocolSwapFee0;
 102 |     |             // calculate fee
 103 |     |             locals.protocolFeesAccrued = OverflowMath.mulDiv(locals.feeAmount, locals.protocolFee, 1e4);
 104 |     |             // fees for this swap step
 105 |     |             locals.feeAmount -= locals.protocolFeesAccrued;
 106 |     |             // save fee growth and protocol fees
 107 |     |             if (zeroForOne == cache.exactIn) {
 108 |     |                 cache.state.pool0.protocolFees += uint128(locals.protocolFeesAccrued);
 109 |     |                 cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal1 += uint200(OverflowMath.mulDiv(locals.feeAmount, Q128, cache.state.pool.liquidity));
 110 |     |             } else {
 111 |     |                 cache.state.pool1.protocolFees += uint128(locals.protocolFeesAccrued);
 112 |     |                 cache.state.pool.feeGrowthGlobal0 += uint200(OverflowMath.mulDiv(locals.feeAmount, Q128, cache.state.pool.liquidity));
 113 |     |             }
 114 |     |         }
 115 |     |         cache.input  += amountIn;
 116 |     |         cache.output += amountOut;
 117 |     | 
 118 |     |         return cache;
 119 |     |     }
 120 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/range/pool/BurnRangeCall.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../utils/Collect.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   7 |     | import '../RangePositions.sol';
   8 |     | 
   9 |     | library BurnRangeCall {
  10 |     |     using SafeCast for int128;
  11 |     | 
  12 |     |     event BurnRange(
  13 |     |         address indexed recipient,
  14 |     |         int24 lower,
  15 |     |         int24 upper,
  16 |     |         uint256 indexed tokenId,
  17 |     |         uint128 liquidityBurned,
  18 |     |         uint128 amount0,
  19 |     |         uint128 amount1
  20 |     |     );
  21 |     | 
  22 |     |     function perform(
  23 |     |         mapping(uint256 => RangePoolStructs.RangePosition)
  24 |     |             storage positions,
  25 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  26 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  27 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  28 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  29 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeCache memory cache,
  30 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeParams memory params
  31 |     |     ) internal {
  32 |     |         // check for invalid receiver
  33 |     |         if (params.to == address(0))
  34 |     |             require(false, 'CollectToZeroAddress()');
  35 |     |         
  36 |     |         // initialize cache
  37 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  38 |     |         cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  39 |     | 
  40 |     |         // check positionId owner
  41 |     |         if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  42 |     |             require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  43 |     |         if (params.burnPercent > 1e38) params.burnPercent = 1e38;
  44 |     |         ( 
  45 |     |             cache.position,
  46 |     |             cache.amount0,
  47 |     |             cache.amount1
  48 |     |         ) = RangePositions.update(
  49 |     |                 ticks,
  50 |     |                 cache.position,
  51 |     |                 cache.state,
  52 |     |                 cache.constants,
  53 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.UpdateParams(
  54 |     |                     cache.position.lower,
  55 |     |                     cache.position.upper,
  56 |     |                     params.positionId,
  57 |     |                     params.burnPercent
  58 |     |                 )
  59 |     |         );
  60 |     |         cache = RangePositions.remove(
  61 |     |             ticks,
  62 |     |             samples,
  63 |     |             tickMap,
  64 |     |             params,
  65 |     |             cache
  66 |     |         );
  67 |     |         // only compound if burnPercent is zero
  68 |     |         if (params.burnPercent == 0)
  69 |     |             if (cache.amount0 > 0 || cache.amount1 > 0) {
  70 |     |                 (
  71 |     |                     cache.position,
  72 |     |                     cache.state,
  73 |     |                     cache.amount0,
  74 |     |                     cache.amount1
  75 |     |                 ) = RangePositions.compound(
  76 |     |                     ticks,
  77 |     |                     tickMap,
  78 |     |                     samples,
  79 |     |                     cache.state,
  80 |     |                     cache.constants,
  81 |     |                     cache.position,
  82 |     |                     RangePoolStructs.CompoundRangeParams(
  83 |     |                         cache.priceLower,
  84 |     |                         cache.priceUpper,
  85 |     |                         cache.amount0.toUint128(),
  86 |     |                         cache.amount1.toUint128(),
  87 |     |                         params.positionId
  88 |     |                     )
  89 |     |                 );
  90 |     |             }
  91 |     |         // save changes to storage
  92 |     |         save(positions, globalState, cache, params.positionId);
  93 |     | 
  94 |     |         // transfer amounts to user
  95 |     |         if (cache.amount0 > 0 || cache.amount1 > 0)
  96 |     |             Collect.range(
  97 |     |                 cache.constants,
  98 |     |                 params.to,
  99 |     |                 cache.amount0,
 100 |     |                 cache.amount1
 101 |     |             );
 102 |     |     }
 103 |     | 
 104 |     |     function save(
 105 |     |         mapping(uint256 => RangePoolStructs.RangePosition)
 106 |     |             storage positions,
 107 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 108 |     |         RangePoolStructs.BurnRangeCache memory cache,
 109 |     |         uint32 positionId
 110 |     |     ) internal {
 111 |     |         positions[positionId] = cache.position;
 112 |     |         globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 113 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
 114 |     |     }
 115 |     | }
