/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/range/pool/MintRangeCall.sol
   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../../interfaces/structs/RangePoolStructs.sol';
   5 |     | import '../../utils/SafeTransfers.sol';
   6 |     | import '../../utils/Collect.sol';
   7 |     | import '../../utils/PositionTokens.sol';
   8 |     | import '../RangePositions.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | library MintRangeCall {
  11 |     |     using SafeCast for uint256;
  12 |     |     using SafeCast for int128;
  13 |     |     using SafeCast for uint128;
  14 |     | 
  15 |     |     event MintRange(
  16 |     |         address indexed recipient,
  17 |     |         int24 lower,
  18 |     |         int24 upper,
  19 |     |         uint32 indexed positionId,
  20 |     |         uint128 liquidityMinted,
  21 |     |         int128 amount0Delta,
  22 |     |         int128 amount1Delta
  23 |     |     );
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     function perform(
  26 |     |         mapping(uint256 => RangePoolStructs.RangePosition)
  27 |     |             storage positions,
  28 |     |         mapping(int24 => PoolsharkStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  29 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage tickMap,
  30 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,
  31 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  32 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory cache,
  33 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeParams memory params
  34 |     |     ) internal {
  35 |     |         // initialize cache
  36 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  37 |     | 
  38 |     |         // id of 0 can be passed to create new position
  39 |     |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
  40 |     |             cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  41 |     |             // existing position
  42 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  43 |     |                 // check for balance held
  44 |     |                 require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  45 |     |             // set bounds as defined by position
  46 |     |             params.lower = cache.position.lower;
  47 |     |             params.upper = cache.position.upper;
  48 |     |             // update existing position
  49 |     |             (
  50 |     |                 cache.position,
  51 |     |                 cache.amount0,
  52 |     |                 cache.amount1
  53 |     |             ) = RangePositions.update(
  54 |     |                     ticks,
  55 |     |                     cache.position,
  56 |     |                     cache.state,
  57 |     |                     cache.constants,
  58 |     |                     RangePoolStructs.UpdateParams(
  59 |     |                         params.lower,
  60 |     |                         params.upper,
  61 |     |                         params.positionId,
  62 |     |                         0
  63 |     |                     )
  64 |     |             );
  65 |     |         } else {
  66 |     |             // create a new position
  67 |     |             params.positionId = cache.state.positionIdNext;
  68 |     |             // increment for next position
  69 |     |             cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
  70 |     |             // set tick bounds on position
  71 |     |             cache.position.lower = params.lower;
  72 |     |             cache.position.upper = params.upper;
  73 |     |         }
  74 |     |         // set cache based on bounds
  75 |     |         cache.priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.lower, cache.constants);
  76 |     |         cache.priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(cache.position.upper, cache.constants);
  77 |     | 
  78 |     |         // compound and transfer remaining back to user
  79 |     |         if (cache.amount0 > 0 || cache.amount1 > 0) {
  80 |     |             (
  81 |     |                 cache.position,
  82 |     |                 cache.state,
  83 |     |                 cache.amount0,
  84 |     |                 cache.amount1
  85 |     |             ) = RangePositions.compound(
  86 |     |                 ticks,
  87 |     |                 tickMap,
  88 |     |                 samples,
  89 |     |                 cache.state,
  90 |     |                 cache.constants,
  91 |     |                 cache.position,
  92 |     |                 RangePoolStructs.CompoundRangeParams( 
  93 |     |                     cache.priceLower,
  94 |     |                     cache.priceUpper,
  95 |     |                     cache.amount0.toUint128(),
  96 |     |                     cache.amount1.toUint128(),
  97 |     |                     params.positionId
  98 |     |                 )
  99 |     |             );
 100 |     |         }
 101 |     |         // validate input amounts
 102 |     |         (params, cache) = RangePositions.validate(params, cache);
 103 |     | 
 104 |     |         // save changes to storage before transfer in
 105 |     |         save(positions, globalState, cache, params.positionId);
 106 |     |         cache.amount0 -= params.amount0.toInt128();
 107 |     |         cache.amount1 -= params.amount1.toInt128();
 108 |     | 
 109 |     |         emit MintRange(
 110 |     |             params.to,
 111 |     |             cache.position.lower,
 112 |     |             cache.position.upper,
 113 |     |             params.positionId,
 114 |     |             cache.liquidityMinted.toUint128(),
 115 |     |             -cache.amount0, /// @dev - emit balance delta from pool POV
 116 |     |             -cache.amount1
 117 |     |         );
 118 |     | 
 119 |     |         // transfer in amounts
 120 |     |         if (cache.amount0 < 0) {
 121 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferIn(cache.constants.token0, (-cache.amount0).toUint128());
 122 |     |             cache.amount0 = 0;
 123 |     |         } 
 124 |     |         if (cache.amount1 < 0) {
 125 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferIn(cache.constants.token1, (-cache.amount1).toUint128());
 126 |     |             cache.amount1 = 0;
 127 |     |         }
 128 |     | 
 129 |     |         // update position with latest fees accrued
 130 |     |         cache = RangePositions.add(
 131 |     |             ticks,
 132 |     |             samples,
 133 |     |             tickMap,
 134 |     |             cache,
 135 |     |             params
 136 |     |         );
 137 |     | 
 138 |     |         // save changes to storage before transfer out
 139 |     |         save(positions, globalState, cache, params.positionId);
 140 |     | 
 141 |     |         // transfer positive amounts back to user
 142 |     |         if (cache.amount0 > 0 || cache.amount1 > 0)
 143 |     |             Collect.range(
 144 |     |                 cache.constants,
 145 |     |                 params.to,
 146 |     |                 cache.amount0,
 147 |     |                 cache.amount1
 148 |     |             );
 149 |     |     }
 150 |     | 
 151 |     |     function save(
 152 |     |         mapping(uint256 => RangePoolStructs.RangePosition)
 153 |     |             storage positions,
 154 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
 155 |     |         RangePoolStructs.MintRangeCache memory cache,
 156 |     |         uint32 positionId
 157 |     |     ) internal {
 158 |     |         positions[positionId] = cache.position;
 159 |     |         globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 160 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
 161 |     |         globalState.positionIdNext = cache.state.positionIdNext;
 162 |     |     }
 163 |     | }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/utils/Collect.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | import '../../interfaces/IERC20Minimal.sol';
  5 |     | import '../../interfaces/structs/LimitPoolStructs.sol';
  6 |     | import '../limit/LimitPositions.sol';
  7 |     | import '../utils/SafeTransfers.sol';
  8 |     | 
  9 |     | library Collect {
 10 |     |     using SafeCast for int128;
 11 |     | 
 12 |     |     event CollectRange(
 13 |     |         uint128 amount0,
 14 |     |         uint128 amount1
 15 |     |     );
 16 |     | 
 17 |     |     function range(
 18 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants,
 19 |     |         address recipient,
 20 |     |         int128 amount0,
 21 |     |         int128 amount1
 22 |     |     ) internal {
 23 |     |         /// @dev - negative balances will revert
 24 |     |         if (amount0 > 0) {
 25 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceededRange(
 26 |     |                 balance(constants.token0),
 27 |     |                 amount0
 28 |     |             );
 29 |     |             /// @dev - cast to ensure user doesn't owe the pool balance
 30 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(recipient, constants.token0, amount0.toUint128());
 31 |     |         }
 32 |     |         if (amount1 > 0) {
 33 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceededRange(
 34 |     |                 balance(constants.token1),
 35 |     |                 amount1
 36 |     |             );
 37 |     |             /// @dev - cast to ensure user doesn't owe the pool balance
 38 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(recipient, constants.token1, amount1.toUint128());
 39 |     |         }
 40 |     |         emit CollectRange(amount0.toUint128(), amount1.toUint128());
 41 |     |     }
 42 |     | 
 43 |     |     function burnLimit(
 44 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
 45 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params
 46 |     |     ) internal returns (
 47 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory
 48 |     |     )    
 49 |     |     {
 50 |     |         uint128 amount0 = params.zeroForOne ? cache.amountOut : cache.amountIn;
 51 |     |         uint128 amount1 = params.zeroForOne ? cache.amountIn : cache.amountOut;
 52 |     | 
 53 |     |         /// zero out balances and transfer out
 54 |     |         if (amount0 > 0) {
 55 |     |             cache.amountIn = 0;
 56 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceeded(
 57 |     |                 balance(cache.constants.token0),
 58 |     |                 amount0
 59 |     |             );
 60 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(params.to, cache.constants.token0, amount0);
 61 |     |         }
 62 |     |         if (amount1 > 0) {
 63 |     |             cache.amountOut = 0;
 64 |     |             EchidnaAssertions.assertPoolBalanceExceeded(
 65 |     |                 balance(cache.constants.token1),
 66 |     |                 amount1
 67 |     |             );
 68 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(params.to, cache.constants.token1, amount1);
 69 |     |         }
 70 |     |         return cache;
 71 |     |     }
 72 |     | 
 73 |     |     function balance(
 74 |     |         address token

 82 |     |                                         address(this)

 84 |     |                                 );

  4 |     | /// @title Safe casting methods
  5 |     | /// @notice Contains methods for safely casting between types
  6 |     | library SafeCast {
  7 |     |     /// @notice Cast a uint256 to a uint128, revert on overflow
  8 |     |     /// @param y The uint256 to be downcasted
  9 |     |     /// @return z The downcasted integer, now type uint128
 10 |     |     function toUint128(uint256 y) internal pure returns (uint128 z) {
 11 |     |         if((z = uint128(y)) != y) require(false, 'Uint256ToUint128:Overflow()');
 12 |     |     }
 13 |     | 
 14 |     |     /// @notice Cast a uint256 to a uint128, revert on overflow
 15 |     |     /// @param y The uint256 to be downcasted
 16 |     |     /// @return z The downcasted integer, now type uint128
 17 |     |     function toUint128(int128 y) internal pure returns (uint128 z) {
 18 |     |         if(y < 0) require(false, 'Int128ToUint128:Underflow()');
 19 |     |         z = uint128(y);
 20 |     |     }

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/utils/SafeTransfers.sol
   1 |     | //SPDX-License-Identifier: Unlicense
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../../external/openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol';
   5 |     | 
   6 |     | library SafeTransfers {
   7 |     |     /**
   8 |     |      * @dev Similar to EIP20 transfer, except it handles a False result from `transferFrom` and reverts in that case.
   9 |     |      *      This will revert due to insufficient balance or insufficient allowance.
  10 |     |      *      This function returns the actual amount received,
  11 |     |      *      which may be less than `amount` if there is a fee attached to the transfer.
  12 |     |      *
  13 |     |      *      Note: This wrapper safely handles non-standard ERC-20 tokens that do not return a value.
  14 |     |      *            See here: https://medium.com/coinmonks/missing-return-value-bug-at-least-130-tokens-affected-d67bf08521ca
  15 |     |      */
  16 |     |     // slither-disable-next-line assembly
  17 |     |     function transferIn(address token, uint256 amount) internal returns (uint256) {
  18 |     |         if (token == address(0)) {
  19 |     |             if (msg.value < amount) require(false, 'TransferFailed(msg.sender, address(this)');
  20 |     |             return amount;
  21 |     |         }
  22 |     |         if (amount == 0) return 0;
  23 |     |         IERC20 erc20Token = IERC20(token);
  24 |     |         uint256 balanceBefore = IERC20(token).balanceOf(address(this));
  25 |     | 
  26 |     |         // ? We are checking the transfer, but since we are doing so in an assembly block
  27 |     |         // ? Slither does not pick up on that and results in a hit
  28 |     |         // slither-disable-next-line unchecked-transfer
  29 |     |         erc20Token.transferFrom(msg.sender, address(this), amount);
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |         bool success;
  32 |     |         assembly {
  33 |     |             switch returndatasize()
  34 |     |             case 0 {
  35 |     |                 // This is a non-standard ERC-20
  36 |     |                 success := 1 // set success to true
  37 |     |             }
  38 |     |             case 32 {
  39 |     |                 // This is a compliant ERC-20
  40 |     |                 returndatacopy(0, 0, 32)
  41 |     |                 success := mload(0) // Set `success = returndata` of external call
  42 |     |             }
  43 |     |             default {
  44 |     |                 // This is an excessively non-compliant ERC-20, revert.
  45 |     |                 success := 0
  46 |     |             }
  47 |     |         }
  48 |     |         if (!success) require(false, 'TransferFailed(msg.sender, address(this)');
  49 |     | 
  50 |     |         // Calculate the amount that was *actually* transferred
  51 |     |         uint256 balanceAfter = IERC20(token).balanceOf(address(this));
  52 |     | 
  53 |     |         return balanceAfter - balanceBefore; // underflow already checked above, just subtract
  54 |     |     }
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |     /**
  57 |     |      * @dev Similar to EIP20 transfer, except it handles a False success from `transfer` and returns an explanatory
  58 |     |      *      error code rather than reverting. If caller has not called checked protocol's balance, this may revert due to
  59 |     |      *      insufficient cash held in this contract. If caller has checked protocol's balance prior to this call, and verified
  60 |     |      *      it is >= amount, this should not revert in normal conditions.
  61 |     |      *
  62 |     |      *      Note: This wrapper safely handles non-standard ERC-20 tokens that do not return a value.
  63 |     |      *            See here: https://medium.com/coinmonks/missing-return-value-bug-at-least-130-tokens-affected-d67bf08521ca
  64 |     |      */
  65 |     |     // slither-disable-next-line assembly
  66 |     |     function transferOut(
  67 |     |         address to,
  68 |     |         address token,
  69 |     |         uint256 amount
  70 |     |     ) internal {
  71 |     |         if (token == address(0)) {
  72 |     |             if (address(this).balance < amount) require(false, 'TransferFailed(address(this), to');
  73 |     |             payable(to).transfer(amount);
  74 |     |             return;
  75 |     |         }
  76 |     |         if (amount == 0) return;
  77 |     |         IERC20 erc20Token = IERC20(token);
  78 |     |         // ? We are checking the transfer, but since we are doing so in an assembly block
  79 |     |         // ? Slither does not pick up on that and results in a hit
  80 |     |         // slither-disable-next-line unchecked-transfer
  81 |     |         erc20Token.transfer(to, amount);
  82 |     | 
  83 |     |         bool success;
  84 |     |         assembly {
  85 |     |             switch returndatasize()
  86 |     |             case 0 {
  87 |     |                 // This is a non-standard ERC-20
  88 |     |                 success := 1 // set success to true
  89 |     |             }
  90 |     |             case 32 {
  91 |     |                 // This is a complaint ERC-20
  92 |     |                 returndatacopy(0, 0, 32)
  93 |     |                 success := mload(0) // Set `success = returndata` of external call
  94 |     |             }
  95 |     |             default {
  96 |     |                 // This is an excessively non-compliant ERC-20, revert.
  97 |     |                 success := 0
  98 |     |             }
  99 |     |         }
 100 |     |         if (!success) require(false, 'TransferFailed(address(this), msg.sender');
 101 |     |     }
 102 |     | 
 103 |     |     /**
 104 |     |      * @dev Similar to EIP20 transfer, except it handles a False result from `transferFrom` and reverts in that case.
 105 |     |      *      This will revert due to insufficient balance or insufficient allowance.
 106 |     |      *      This function returns the actual amount received,
 107 |     |      *      which may be less than `amount` if there is a fee attached to the transfer.
 108 |     |      *
 109 |     |      *      Note: This wrapper safely handles non-standard ERC-20 tokens that do not return a value.
 110 |     |      *            See here: https://medium.com/coinmonks/missing-return-value-bug-at-least-130-tokens-affected-d67bf08521ca
 111 |     |      */
 112 |     |     // slither-disable-next-line assembly

/home/ec2-user/git/limit/contracts/libraries/utils/String.sol
  1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
  2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
  3 |     | 
  4 |     | library String {
  5 |     |     bytes16 private constant alphabet = "0123456789abcdef";
  6 |     | 
  7 |     |     function from(bytes32 value) internal pure returns(string memory) {
  8 |     |         return toString(abi.encodePacked(value));
  9 |     |     }
 10 |     | 
 11 |     |     function from(address account) internal pure returns(string memory) {
 12 |     |         return toString(abi.encodePacked(account));
 13 |     |     }
 14 |     | 
 15 |     |     function from(uint256 value) internal pure returns(string memory) {
 16 |     |         unchecked {
 17 |     |             uint256 length = log10(value) + 1;
 18 |     |             string memory buffer = new string(length);
 19 |     |             uint256 ptr;
 20 |     |             /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 21 |     |             assembly {
 22 |     |                 ptr := add(buffer, add(32, length))
 23 |     |             }
 24 |     |             while (true) {
 25 |     |                 ptr--;
 26 |     |                 /// @solidity memory-safe-assembly
 27 |     |                 assembly {
 28 |     |                     mstore8(ptr, byte(mod(value, 10), alphabet))
 29 |     |                 }
 30 |     |                 value /= 10;
 31 |     |                 if (value == 0) break;
 32 |     |             }
 33 |     |             return buffer;
 34 |     |         }
 35 |     |     }
 36 |     | 
 37 |     |     function from(int256 value) internal pure returns (string memory) {
 38 |     |         return string(abi.encodePacked(value < 0 ? "-" : "", from(abs(value))));
 39 |     |     }
 40 |     | 
 41 |     |     function abs(int256 n) internal pure returns (uint256) {
 42 |     |         unchecked {
 43 |     |             // must be unchecked in order to support `n = type(int256).min`
 44 |     |             return uint256(n >= 0 ? n : -n);
 45 |     |         }
 46 |     |     }
 47 |     | 
 48 |     |     function log10(uint256 value) internal pure returns (uint256) {
 49 |     |         uint256 result = 0;
 50 |     |         unchecked {
 51 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 64) {
 52 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 64;
 53 |     |                 result += 64;
 54 |     |             }
 55 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 32) {
 56 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 32;
 57 |     |                 result += 32;
 58 |     |             }
 59 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 16) {
 60 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 16;
 61 |     |                 result += 16;
 62 |     |             }
 63 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 8) {
 64 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 8;
 65 |     |                 result += 8;
 66 |     |             }
 67 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 4) {
 68 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 4;
 69 |     |                 result += 4;
 70 |     |             }
 71 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 2) {
 72 |     |                 value /= 10 ** 2;
 73 |     |                 result += 2;
 74 |     |             }
 75 |     |             if (value >= 10 ** 1) {
 76 |     |                 result += 1;
 77 |     |             }
 78 |     |         }
 79 |     |         return result;
 80 |     |     }
 81 |     | 
 82 |     |     function toString(bytes memory data) internal pure returns(string memory) {
 83 |     |         bytes memory str = new bytes(2 + data.length * 2);
 84 |     |         str[0] = "0";
 85 |     |         str[1] = "x";
 86 |     |         for (uint i = 0; i < data.length;) {
 87 |     |             str[2+i*2] = alphabet[uint(uint8(data[i] >> 4))];
 88 |     |             str[3+i*2] = alphabet[uint(uint8(data[i] & 0x0f))];
 89 |     |             unchecked {
 90 |     |                 ++i;
 91 |     |             }
 92 |     |         }
 93 |     |         return string(str);
 94 |     |     }
 95 |     | }

  33 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitParams memory params,
  34 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache
  35 |     |     ) external {
  36 |     |         // check for invalid receiver
  37 | *   |         if (params.to == address(0))
  38 |     |             require(false, 'CollectToZeroAddress()');
  39 |     |         
  40 |     |         // initialize cache
  41 | *   |         cache.state = globalState;
  42 |     |         cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  43 |     | 
  44 |     |         // check positionId owner
  45 |     |         if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  46 |     |             require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  47 |     | 
  48 |     |         // update position
  49 |     |         (
  50 |     |             params,
  51 |     |             cache
  52 |     |         ) = LimitPositions.update(
  53 |     |             ticks,
  54 |     |             tickMap,
  55 |     |             cache,
  56 |     |             params
  57 |     |         );
  58 |     | 
  59 |     |         int24 lower = cache.position.lower;
  60 |     |         int24 upper = cache.position.upper;
  61 |     |         bool positionExists = cache.position.liquidity != 0;
  62 |     | 
  63 |     |         // save position before transfer
  64 |     |         if ((params.zeroForOne ? params.claim != cache.position.upper
  65 |     |                                : params.claim != cache.position.lower)) {
  66 |     |             if (cache.position.liquidity > 0) {
  67 |     |                 if (params.zeroForOne) {
  68 |     |                     cache.position.lower = params.claim;
  69 |     |                 } else {
  70 |     |                     cache.position.upper = params.claim;
  71 |     |                 }
  72 |     |                 positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
  73 |     |             } else {
  74 |     |                 IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  75 |     |                 delete positions[params.positionId];
  76 |     |             }
  77 |     |         } else {
  78 |     |             IPositionERC1155(cache.constants.poolToken).burn(msg.sender, params.positionId, 1, cache.constants);
  79 |     |             delete positions[params.positionId];
  80 |     |         }
  81 |     | 
  82 |     |         cache = Collect.burnLimit(
  83 |     |             cache,
  84 |     |             params
  85 |     |         );
  86 |     | 
  87 |     |         revert SimulateBurn(lower, upper, positionExists);
  88 |     |     }
  89 |     | 
  90 |     |     function save(
  91 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.BurnLimitCache memory cache,
  92 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  93 |     |         bool zeroForOne
  94 |     |     ) internal {
  95 |     |         globalState.epoch = cache.state.epoch;
  96 |     |         globalState.liquidityGlobal = cache.state.liquidityGlobal;
  97 |     |         if (zeroForOne) {
  98 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
  99 |     |             globalState.pool0 = cache.state.pool0;
 100 |     |         } else {
 101 |     |             globalState.pool = cache.state.pool;
 102 |     |             globalState.pool1 = cache.state.pool1;
 103 |     |         }
 104 |     |     }

  68 |     |         // Echidna funcs
  69 | *   |     function getResizedTicks(
  70 |     |         mapping(uint256 => LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition)
  71 |     |             storage positions,
  72 |     |         mapping(int24 => LimitPoolStructs.Tick) storage ticks,
  73 |     |         RangePoolStructs.Sample[65535] storage samples,

  75 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.TickMap storage limitTickMap,
  76 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.GlobalState storage globalState,
  77 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitParams memory params,
  78 |     |         LimitPoolStructs.MintLimitCache memory cache
  79 |     |     ) external {
  80 | *   |         bool positionCreated = false;
  81 | *   |         if (params.positionId > 0) {
  82 |     |             if (PositionTokens.balanceOf(cache.constants, msg.sender, params.positionId) == 0)
  83 |     |                 // check for balance held
  84 |     |                 require(false, 'PositionNotFound()');
  85 |     |             cache.position = positions[params.positionId];
  86 |     |         }
  87 |     | 
  88 |     |         cache.state = globalState;
  89 |     | 
  90 |     |         // resize position if necessary
  91 |     |         (params, cache) = LimitPositions.resize(
  92 |     |             ticks,
  93 |     |             samples,
  94 |     |             rangeTickMap,
  95 |     |             limitTickMap,
  96 |     |             params,
  97 |     |             cache
  98 |     |         );
  99 |     | 
 100 |     |         // save state for reentrancy safety
 101 |     |         save(cache, globalState, !params.zeroForOne);
 102 |     | 
 103 |     |         // transfer in token amount
 104 |     |         SafeTransfers.transferIn(
 105 |     |                                  params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token0 
 106 |     |                                                    : cache.constants.token1,
 107 |     |                                  params.amount + cache.swapCache.input
 108 |     |                                 );
 109 |     |         // transfer out if swap output 
 110 |     |         if (cache.swapCache.output > 0)
 111 |     |             SafeTransfers.transferOut(
 112 |     |                 params.to,
 113 |     |                 params.zeroForOne ? cache.constants.token1 
 114 |     |                                   : cache.constants.token0,
 115 |     |                 cache.swapCache.output
 116 |     |             );
 117 |     |         // mint position if amount is left
 118 |     |         if (params.amount > 0 && params.lower < params.upper) {
 119 |     |             if (params.positionId == 0 ||                       // new position
 120 |     |                     params.lower != cache.position.lower ||     // lower mismatch
 121 |     |                     params.upper != cache.position.upper) {     // upper mismatch
 122 |     |                 LimitPoolStructs.LimitPosition memory newPosition;
 123 |     |                 newPosition.lower = params.lower;
 124 |     |                 newPosition.upper = params.upper;
 125 |     |                 // use new position in cache
 126 |     |                 cache.position = newPosition;
 127 |     |                 params.positionId = cache.state.positionIdNext;
 128 |     |                 cache.state.positionIdNext += 1;
 129 |     |             }
 130 |     |             cache.pool = params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 : cache.state.pool1;
 131 |     |             
 132 |     |             // bump to the next tick if there is no liquidity
 133 |     |             if (cache.pool.liquidity == 0) {
 134 |     |                 /// @dev - this makes sure to have liquidity unlocked if undercutting
 135 |     |                 (cache, cache.pool) = LimitTicks.unlock(cache, cache.pool, ticks, limitTickMap, params.zeroForOne);
 136 |     |             }
 137 |     | 
 138 |     |             if (params.zeroForOne) {
 139 |     |                 uint160 priceLower = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.lower, cache.constants);
 140 |     |                 if (priceLower <= cache.pool.price) {
 141 |     |                     // save liquidity if active
 142 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 143 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 144 |     |                     }
 145 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceLower;
 146 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.lower;
 147 |     |                     /// @auditor - double check liquidity is set correctly for this in insertSingle
 148 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 149 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 150 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 151 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 152 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 153 |     |                 }
 154 |     |             } else {
 155 |     |                 uint160 priceUpper = ConstantProduct.getPriceAtTick(params.upper, cache.constants);
 156 |     |                 if (priceUpper >= cache.pool.price) {
 157 |     |                     if (cache.pool.liquidity > 0) {
 158 |     |                         cache.pool = LimitTicks.insertSingle(params, ticks, limitTickMap, cache, cache.pool, cache.constants);
 159 |     |                     }
 160 |     |                     cache.pool.price = priceUpper;
 161 |     |                     cache.pool.tickAtPrice = params.upper;
 162 |     |                     cache.pool.liquidity += uint128(cache.liquidityMinted);
 163 |     |                     cache.position.crossedInto = true;
 164 |     |                     // set epoch on start tick to signify position being crossed into
 165 |     |                     /// @auditor - this is safe assuming we have swapped at least this far on the other side
 166 |     |                     emit SyncLimitPool(cache.pool.price, cache.pool.liquidity, cache.state.epoch, cache.pool.tickAtPrice, params.zeroForOne);
 167 |     |                 }
 168 |     |             }
 169 |     |             (cache.pool, cache.position) = LimitPositions.add(
 170 |     |                 cache,
 171 |     |                 ticks,
 172 |     |                 limitTickMap,
 173 |     |                 params
 174 |     |             );
 175 |     | 
 176 |     |             positionCreated = true;
 177 |     | 
 178 |     |             // save position to storage
 179 |     |             positions[params.positionId] = cache.position;
 180 |     | 
 181 |     |             // update cache
 182 |     |             params.zeroForOne ? cache.state.pool0 = cache.pool 
 183 |     |                               : cache.state.pool1 = cache.pool;
 184 |     | 
 185 |     |             emit MintLimit(
 186 |     |                 params.to,
 187 |     |                 params.lower,
 188 |     |                 params.upper,
 189 |     |                 params.zeroForOne,
 190 |     |                 params.positionId,
 191 |     |                 cache.position.epochLast,
 192 |     |                 uint128(params.amount + cache.swapCache.input),
 193 |     |                 uint128(cache.swapCache.output),
 194 |     |                 uint128(cache.liquidityMinted)
 195 |     |             );
 196 |     |         }
 197 |     | 
 198 |     |         // save lp side for safe reentrancy
 199 |     |         save(cache, globalState, params.zeroForOne);
 200 |     |     
 201 |     |         revert SimulateMint(params.lower, params.upper, positionCreated);
 202 |     |     }

   1 |     | // SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
   2 |     | pragma solidity 0.8.13;
   3 |     | 
   4 |     | import '../interfaces/IPool.sol';
   5 |     | import '../interfaces/limit/ILimitPool.sol';
   6 |     | import '../interfaces/limit/ILimitPoolFactory.sol';

   8 |     | import '../base/events/LimitPoolManagerEvents.sol';
   9 |     | 
  10 |     | /**
  11 |     |  * @dev Defines the actions which can be executed by the factory admin.
  12 |     |  */
  13 |     | contract LimitPoolManager is ILimitPoolManager, LimitPoolManagerEvents {
  14 |     |     address public owner;
  15 |     |     address public feeTo;
  16 |     |     address public factory;
  17 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE = 1e4; /// @dev - max protocol swap fee of 100%
  18 |     |     uint16  public constant MAX_PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE = 1e2; /// @dev - max protocol fill fee of 1%
  19 |     |     // impl name => impl address
  20 |     |     mapping(bytes32 => address) internal _poolImpls;
  21 |     |     mapping(bytes32 => address) internal _tokenImpls;
  22 |     |     // swap fee => tick spacing
  23 |     |     mapping(uint16 => int16) internal _feeTiers;
  24 |     | 
  25 |     |     error InvalidSwapFee();
  26 |     |     error InvalidTickSpacing();
  27 |     |     error InvalidImplAddress();
  28 |     |     error TickSpacingAlreadyEnabled();
  29 |     |     error ImplementationAlreadyExists();
  30 |     | 
  31 |     |     constructor() {
  32 |     |         owner = msg.sender;
  33 |     |         feeTo = msg.sender;
  34 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(address(0), msg.sender);
  35 |     | 
  36 |     |         // create initial fee tiers
  37 |     |         _feeTiers[500] = 10;
  38 |     |         _feeTiers[10000] = 100;
  39 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(500, 10);
  40 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(10000, 100);
  41 |     |     }
  42 |     | 
  43 |     |     /**
  44 |     |      * @dev Throws if called by any account other than the owner.
  45 |     |      */
  46 |     |     modifier onlyOwner() {
  47 |     |         _checkOwner();
  48 |     |         _;
  49 |     |     }
  50 |     | 
  51 |     |     modifier onlyFeeTo() {
  52 |     |         _checkFeeTo();
  53 |     |         _;
  54 |     |     }
  55 |     | 
  56 |     |     /**
  57 |     |      * @dev Transfers ownership of the contract to a new account (`newOwner`).
  58 |     |      * Can only be called by the current owner.
  59 |     |      */
  60 |     |     function transferOwner(address newOwner) public virtual onlyOwner {
  61 |     |         if(newOwner == address(0)) require (false, 'TransferredToZeroAddress()');
  62 |     |         _transferOwner(newOwner);
  63 |     |     }
  64 |     | 
  65 |     |     function transferFeeTo(address newFeeTo) public virtual onlyFeeTo {
  66 |     |         if(newFeeTo == address(0)) require (false, 'TransferredToZeroAddress()');
  67 |     |         _transferFeeTo(newFeeTo);
  68 |     |     }
  69 |     | 
  70 |     |     /**
  71 |     |      * @dev Transfers ownership of the contract to a new account (`newOwner`).
  72 |     |      * Internal function without access restriction.
  73 |     |      */
  74 |     |     function _transferOwner(address newOwner) internal virtual {
  75 |     |         address oldOwner = owner;
  76 |     |         owner = newOwner;
  77 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(oldOwner, newOwner);
  78 |     |     }
  79 |     | 
  80 |     |     /**
  81 |     |      * @dev Transfers fee collection to a new account (`newFeeTo`).
  82 |     |      * Internal function without access restriction.
  83 |     |      */
  84 |     |     function _transferFeeTo(address newFeeTo) internal virtual {
  85 |     |         address oldFeeTo = feeTo;
  86 |     |         feeTo = newFeeTo;
  87 |     |         emit OwnerTransfer(oldFeeTo, newFeeTo);
  88 |     |     }
  89 |     | 
  90 |     |     function enableTickSpacing(
  91 |     |         int16 tickSpacing,
  92 |     |         uint16 swapFee
  93 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
  94 |     |         if (_feeTiers[swapFee] != 0) revert TickSpacingAlreadyEnabled();
  95 |     |         if (tickSpacing <= 0) revert InvalidTickSpacing();
  96 |     |         if (tickSpacing % 2 != 0) revert InvalidTickSpacing();
  97 |     |         if (swapFee == 0) revert InvalidSwapFee();
  98 |     |         if (swapFee > 10000) revert InvalidSwapFee();
  99 |     |         _feeTiers[swapFee] = tickSpacing;
 100 |     |         emit FeeTierEnabled(swapFee, tickSpacing);
 101 |     |     }
 102 |     | 
 103 |     |     function enableImplementation(
 104 |     |         bytes32 poolType_,
 105 |     |         address poolImpl_,
 106 |     |         address tokenImpl_
 107 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 108 |     |         if (_poolImpls[poolType_] != address(0)) revert ImplementationAlreadyExists();
 109 |     |         if (poolImpl_ == address(0) || tokenImpl_ == address(0)) revert InvalidImplAddress();
 110 |     |         /// @dev - prevent same addresses since factory does not support this
 111 |     |         if (poolImpl_ == tokenImpl_) revert InvalidImplAddress();
 112 |     |         _poolImpls[poolType_] = poolImpl_;
 113 |     |         _tokenImpls[poolType_] = tokenImpl_;
 114 |     |         emit ImplementationEnabled(poolType_, poolImpl_, tokenImpl_);
 115 |     |     }
 116 |     | 
 117 |     |     function setFactory(
 118 |     |         address factory_
 119 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 120 |     |         if (factory != address(0)) require (false, 'FactoryAlreadySet()');
 121 |     |         emit FactoryChanged(factory, factory_);
 122 |     |         factory = factory_;
 123 |     |     }
 124 |     | 
 125 |     |     function collectProtocolFees(
 126 |     |         address[] calldata pools
 127 |     |     ) external {
 128 |     |         if (pools.length == 0) require (false, 'EmptyPoolsArray()');
 129 |     |         uint128[] memory token0FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 130 |     |         uint128[] memory token1FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 131 |     |         // pass empty fees params
 132 |     |         FeesParams memory feesParams;
 133 |     |         for (uint i; i < pools.length;) {
 134 |     |             (
 135 |     |                 token0FeesCollected[i],
 136 |     |                 token1FeesCollected[i]
 137 |     |             ) = IPool(pools[i]).fees(feesParams);
 138 |     |             unchecked {
 139 |     |                 ++i;
 140 |     |             }
 141 |     |         }
 142 |     |         emit ProtocolFeesCollected(pools, token0FeesCollected, token1FeesCollected);
 143 |     |     }
 144 |     | 
 145 |     |     // protocol fee flags
 146 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0 = 2**0;
 147 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1 = 2**1;
 148 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0 = 2**2;
 149 |     |     uint8 internal constant PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1 = 2**3;
 150 |     | 
 151 |     |     function modifyProtocolFees(
 152 |     |         address[] calldata pools,
 153 |     |         FeesParams[] calldata feesParams
 154 |     |     ) external onlyOwner {
 155 |     |         if (pools.length == 0) require (false, 'EmptyPoolsArray()');
 156 |     |         if (pools.length != feesParams.length) {
 157 |     |             require (false, 'MismatchedArrayLengths()');
 158 |     |         }
 159 |     |         uint128[] memory token0FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 160 |     |         uint128[] memory token1FeesCollected = new uint128[](pools.length);
 161 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolSwapFees0 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 162 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolSwapFees1 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 163 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolFillFees0 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 164 |     |         uint16[] memory protocolFillFees1 = new uint16[](pools.length);
 165 |     |         for (uint i; i < pools.length;) {
 166 |     |             (
 167 |     |                 token0FeesCollected[i],
 168 |     |                 token1FeesCollected[i]
 169 |     |             ) = IPool(pools[i]).fees(
 170 |     |                 feesParams[i]
 171 |     |             );
 172 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_0) > 0) {
 173 |     |                 protocolSwapFees0[i] = feesParams[i].protocolSwapFee0;
 174 |     |             }
 175 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_SWAP_FEE_1) > 0) {
 176 |     |                 protocolSwapFees1[i] = feesParams[i].protocolSwapFee1;
 177 |     |             }
 178 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_0) > 0) {
 179 |     |                 protocolFillFees0[i] = feesParams[i].protocolFillFee0;
 180 |     |             }
 181 |     |             if ((feesParams[i].setFeesFlags & PROTOCOL_FILL_FEE_1) > 0) {
 182 |     |                 protocolFillFees1[i] = feesParams[i].protocolFillFee1;
 183 |     |             }
 184 |     |             // else values will remain zero
 185 |     |             unchecked {
 186 |     |                 ++i;
 187 |     |             }
 188 |     |         }
 189 |     |         emit ProtocolSwapFeesModified(
 190 |     |             pools,
 191 |     |             protocolSwapFees0,
 192 |     |             protocolSwapFees1
 193 |     |         );
 194 |     |         emit ProtocolFillFeesModified(
 195 |     |             pools,
 196 |     |             protocolFillFees0,
 197 |     |             protocolFillFees1
 198 |     |         );
 199 |     |         emit ProtocolFeesCollected(

 122 |     |         address _from,
 123 |     |         address _to,

 125 |     |         uint256[] calldata _amounts
 126 |     |     ) public virtual override

 165 |     |     function balanceOfBatch(
 166 |     |         address[] calldata _accounts,
 167 |     |         uint256[] calldata _ids
 168 |     |     ) public view virtual override
 169 |     |         checkLength(_accounts.length, _ids.length)
 170 |     |         returns (uint256[] memory batchBalances)
 171 |     |     {
 172 |     |         batchBalances = new uint256[](_accounts.length);
 173 |     |         unchecked {
 174 |     |             for (uint256 i; i < _accounts.length; ++i) {
 175 |     |                 batchBalances[i] = balanceOf(_accounts[i], _ids[i]);
 176 |     |             }

 180 |     |     function _mint(
 181 |     |         address _account,
 182 |     |         uint256 _id,
 183 |     |         uint256 _amount
 184 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 185 |     |         if (_account == address(0)) revert MintToAddress0();
 186 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(address(0), _account, _id, _amount);
 187 |     |         _totalSupplyById[_id] += _amount;
 188 |     |         uint256 _accountBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_account];
 189 |     |         unchecked {
 190 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_account] = _accountBalance + _amount;
 191 |     |         }
 192 |     |         emit TransferSingle(msg.sender, address(0), _account, _id, _amount);
 193 |     |     }
 194 |     | 
 195 |     |     function _burn(
 196 |     |         address _account,
 197 |     |         uint256 _id,
 198 |     |         uint256 _amount
 199 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 200 |     |         if (_account == address(0)) revert BurnFromAddress0();
 201 |     |         uint256 _accountBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_account];
 202 |     |         if (_accountBalance < _amount) revert BurnExceedsBalance(_account, _id, _amount);
 203 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(_account, address(0), _id, _amount);
 204 |     |         unchecked {
 205 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_account] = _accountBalance - _amount;
 206 |     |             _totalSupplyById[_id] -= _amount;
 207 |     |         }
 208 |     |         emit TransferSingle(msg.sender, _account, address(0), _id, _amount);
 209 |     |     }
 210 |     | 
 211 |     |     function _transfer(
 212 |     |         address _from,
 213 |     |         address _to,
 214 |     |         uint256 _id,
 215 |     |         uint256 _amount
 216 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 217 |     |         uint256 _fromBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_from];
 218 |     |         if (_fromBalance < _amount) revert TransferExceedsBalance(_from, _id, _amount);
 219 |     |         _beforeTokenTransfer(_from, _to, _id, _amount);
 220 |     |         unchecked {
 221 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_from] = _fromBalance - _amount;
 222 |     |         }
 223 |     |         uint256 _toBalance = _tokenBalances[_id][_to];
 224 |     |         unchecked {
 225 |     |             _tokenBalances[_id][_to] = _toBalance + _amount;
 226 |     |         }
 227 |     |     }
 228 |     | 
 229 |     |     function _setApprovalForAll(
 230 |     |         address _owner,
 231 |     |         address _spender,
 232 |     |         bool _approved
 233 |     |     ) internal virtual {
 234 |     |         if (_owner == _spender) revert SelfApproval(_owner);
 235 |     |         _spenderApprovals[_owner][_spender] = _approved;
 236 |     |         emit ApprovalForAll(_owner, _spender, _approved);
 237 |     |     }
 238 |     | 
 239 |     |     function _isApprovedForAll(address _owner, address _spender) internal view virtual returns (bool) {
 240 |     |         return _owner == _spender || _spenderApprovals[_owner][_spender];
 241 |     |     }

 245 |     |         address from,

 247 |     |         uint256 id,
 248 |     |         uint256 amount

 251 |     |     function _onlyCanonicalPoolTokens(
 252 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 253 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 254 |     |         // generate key for pool
 255 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(
 256 |     |             poolImpl(),
 257 |     |             constants.token0,
 258 |     |             constants.token1,
 259 |     |             constants.swapFee
 260 |     |         ));
 261 |     | 
 262 |     |         // compute address
 263 |     |         address predictedAddress = LibClone.predictDeterministicAddress(
 264 |     |             original,
 265 |     |             abi.encodePacked(
 266 |     |                 poolImpl()
 267 |     |             ),
 268 |     |             key,
 269 |     |             factory
 270 |     |         );
 271 |     | 
 272 |     |         if (predictedAddress != address(this)) return false;
 273 |     | 
 274 |     |         return true;
 275 |     |     }
 276 |     | 
 277 |     |     function _onlyCanonicalPools(
 278 |     |         PoolsharkStructs.LimitImmutables memory constants
 279 |     |     ) private view returns (bool) {
 280 |     |         // generate key for pool
 281 |     |         bytes32 key = keccak256(abi.encode(

 285 |     |             constants.swapFee

 293 |     |                 constants.token0,
 294 |     |                 constants.token1,
 295 |     |                 constants.poolToken,
 296 |     |                 constants.bounds.min,

 300 |     |                 constants.swapFee
 301 |     |             ),
 302 |     |             key,
 303 |     |             factory
 304 |     |         );
 305 |     | 
 306 |     |         if (predictedAddress != msg.sender) return false;
 307 |     | 
 308 |     |         return true;
 309 |     |     }

 311 |     |     /// @notice Return if the `_target` contract supports ERC-1155 interface
 312 |     |     /// @param _target The address of the contract
 313 |     |     /// @return supported Whether the contract is supported (true) or not (false)
 314 |     |     function _verifyERC1155Support(address _target) private view returns (bool supported) {
 315 |     |         if (_target.code.length == 0) return true;
 316 |     |         bytes memory encodedParams = abi.encodeWithSelector(
 317 |     |             IERC165.supportsInterface.selector,
 318 |     |             type(IPositionERC1155).interfaceId
 319 |     |         );
 320 |     |         (bool success, bytes memory result) = _target.staticcall{gas: 30_000}(encodedParams);
 321 |     |         if (result.length < 32) return false;
 322 |     |         return success && abi.decode(result, (bool));
 323 |     |     }
